---
title: 023

---
      sūta uvāca।।  
tato manvantare'tīte cākṣuṣe daivataiḥ saha।  
vaivasvatāya mahate pṛthivīrājyamādiśat ।। 23.1 ।।  
  
tasya vaivasvato vakṣye sāmpratasya mahātmanaḥ।  
ānupūrvyeṇa vai viprāḥ kīrttyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। 23.2 ।।  
  
manorvaivasvatasyeha sargamādāya sāmpratam ।  
manoḥ prathamajasyāsan navaputrāstu tatsamāḥ ।। 23.3 ।।  
  
ikṣvākurnahuṣaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca।  
nariṣyantastathā prāṃśu rnābhāgo'riṣṭa eva ca।  
karūṣaśca pṛṣadhraśca navaite mānavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 23.4 ।।  
  
brahmaṇā tu manuḥ pūrvaṃ coditastu nibodhata।  
sraṣṭuṃ pracakrame kāmaṃ niṣphalaṃ samavarttata ।। 23.5 ।।  
  
athākarotputrakāmaḥ parāmiṣṭiṃ prajāpatiḥ।  
mitrāvaruṇayoraṃśe manurāhutimāvapat ।। 23.6 ।।  
  
tatra divyāmbaradharā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā।  
divyasannahanā caiva iḍā jajñe iti śrutiḥ ।। 23.7 ।।  
  
tāmiletyatha hovāca manurddaṇḍadharaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
anugacchāmi bhadrante tamilā pratyuvāca ha ।। 23.8 ।।  
  
dharmmayuktamidaṃ vācyaṃ putrakāmaṃ prajāpatim।  
mitrāvaruṇayoraṃśe jātāsmi vadatāṃ vara ।। 23.9 ।।  
  
tayoḥ sakaśaṃ yāsyāmi mā no dharmo hato'vadhīt।  
saivamuktvā punarddevī tayorantikamāgamat ।। 23.10 ।।  
  
gatvāntikaṃ varārohā prāñjalirvākyamabravīt ।  
aṃśe'sminyuvayorjātā devau kiṃ karavāṇi ca ।। 23.11 ।।  
  
manunaivāhamuktāsmi anugacchasva māmiti।  
tathā tu vadatīṃ sādhvīmiḍāmāśritya tāvubhau ।। 23.12 ।।  
  
devau ca mitrāvaruṇāvidaṃ vacanamūcatuḥ ।  
anena tava dharmajñe praśrayeṇa damena ca ।। 23.13 ।।  
  
satyena caiva suśroṇi prītau svo varavarṇini।  
āvayostvaṃ mahābhāge khyātiṃ kanyā prayāsyasi ।। 23.14 ।।  
  
sudyumna iti vikhyātastriṣu lokeṣu pūjitaḥ।  
jagatpriyo dharmmaśīlo manorvaṃśa vivarddhanaḥ ।। 23.15 ।।  
  
mānavaḥ sa tu sudyumnaḥ strībhāvamagamat prabhuḥ।  
sā tu devī varaṃ labdhvā nivṛttā pitaraṃ prati ।। 23.16 ।।  
  
budhenāntaramāsādya maithunāyopamantritā।  
somaputrādbudhāccāsyā ailo jajñe purūravāḥ ।। 23.17 ।।  
  
budhāt sā janayitvā tu sudyumnaṃ punarāgatā।  
sudyumnasya ca dāyādāstrayaḥ paramadhārmmikāḥ ।। 23.18 ।।  
  
utkalaśca gayaścaiva vinatāśvastathaiva ca।  
utkalasyotkalaṃ rāṣṭraṃ vinatāśvasya paścimam ।  
dikṣu vātasya rājarṣergayasya tu gayā purī ।। 23.19 ।।  
  
pravisṛṣṭe manau tasmin prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā divākaraḥ।  
daśadhā taddadhat kṣetramakarot pṛthivīmimām ।। 23.20 ।।  
  
ikṣvākureva dāyādānanyān daśa samāpnuyāt।  
kanyābhāvāttu sudyumno nainaṃ bhāgamavāpnuyāt ।। 23.21 ।।  
  
vasiṣṭhavacanāccāsīt pratiṣṭāno mahādyutiḥ।  
pratiṣṭā dharmarājasya sudyumnasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 23.22 ।।  
  
tat purūravase prādādrāṣṭraṃ prāpya mahāyaśāḥ।  
mānavebhyo mahābhāgā strīpuṃsorlakṣaṇaṃ prati।  
mānavaḥ sa tu sudyumnaḥ strībhāvamagamat punaḥ ।। 23.23 ।।  
  
etacchrutvā tu ṛṣayaḥ papracchustadanantaram ।  
mānavaḥ sa tu sudyumnaḥ strībhāvamagamat katham ।। 23.24 ।।  
  
      sūta uvāca।।  
provāca vacanaṃ devī priyahetoḥ priyaṃ priyā ।  
sa me mamāśrame deva yaḥ pumān saṃpravekṣyati।  
bhaviṣyati dhruvaṃ nārī sā tulyāpsarasāṃ śubhā ।। 23.25 ।।  
  
tatra sarvāṇi bhūtāni piśācāḥ paśavaśca ye।  
strībhūtāḥ saha rudreṇa krīḍantyapsaraso tathā ।। 23.26 ।।  
  
umāvanaṃ praviṣṭastu sa rājā mṛgayāṃ gataḥ।  
saha piśācairbhūtaistu rudraiḥ strībhāvamāsthitaḥ ।। 23.27 ।।  
  
tasmāt sa rājā sudyumnaḥ strībhāvaṃ labdhavān punaḥ ।  
mahādevaprasādācca gāṇapatya mavāpnuyāt ।। 23.28 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte vaivasvatamanoḥ sṛṣṭikathanaṃ nāma trayoviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 23 ।। 


---
title: 024

---
          sūta uvāca।।  
nisargaṃ manu putrāṇāṃ vistareṇa nibodhata।  
pṛṣadhro hisayitvā tu gurorgāvamabhakṣayat ।। 24.1 ।।  
  
śāpācchūdratvamāpannaścyavanasya mahātmanaḥ।  
karūṣasya tu kārūṣaḥ kṣatriyo yuddhadurmadaḥ ।। 24.2 ।।  
  
sahasrakṣatriyagaṇavikrāntaḥ saṃbabhūva ha।  
nābhāgāriṣṭaputrastu vidvānāsīdbhalandanaḥ ।। 24.3 ।।  
  
bhalandanasya putro'bhūt prāṃśurnāma mahābalaḥ।  
prāṃśoreko'bhavat putraḥ prajāniriti viśrutaḥ ।। 24.4 ।।  
  
prajānerabhavat putraḥ khanitro nāma vīryavān।  
tasya putro'bhavacchrīmān kṣupo nāma mahāyaśāḥ ।। 24.5 ।।  
  
kṣupasya viṃśaḥ putrastu pratimā na babhūva ha।  
viṃśaputrastu kalyāṇo viviṃśo nāma dhārmikaḥ ।। 24.6 ।।  
  
viviṃśaputro dharmātmā khaninetraḥ pratāpavān।  
karandhamastasya putrastretāyugamukhe'bhavat ।। 24.7 ।।  
  
karandhamasutaścāpi āvikṣinnāma vīryavān।  
āvikṣito vyatikrāmat pitaraṃ guṇavattayā ।। 24.8 ।।  
  
marutto nāma dharmātmā cakravarttisamo nṛpaḥ।  
saṃvarttena divaṃ nītaḥ sasuhṛt saha bāndhavaiḥ ।। 24.9 ।।  
  
vivādo'tra mahānāsīt saṃvarttasya bṛhaspateḥ।  
ṛddhiṃ dṛṣṭvā tu yajñasya kruddhastasya bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 24.10 ।।  
  
saṃparttena hṛte yajñe cukopa subhṛśantadā।  
lokānāṃ sa hi nāśaya daivatairhi prasāditaḥ ।। 24.11 ।।  
  
maruttaścakravarttī sa nariṣyantamavāptavān।  
nariṣyantasya dāyādo rājā daṇḍadharo damaḥ ।। 24.12 ।।  
  
tasya putrastu vikrānto rājāsīdrāṣṭravarddhanaḥ ।  
sudhṛtī tasya putrastu naraḥ sudhṛtinaḥ sutaḥ ।। 24.13 ।।  
  
kevalastasya putrastu bandhumān kevalātmajaḥ।  
atha bandhumataḥ putro dharmātmā vegavān nṛpaḥ ।। 24.14 ।।  
  
budho vegavataḥ putra stṛṇabindurbudhātmajaḥ।  
tretāyugamukhe rājā tṛtīye saṃbabhūva ha ।। 24.15 ।।  
  
kanyā tu tasya draviḍā mātā viśravaso hi sā।  
putraścāsya viśālo'bhūd rājā paramadhārmikaḥ ।। 24.16 ।।  
  
viśālasya samutpannā viśālā nayanirmitā।  
viśālasya suto rājā hemacandro mahābalaḥ ।। 24.17 ।।  
  
sucandra iti vikhyāto hemacandrādanantaram।  
sucandratanayo rājā dhūmrāśca iti viśrutaḥ ।। 24.18 ।।  
  
dhūmrāśvatanayo vidvān sṛñjayaḥ samapadyata।  
sṛñjayasya sutaḥ śrīmān sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ।। 24.19 ।।  
  
kṛśāśvaḥ sahadevasya putraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ।  
kṛśāśvasya mahātejāḥ somadattaḥ pratāpavān ।। 24.20 ।।  
  
somadattasya rājarṣeḥ sutobhūjjanamejayaḥ।  
janamejayātmajaścaiva pramatirnāma viśrutaḥ ।। 24.21 ।।  
  
tṛṇabinduprasādena sarve vaiśālakā nṛpāḥ ।  
dīrghāyuṣo mahātmāno vīryavantaḥ sudhārmikāḥ ।। 24.22 ।।  
  
śaryātermithunaṃ tvāsīdānārto nāma viśrutaḥ।  
putraḥ sukanyā kanyā na bhāryāyā cyavanasya tu ।। 24.23 ।।  
  
ānārttasya tu dāyādo revo nāmnā tu vīryavān।  
ānartto viṣayo yasya purī cāpi kuśasthalī ।। 24.24 ।।  
  
revasya raivataḥ putraḥ kakujhī nāma dhārmikaḥ।  
jyeṣṭo bhrātṛśatasyāsīdrājā prāpya kuśasthalīm ।। 24.25 ।।  
  
kanyayā saha śrutvā ca gandharvaṃ brahmaṇo'ntike।  
muhūrttaṃ devadevasya mārtyaṃ bahuyugaṃ vibhoḥ ।। 24.26 ।।  
  
ājagāma yuvā caiva svāṃ purīṃ yādavairvṛtām।  
kṛtāṃ dvāravatīṃ nāma bahudvārāṃ manoramām ।। 24.27 ।।  
  
bhojavṛṣṭyandhakairguptāṃ vasudevapurogamaiḥ।  
tāṅkathāṃ raivataḥ śrutvā yathātattvamarindamaḥ ।। 24.28 ।।  
  
kanyā tu baladevāya suvratāṃ nāma revatīm।  
dattvā jagāma śikharaṃ merostapasi saṃsthitaḥ ।। 24.29 ।।  
  
reme rāmaśca dharmātmā revatyā sahitaḥ kila।  
tāṃ kathāmṛṣayaḥ śrutvā papracchustadanantaram ।। 24.30 ।।  
  
        ṛṣya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
kathaṃ bahuyuge kāle vyatīte sūtanandana।  
na jarāṃ revatī prāptā palitañca kutaḥ prabho ।। 24.31 ।।  
  
meruṃ gatasya vā tasya śaryyāteḥ santatiḥ katham।  
sthitā pṛthivyāmadyāpi śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ ।। 24.32 ।।  
  
kiyanto vā suragaṇā gandharvvāstatra kīdṛśāḥ।  
yacchrutvā raivataḥ kālān muhūrttamiva manyate ।। 24.33 ।।  
  
             sūta uvāca।।  
na jarā kṣutpipāsā vā na ca mṛtyubhayaṃ tataḥ।  
na ca rogaḥ prabhavati brahmalokagatasya hi ।। 24.34 ।।  
  
gāndharvvaṃ prati yaccāpi pṛṣṭastu munisattamāḥ।  
tato'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yāthātathyena suvratāḥ ।। 24.35 ।।  
  
sapta svarāstrayo grāmā mūrcchanāstvekaviṃśatiḥ।  
tālāścaikonapañcāśadityetat svaramaṇḍalam ।। 24.36 ।।  
  
ṣaḍjarṣabhau ca gāndhāro madhyamaḥ pañcamastathā।  
dhaivataścāpi vijñeyastathā cāpi niṣādavān ।। 24.37 ।।  
  
sauvīrī madhyamagrāmo hariṇāsyā tathaiva ca।  
syātkalopabalopetā caturthī śuddhamadhyamā ।। 24.38 ।।  
  
śārṅgī ca pāvanī caiva dṛṣṭākā ca yathākramam।  
mdhyamagrāmikīḥ khyātāḥ ṣaḍjagrāmaṃ nibodhata ।। 24.39 ।।  
  
uttaramandrā rajanī tathā yā cottarāyatā।  
śuddhaṣaḍjā tathā caiva jānīyāt saptamāṃ ca tām ।। 24.40 ।।  
  
gāndhāragrāmi kāṃścānyān kīrtyamānān nibodhata।  
āgniṣṭomikamādyantu dvitīyaṃ vājapeyikam ।। 24.41 ।।  
  
tṛtīyaṃ pauṇḍrakaṃ proktaṃ caturthaṃ cāśvamedhikam।  
pañcamaṃ rājasūyaṃ va ṣaṣṭhaṃ cakrasuvarṇakam ।। 24.42 ।।  
  
saptamaṃ gosavaṃ nāma mahāvṛṣṭikamaṣṭamam।  
brahmadānañca navamaṃ prājāpatyamanantaram ।। 24.43 ।।  
  
nāgapakṣāśrayaṃ vidyādgotarañca tathaiva ca।  
hayakrāntaṃ mṛgakrāntaṃ viṣṇukrāntaṃ manoharam ।। 24.44 ।।  
  
sūryyakrāntaṃ vareṇyañca mattakokilavādinam।  
sāvitramarddhasāvitraṃ sarvvato madrameva ca ।। 24.45 ।।  
  
suvarṇañca sutandrañca viṣṇuvaiṣṇuvarāvubhau।  
sāgaraṃ vijayañcaiva sarvabhūtamanoharam ।। 24.46 ।।  
  
haṃsaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ vijānīmastumburupriyameva ca।  
manoharamadhātryañca gandharvānugataśca yaḥ ।। 24.47 ।।  
  
alambuṣeṣṭaśca tathā nāradapriya eva ca।  
kathito bhīmasenena nāgarāṇāṃ yathā priyaḥ ।। 24.48 ।।  
  
karopanīta vinatā śrīrākhyo bhārgavapriyaḥ।  
viṃśatirmadhyamagrāmaḥ ṣaḍjagrāmaścaturddaśa ।। 24.49 ।।  
  
tathā pañcadaśecchanti gāndhāragrāmasaṃsthitān ।  
sasauvīrā tu gāndhārī brahmaṇā hyupagīyate ।। 24.50 ।।  
  
uttarādisvarasyaiva brahmā vai devatā'tra ca।  
harideśasamutpannā hariṇāsyā vyajāyata।  
mūrcchanā hariṇāsyaiva asyā indro'dhidaivatam ।। 24.51 ।।  
  
karopanītavitatā marudbhiḥ svaramaṇḍale।  
sā kalopanatā tasmānmārutaścātra daivatam ।। 24.52 ।।  
  
manudeśasamutpannā mūrcchanā śuddhamadhyam।  
madhyamo'tra svaraḥ śuddho gandharvvaścātra devatā ।। 24.53 ।।  
  
mṛgaiḥ saha sañcarate siddhānāṃ mārgadarśane।  
yasmāttasmāt smṛtā mārgī mṛgendro'syāśca devatā ।। 24.54 ।।  
  
sā cāśramasamāyuktā anekān pauravān ravān।  
mūrcchanā yojanā hyeṣā rajasā rajanī tataḥ ।। 24.55 ।।  
  
tāla uttaramandrāṃśaḥ ṣaḍjadaivatakāṃ viduḥ।  
tasmāduttaratālañca prathamaṃ svāyataṃ viduḥ।  
tasmāduttaramandro'yaṃ devatāsya dhruvo dhruvam ।। 24.56 ।।  
  
apānāduttaratvācca dhaivatasyottarāyaṇaḥ।  
syādiyaṃ mūrcchanā hyevaṃ pitaraḥ śrāddhadevatāḥ ।। 24.57 ।।  
  
śuddhaṣaḍjasvaraṃ kṛtvā yasmādagniṃ maharṣayaḥ।  
upatiṣṭhanti tasmāttaṃ jānīyācchuddhaṣaḍ‌jikam ।। 24.58 ।।  
  
yaḥ satāṃ mūrcchanāṃ kṛtvā pañcamasvarako bhavet ।  
yakṣīṇāṃ mūrcchanā sā tu yākṣikā mūrcchanā smṛtā ।। 24.59 ।।  
  
nāgadṛṣṭirviṣā gītā nopasarpanti mūrcchanām।  
bhavantīva hṛtā hyete brahmaṇā nāgadevatāḥ।  
ahīnāṃ mūrcchanā hyeṣā varuṇaścātra devatā ।। 24.60 ।।  
  
śakuntakānāṃ kṛtvā ca upamāṃ yānti kinnarāḥ ।  
uttamāṃ mūrcchanā tasmāt pakṣirājo'tra devatā ।। 24.61 ।।  
  
gāndhārarāgaśabdena gāṃ ca dhārayate'rthataḥ।  
tasmādviśuddhagāndhārī gandharvaścādhidaivatam ।। 24.62 ।।  
  
gāndhārānantaraṃ gatvā sṛṣṭeyaṃ mūrcchanā yataḥ।  
tasmāduttaragāndhārī vasavaścātra devatāḥ ।। 24.63 ।।  
  
seyaṃ khalu mahābhūtā pitāmaha mupasthitā।  
ṣaḍjeyaṃ mūrcchanā tasmāt smṛtā hyanaladevatā ।। 24.64 ।।  
  
divyeyaṃ cāyatā tena mandaṣaṣṭā ca mūrcchane।  
nivṛttaguṇanāmānaṃ pañcamañcātra dhaivatam ।। 24.65 ।।  
  
pūrṇāḥ saptasvarā hyevaṃ mūrcchanāḥ saṃprakīrttitāḥ।  
nānāsādhāraṇāścaiva ṣaḍevānuvidastathā ।। 24.66 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte vaivasvata manuvaṃśagāndharvvamūrcchanālakṣaṇakathanaṃ nāma caturviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 24 ।। 


---
title: 025

---
pūrvvācāryyamataṃ buddhvā pravakṣyāmyanupūrvvaśaḥ।  
triṃśataṃ vai alaṅkārāṃstān me nigadataḥ śrṛṇu ।। 25.1 ।।  
  
alaṅkārāstu vaktavyāḥ svaiḥsvairvarṇaiḥ prahetavaḥ।  
saṃsthānayogaiśca tathā pādānāṃ cānvavekṣayā ।। 25.2 ।।  
  
vākyārthapadayogārthairalaṅkārasya pūraṇam।  
padāni gītakasyāhuḥ purastāt pṛṣṭhato'thavā ।। 25.3 ।।  
  
sthānāni trīṇi jānīyāduraḥkaṇṭhaśirastathā।  
eteṣu triṣu sthāneṣu pravṛtto vidhiruttamaḥ ।। 25.4 ।।  
  
catvāraḥ prakṛtau varṇāḥ pravicāraścaturvidhaḥ।  
vikalpamaṣṭadhā caiva devāḥ ṣoḍaśadhā viduḥ ।। 25.5 ।।  
  
sthāyī varṇaḥ prasaṃcārī tṛtīyamavarohaṇam।  
ārohaṇaṃ caturthantu varṇaṃ varṇavido viduḥ ।। 25.6 ।।  
  
tatraikaḥ saṃcarasthāyī sacarāstacarībhavan।  
atha rohaṇavarṇānāmavarohaṃ vinirdiśet ।। 25.7 ।।  
  
ārohaṇena cārohavarṇaṃ varṇavido viduḥ।  
eteṣāmeva varṇānāmalaṅkārānnibodhata ।। 25.8 ।।  
  
alaṅkārāstu catvāraḥ sthāpanī kramarejinaḥ।  
pramādaścāpramādaśca teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।। 25.9 ।।  
  
visvaroṣṭrakalāścaiva sthānādekāntaraṃ gatāḥ।  
āvarttasyākramotpattī dve kāryye parimāṇataḥ ।। 25.10 ।।  
  
kumāramaparaṃ vidyādvistaraṃ vamanaṃ gatam।  
eṣa vai cāpyapāṅgastu kutārekaḥ kalādhikaḥ ।। 25.11 ।।  
  
śyenastvekāntare jātaḥ kalāmātrāntare sthitaḥ।  
tasmiṃścaiva svare vṛddhistiṣṭhate tadvilakṣaṇā ।। 25.12 ।।  
  
śyenastu aparohastu uttaraḥ parikīrttitaḥ।  
kalākalapramāṇācca sa bindurnāma cāyate ।। 25.13 ।।  
  
bindurekakalā kāryā varṇāntasthāyinī bhavet।  
viparyayasvaro'pi syādyasya durghaṭito'pi na ।। 25.14 ।।  
  
ekāntarā tu vādyantu ṣaḍjataḥ paramaḥ svaraḥ।  
ākṣepāskandanaṃ kāryyaṃ kākasyevoccapuṣkalam ।। 25.15 ।।  
  
santārau tau tu sañcāryau kāryaṃ vā kāraṇaṃ tathā।  
ākṣiptamavarohyāpi prokṣamadyantathaiva ca ।। 25.16 ।।  
  
dvādaśañca kalāsthānamekāntaragatantataḥ।  
preṅkholitamalaṅkāramevaṃ svarasamanvitam ।। 25.17 ।।  
  
svarasaṃkrāmakāccaiva tataḥ proktantu puṣkalam।  
prakṣiptameva kalayā pādānītarayorbhavet ।। 25.18 ।।  
  
dvikalaṃ vā yathā bhūtaṃ yattad hrāsitamucyate।  
uccārādvisvarārūḍhā tathā cāṣṭasvarāntaram ।। 25.19 ।।  
  
yastu syādavaroho vā tārato mandrato'pi vā।  
ekāntarahitā hyete tameva svaramantataḥ ।। 25.20 ।।  
  
makṣipracchedano nāma catuṣkalagaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
alaṅkārā bhavantyete triṃśadye vai prakīrttitāḥ।  
varṇasthānaprayogeṇa kalāmātrā pramāṇataḥ ।। 25.21 ।।  
  
saṃsthānañca pramāṇaṃ ca vikāro lakṣaṇantathā।  
caturvidhamidaṃ jñeyamalaṅkāraprayojanam ।। 25.22 ।।  
  
yathātmano hyalaṅkāro viparyasto'tigarhitaḥ।  
varṇamevāpyalaṃkarttuṃ viṣamaṃ hyātmasambhavāt ।। 25.23 ।।  
  
nānābharaṇasaṃyogādyathā nāryā vibhūṣaṇam।  
varṇasya caivālaṅkāro viparyasto'tigarhitaḥ ।। 25.24 ।।  
  
na pāde kuṇḍale dṛṣṭe na kaṇṭe rasanā yathā।  
evameva hyalaṅkāro viparyasto vigarhitaḥ ।। 25.25 ।।  
  
kriyamāṇo'pyalaṅkāro rāgaṃ yaścaiva darśayet।  
yathoddiṣṭasya mārgasya karttavyasya vidhīyate ।। 25.26 ।।  
  
lakṣaṇaṃ paryyavasthāpi varṇikābhiḥ pravarttanam।  
yāthātathyena vakṣyāmi māsedbhavamukhodbhave ।। 25.27 ।।  
  
trayoviṃśatyaśītistu teṣāmetadviparyayaḥ।  
ṣaḍjapakṣo'pi tattvādau madhyo hīnasvaro bhavet ।। 25.28 ।।  
  
ṣaḍjamadhyamayoścaiva grāmayoḥ paryyapastathā।  
mānoyottaramandrasya ṣaḍevātrāvikasya ca ।। 25.29 ।।  
  
svarālaṃpratyayaścaiva sarvveṣāṃ pratyayaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
anugamya bahirgītaṃ vijñātaṃ pañcadaivatam ।। 25.30 ।।  
  
gorūpāṇāṃ purastāttu madhyamāṃśastu paryyayaḥ।  
tayorvibhāgo gītānāṃ lāvaṇyamārgasaṃsthitaḥ ।। 25.31 ।।  
  
anuṣaṅgaṃ mayoddiṣṭaṃ svasārañca svarāntaram।  
paryyayaḥ saṃpravartteta saptasvarapadakramam ।। 25.32 ।।  
  
gāndhārāṃśena gīyante catvāri mandrakāṇi ca।  
pañcamo madhyamaścaiva dhaivate tu niṣādajaiḥ।  
ṣaḍjarṣabhaiśca jānīmo mandrakeṣveva nāntare ।। 25.33 ।।  
  
dve cāparāntike vidyāddhayaśullāṣṭakasya tu।  
prākṛte vaiṇavaiścaiva gāndhārāṃśe prayujyate ।। 25.34 ।।  
  
padasya tu trayaṃ rūpaṃ saptarūpantu kauśikam।  
gāndhārāṃśena kārtsnyena paryayasya vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
evañcaiva kramoddiṣṭo madhyamāṃśasya madhyamaḥ ।। 25.35 ।।  
  
yāni gītāni proktāni rūpeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ।  
tattu saptasvaraṃ kāryyaṃ saptarūpañca kauśikam ।। 25.36 ।।  
  
aṅgadarśanamityāhurmāne dve samake tathā।  
dvitīyabhāvācaraṇā mātrā nābhipratiṣṭitā ।। 25.37 ।।  
  
uttare ca prakṛtyevaṃ mātrā tallīyate tathā ।  
hantāraḥ piṇḍako yatra mātrāyāṃ nātivarttate ।। 25.38 ।।  
  
pādenaikena mātrāyāṃ pādonāmati vīraṇā।  
saṃkhyāyāścopahananaṃ tatra yānamiti smṛtam ।। 25.39 ।।  
  
dvitīyaṃ pādabhaṅgañca graheṇābhipratiṣṭitam।  
pūrvvamaṣṭatṛtīye tu dvitīyaṃ cāparītake ।। 25.40 ।।  
  
arddhena pādasāmyasya pādabhāgācca pañcake।  
pādabhāgaṃ sapādaṃ tu prakṛtyāmapi saṃsthitam ।। 25.41 ।।  
  
caturthamuttare caiva madravatyāṃ ca madrake।  
madrake dakṣiṇasyāpi yathoktā varttate kalā ।। 25.42 ।।  
  
pūrvvamevānuyogantu dvitīyā buddhiriṣyate।  
pādau cāharaṇaṃ cāsmat pāraṃ nātra vidhīyate ।। 25.43 ।।  
  
ekatvamupayogasya dvayoryaddhi dvijottama।  
anekasamavāyastu patākāhariṇaṃ smṛtam ।। 25.44 ।।  
  
tisṝṇāṃ caiva vṛttīnāṃ vṛttau vṛttā ca dakṣiṇā।  
aṣṭau tu samavāyāste sauvīrā mūrcchanā tathā।  
kuśatyanuttaraḥ satyaṃ sapta sattvasvaraṃ tu yaḥ ।। 25.45 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte gītālaṅkāranirddeśo nāma paṃcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 25 ।। *  
 


---
title: 026

---
         sūta uvāca।।  
kakujhinastu taṃ lokaṃ raivatasya gatasya ha।  
hatāḥ puṇyajanaiḥ sarvvā rākṣasaiḥ sā kuśasthalī ।। 26.1 ।।  
  
tadvai bhrātṛśataṃ tasya dhārmmikasya mahātmanaḥ।  
nibadhyamānā rakṣobhirdiśaḥ saṃprādravan bhayāt ।। 26.2 ।।  
  
teṣāntu te bhayā krāntāḥ kṣatriyāstatra tatra hi।  
anvavāyastu sumahān mahāṃstatra dvijottamāḥ ।। 26.3 ।।  
  
prayatā iti vikhyātā dikṣu sarvvāsu dhārmmikāḥ।  
dhṛṣṭasya dhārṣṭakaṃ kṣatraṃ raṇadhṛṣṭaṃ babhūva ha ।। 26.4 ।।  
  
trisāhasrantu sagaṇaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahātmanām।  
nabhagasya ca dāyādo nābhāgo nāma vīryyavān ।। 26.5 ।।  
  
ambarīṣastu nābhāgirvirūpastasya cātmajaḥ।  
pṛṣadaśvo virūpasya tasya putro rathītaraḥ ।। 26.6 ।।  
  
ete kṣatraprasūtā vai punaścāṅgirasaḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
rathītarāṇāṃ pravarāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ ।। 26.7 ।।  
  
kṣuvatastu manoḥ pūrvvamikṣyākurabhiniḥsṛtaḥ ।  
tasya putraśataṃ tvāsīdikṣvākorbhūridakṣiṇam ।। 26.8 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ jyeṣṭo vikukṣiśca nemirdaṇḍaśca te trayaḥ।  
śakunipramukhāstasya putrāḥ paṃcāśatastu te ।। 26.9 ।।  
  
uttarāpathadeśasya rakṣitāro mahīkṣitaḥ।  
catvāriṃśattathāṣṭau ca dakṣiṇasyāñca te diśi ।। 26.10 ।।  
  
viṃśatipramukhāste tu dakṣiṇāpatharakṣiṇaḥ।  
ikṣvākustu vikukṣiṃ vai aṣṭakāyāmathādiśet ।। 26.11 ।।  
  
          rājovāca।।  
māṃsamānaya śrāddheyaṃ mṛgān hatvā mahābala।  
śrāddhamadya nu kartavyamaṣṭakāyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। 26.12 ।।  
  
sa gatastu mṛgavyāṃ vai vacanāttasya dhīmataḥ।  
mṛgān sahasraśo hatvā pariśrāntaśca vīryyavān।  
bhakṣayacchaśakantatra vikukṣirmṛgayāṅgataḥ ।। 26.13 ।।  
  
āgate sa vikukṣau tu samāṃse sahasainike।  
vasiṣṭhañcodayāmāsa māṃsaṃ prokṣayatāmiti ।। 26.14 ।।  
  
tatheti codito rājñā vidhivatsamupasthitaḥ।  
sa dṛṣṭvopahataṃ māṃsaṃ kruddho rājānamabravīt ।। 26.15 ।।  
  
śūdreṇopahataṃ māṃsaṃ putreṇa tava pārthiva।  
śaśabhakṣādabhojyaṃ vai tava māṃsaṃ mahādyute ।। 26.16 ।।  
  
śaśo durātmanā pūrvamaraṇye bhakṣito'nagha।  
tena māṃsamidaṃ duṣṭaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nṛpasattama ।। 26.17 ।।  
  
ikṣvākustu tataḥ kruddho vikukṣimidamabravīt।  
pitṛkarmmaṇi nirddiṣṭo mayā tvaṃ mṛgayāṅkataḥ।  
śaśaṃ bhakṣayase'raṇye nirghṛṇaḥ pūrvvamadya nu ।। 26.18 ।।  
  
tasmātparityajāmi tvāṃ gaccha tvaṃ svena karmmaṇā।  
evamikṣvākunā tyakto vasiṣṭhavacanāt sutaḥ ।। 26.19 ।।  
  
ikṣvākau saṃsthite tasmiñchaśī sa pṛthivīmimām ।  
prāptaḥ paramadharmmātmā sa cāyodhyādhipo'bhavat ।। 26.20 ।।  
  
tadākarotsa rājyaṃ vai vasiṣṭhaparinoditaḥ।  
tataḥ stenena sā pūrṇo rājyāvasthā mahīpateḥ ।। 26.21 ।।  
  
kālena gatavāṃstatra sa ca nyūnatarāṅgatim।  
jñātvaivametadākhyānaṃ nā vidhirbhakṣayettu vai ।। 26.22 ।।  
  
māṃ sabhakṣayitāmutra yasya māṃsamihājyaham।  
etanmāṃsasya māṃsatvaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ ।। 26.23 ।।  
  
śaśādasya tu dāyādaḥ kakutstho nāma vīryyavān।  
indrasya vṛṣabhūtasya kakutstho jāyate purā ।। 26.24 ।।  
  
pūrvvamāḍībake yuddhe kakutsthastena sa smṛtaḥ ।  
anenāstu kakutsthasya pṛthuromā ca sa smṛtaḥ ।। 26.25 ।।  
  
vṛṣadaśvaḥ pṛthoḥ putrastasmādandhrastu vīryyavān ।  
āndhrastu yavanāśvastu śrāvastastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 26.26 ।।  
  
jajñe śrāvastako rājā śrāvastī yena nirmitā।  
śrāvastasya tu dāyādo bṛhadaśvo mahāyaśāḥ ।। 26.27 ।।  
  
bṛhadaśvasutaścāpi kubalāśca iti śrutiḥ।  
yaḥ sa dhundhuvadhādrājā dhundhumāratvamāgataḥ ।। 26.28 ।।  
  
         ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
dhundhuvadhaṃ mahāprājña śrotumicchami vistarāt।  
yadarthaṃ kubalāśvaḥ sa dhundhumāratvamāgataḥ ।। 26.29 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
bṛhadaśvasya putrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ।  
sarve vidyāsu niṣṇātā balavanto durāsadāḥ ।। 26.30 ।।  
  
babhūvurddhārmikāḥ sarve yajvāno bhūridakṣiṇāḥ।  
kubalāśvaṃ mahāvīryaṃ śūramuttamadhārmikam ।। 26.31 ।।  
  
bṛhadaśvo'bhyaṣiñcattaṃ tasmin rāṣṭre narādhipaḥ।  
putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīstu vanaṃ rājā viveśa ha ।। 26.32 ।।  
  
bṛhadaśvaṃ mahārājaṃ śūramuttamadhārmmikam ।  
prayātaṃ tamuttaṅkastu brahmarṣiḥ pratyavārayat ।। 26.33 ।।  
  
        uttaṅka uvāca।।  
bhavato rakṣaṇaṃ kāryyaṃ tattāvat kartumarhati।  
nirudvignastapaḥ kartuṃ na hi śaknomi pārthiva ।। 26.34 ।।  
  
mamāśramasamīpeṣu sameṣu marudhanvasu।  
samudro vālukāpūrṇastatra tiṣṭhati bhūpate ।। 26.35 ।।  
  
devatānāmavadhyastu mahākāyo mahābalaḥ।  
antarbhūmigatastatra vālukāntarhito mahān ।। 26.36 ।।  
  
sa manostanayaḥ krūro dhundhurnāma sudāruṇaḥ।  
śataṃ lokavināśāya tapa āsthāya dāruṇam ।। 26.37 ।।  
  
saṃvatsarasya paryyante sa niḥśvāsaṃ pramuñcati।  
yadā tadā mahī tatra calitā sma sakānanā ।। 26.38 ।।  
  
tasya niḥśvāsavātena raja uddhūyate mahat।  
ādityapathamāvṛtya saptāhaṃ bhūmikampanam ।। 26.39 ।।  
  
savisphuliṅgaṃ sajvālaṃ sadhūmamatidāruṇam ।  
tena rājanna śaknomi tasmin sthātuṃ sva āśrame ।। 26.40 ।।  
  
taṃ vāraya mahābāho lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā।  
tejaste sumahāviṣṇustejasāpyāyayiṣyati ।। 26.41 ।।  
  
lokāḥ svasthā bhavantvadya tasmin vinihate'sure ।  
tvaṃ hi tasya vadhāyādya samarthaḥ pṛthivīpate ।। 26.42 ।।  
  
viṣṇunā ca varo datto mama pūrvvaṃ tato'nagha।  
na hi dhundhurmahāvīryyastejasālpena śakyate ।। 26.43 ।।  
  
nirddagdhuṃ pṛthivīpāla api varṣa śatairiha।  
vīryyaṃ hi sumahattasya devairapi durāsaham ।। 26.44 ।।  
  
evamuktastu rājarṣiruttaṅkena mahātmanā।  
kubalāśvaṃ sutaṃ prādāttasmin dhundhunivāraṇe ।। 26.45 ।।  
  
rājā saṃnyastaśastro'hamayantu tanayo mama।  
bhaviṣyati dvijaśveṣṭha dhundhumāro na saṃśayaḥ ।। 26.46 ।।  
  
sa taṃ vyādiśya tanayaṃ dhundhumāraṇamudyatam।  
jagāma parvvatāyaiva tapase śaṃsitavrataḥ ।। 26.47 ।।  
  
kubalāśvastu dharmmātmā piturvacanamāsthitaḥ।  
sahasrairekaviṃśatyā putrāṇāṃ saha pārthivaḥ।  
prāyāduttaṅka sahito dhundhostasya nivāraṇe ।। 26.48 ।।  
  
tamāviśattato viṣṇurbhagavān svena tejasā।  
uttaṅkasya niyogāttu lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 26.49 ।।  
  
tasmin prayāte durddharṣe divi śabdo mahānabhūt।  
adyaprubhṛtyeṣa nṛpo dhundhumāro bhaviṣyati ।। 26.50 ।।  
  
divyaiḥ puṣpaiśca taṃ devāḥ samamaṃsata adbhutam।  
sagatvā puruṣa vyāghrastanayaiḥ saha vīryyavān ।। 26.51 ।।  
  
samudraṃ khanayāmāsa vālukārṇavamavyayam।  
nārāyaṇena rājarṣistejasāpyāyito hi saḥ ।। 26.52 ।।  
  
babhūvātibalo bhūya uttaṅkasya vaśe sthitaḥ।  
tasya putraiḥ khanadbhiśca vālukāntarhitastadā ।। 26.53 ।।  
  
dhundhurāsāditastatra diśamāśritya paścimām।  
mukhajenāgninā kruddho lokānudvarttayanniva ।। 26.54 ।।  
  
vāri śuśrāva yogena mahodadhirivodaye।  
somasya somapaśreṣṭha dhārormikalilo mahān ।। 26.55 ।।  
  
tasya putrāstu nirddagdhāstribhirūnāstu rākṣasāḥ।  
tataḥ sa rājātibalo dhundhubandhunibarhaṇaḥ ।। 26.56 ।।  
  
tasya vārimayaṃ vegamapibat sa narādhipaḥ।  
yogī yogena vahniṃ vā śamayāmāsa vāriṇā ।। 26.57 ।।  
  
nirasyattaṃ mahākāyaṃ balenodakarākṣasam।  
uttaṅkaṃ darśayāmāsa kṛtakarmmā narādhipaḥ ।। 26.58 ।।  
  
uttaṅkaśca varaṃ prādāttasmai rājñe mahātmane।  
adāttasyākṣayaṃ vittaṃ śatrubhiścāpyadhṛṣyatām ।। 26.59 ।।  
  
dharmme ratiñca satataṃ svarge vāsaṃ tathākṣayam।  
putrāṇāṃ cākṣayāँllokān svarge ye rākṣasā hatāḥ ।। 26.60 ।।  
  
tasya putrāstrayaḥ śiṣṭā dṛḍhāśvo jyeṣṭha ucyate।  
bhadrāśvaḥ kapilāśvaśca kanīyāsau tu tau smṛtau ।। 26.61 ।।  
  
dhaundhumārirdṛḍhāśvastu haryaśvastasya cātmajaḥ।  
haryaśvasya nikumbho'bhūt kṣatradharmarataḥ sadā ।। 26.62 ।।  
  
saṃhatāśvo nikumbhasya śruto raṇaviśāradaḥ ।  
kṛśāśvaścākṣayāśvaśca saṃhatāśca sutāvubhau ।। 26.63 ।।  
  
tasya patnī haimavatī satāṃ matidṛṣadvatī।  
vikhyātā triṣu lokeṣu putrastasyāḥ prasenajit ।। 26.64 ।।  
  
yuvanāśvaḥ sutastasya triṣu lokeṣvatidyutiḥ।  
atyantadhārmiko gaurī tasya patnī pativratā ।। 26.65 ।।  
  
abhiśastā tu sā bhartrā nadī sā bāhudā kṛtā ।  
tasyāstu gaurikaḥ putra ścakravarttī babhūva ha ।। 26.66 ।।  
  
māndhātā yauvanāśvo vai trailokyavijayī nṛpaḥ।  
atrāpyudāharantīmau ślokau paurāṇikī dvijāḥ ।। 26.67 ।।  
  
yāvatsūrya udayati yāvacca pratitiṣṭhati।  
sarvaṃ tadyauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ kṣetramucyate ।। 26.68 ।।  
  
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ ślokaṃ vaṃśavido janāḥ ।  
yauvanāśvaṃ mahātmānaṃ yajvāna mamitaujasam।  
māndhātā tu tanurviṣṇoḥ purāṇajñāḥ prajakṣate ।। 26.69 ।।  
  
tasya caitrarathī bhāryyā śaśabindoḥ sutā'bhavat।  
sādhvī bindumatī nāma rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ।। 26.70 ।।  
  
pativratā ca jyeṣṭā ca bhrātṝṇāmayutasya sā।  
tasyāmutpādayāmāsa māndhātā trīn sutān prabhuḥ ।। 26.71 ।।  
  
purukutsamambarīṣaṃ mucukundañca viśrutam।  
ambarīṣasya dāyādo yuvanāśvo'paraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 26.72 ।।  
  
harito yuvanāśvasya hāritāḥ śūrayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
ete hyaṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ ।। 26.73 ।।  
  
purukutsasya dāyādastrasaddasyurmahāyaśāḥ।  
narmadāyāṃ samutpannaḥ sambhūtastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 26.74 ।।  
  
sambhūtasyātmajaḥ putro hyanaraṇyaḥ pratāpavān।  
rāvaṇena hato yena trilokīvijaye purā ।। 26.75 ।।  
  
trasadaśvo'naraṇyasya haryyaśvastasya cātmajaḥ ।  
haryyaśvāttu dṛṣadvatyāṃ jajñe vasumato nṛpaḥ ।। 26.76 ।।  
  
tasya putro'bhavadrājā tridhanvā nāma dhārmmikaḥ।  
āsīt traidhanvanaścāpi vidvāṃstrayyāṃ raṇaprabhuḥ ।। 26.77 ।।  
  
tasya satyavrato nāma kumāro'bhūnmahābalaḥ।  
tena bhāryyā vidarbhasya hṛtā hatvā divaukasaḥ ।। 26.78 ।।  
  
pāṇigrahaṇamantreṣu niṣṭāṃ samprāpitoṣviha।  
viṣṇuvṛddhaḥ sutastasya viṣṇu vṛddho yataḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
ete hyaṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ kṣātropetāḥ samāśritāḥ ।। 26.79 ।।  
  
kāmādbalācca mohācca saṅkarṣaṇabalena ca।  
bhāvino'rthasya ca balāt tatkṛtaṃ tena dhīmatā ।। 26.80 ।।  
  
tamadharmmeṇa saṃyuktaṃ pitā trayīguṇo'tyajat।  
apadhvaṃseti bahuśo'vadat krodhasamanvitaḥ ।। 26.81 ।।  
  
pitaraṃ so'bravīdekaḥ kva gacchāmīti vai muhuḥ।  
pitā cainamathovāca śvapākaiḥ saha varttaya ।। 26.82 ।।  
  
nāhaṃ putreṇa putrārthī tvayādya kulapāṃsana।  
ityuktaḥ sa nirākrāmannagarādvacanādvibho ।। 26.83 ।।  
  
na cainaṃ dhārayāmāsa vasiṣṭo bhagavānṛṣiḥ।  
sa tu satyavrato dhīmāñchvapākāvasathāntikam।  
pitrā mukto'vasadvīraḥ pitā cāsya vanaṃ yayau ।। 26.84 ।।  
  
tasmiṃstu viṣaye tasya nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ।  
samā dvādaśa saṃpūrṇāstenādharmmeṇa vai tadā ।। 26.85 ।।  
  
dārāṃstu tasya viṣaye viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ।  
saṃnyasya sāgarānūpe cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।। 26.86 ।।  
  
tasya patnī gale baddhvā madhyamaṃ putramaurasam।  
śikhayā bharaṇārthāya vyakrīṇādghośatena vai ।। 26.87 ।।  
  
taṃ tu baddhaṃ gale dṛṣṭvā vikrītaṃ taṃ narottamaḥ।  
maharṣiputraṃ dharmmātmā mokṣayāmāsa suvrataḥ ।। 26.88 ।।  
  
satyavrato mahābuddhirbharaṇaṃ tasya cākarot ।  
viśvāmitrasya tuṣṭyarthamanukampārthameva ca ।। 26.89 ।।  
  
so'bhavadghālavo nāma gale baddho mahātapāḥ।  
maharṣiḥ kauśikastātastena vīryeṇa mokṣitaḥ ।। 26.90 ।।  
  
tasya vratena bhaktyā ca kṛpayā ca pratijñayā।  
viśvāmitrakalatrañca babhāra vinaye sthitaḥ ।। 26.91 ।।  
  
hatvā mṛgān varāhāṃśca mahiṣāṃśca vanecarān।  
viśvāmitrāśramābhyāśe tanmāṃsamapacattataḥ ।। 26.92 ।।  
  
upāṃśuvratamāsthāya dīkṣāṃ dvādaśavārṣikīm।  
piturniyogātabhajannṛpe tu vanamāsthite ।। 26.93 ।।  
  
ayodhyāñcaiva rājyañca tathaivāntaḥpuraṃ muniḥ।  
yājyopādhyāyasaṃyogādvasiṣṭhaḥ parirakṣitaḥ ।। 26.94 ।।  
  
satyavratastu bālyāttu bhāvino'rthasya vai balāt।  
vasiṣṭe'bhyādhikaṃ manyuṃ dhārayāmāsa manyunā ।। 26.95 ।।  
  
pitrā rudaṃstadā rāṣṭrāt parityaktaṃ svamātmajam।  
na vārayāmāsa munirvasiṣṭhaḥ kāraṇena vai ।। 26.96 ।।  
  
pāṇigrahaṇamantrāṇāṃ niṣṭā syāt saptame pade।  
evaṃ satyavratastān vai kṛtavān saptame pade ।। 26.97 ।।  
  
jānan dharmmān vasiṣṭhastu na ca mantrānihecchati।  
iti satyavrate roṣaṃ vasiṣṭo manasākarot ।। 26.98 ।।  
  
gururbuddhyā tu bhagavān vasiṣṭhaḥ kṛtavāṃstadā।  
na tu satyavrato buddhyā upāṃśuvratamasya vai ।। 26.99 ।।  
  
tasmiṃścoparate yo yatpiturāsīnmahāmanāḥ।  
tena dvādaśavarṣāṇi nāvarṣat pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 26.100 ।।  
  
tena tvidānīṃ bahudhā dīkṣāṃ tāṃ durbalāṃ bhuvi।  
kulasya niṣkṛtiḥ svasya kṛteyañca bhavediti ।। 26.101 ।।  
  
tato vasiṣṭo bhagavān pitrā tyaktaṃ nyavārayat।  
abhiṣekṣyāmyahaṃ rājye paścādenamiti prabhuḥ ।। 26.102 ।।  
  
sa tu dvādaśavarṣāṇi dīkṣāntāmudvahan balī।  
avidyamāne māṃse tu vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 26.103 ।।  
  
sarvvakāmadughāṃ dhenuṃ saṃdadarśa nṛpātmajaḥ।  
tāṃ vai krodhācca mohācca śramāccaiva kṣudhānvitaḥ ।। 26.104 ।।  
  
dasyudharmmaṃ gato dṛṣṭvā jaghāna balināṃ varaḥ।  
sa tu māṃsaṃ svayaṃ caiva viśvāmitrasya cātmajān ।। 26.105 ।।  
  
bhojayāmāsa tacchrutvā vasiṣṭhastaṃ tadātyajat।  
provāca caiva bhagavān vasiṣṭhastaṃ nṛpātmajam ।। 26.106 ।।  
  
pātaye krūra he krūra tava śaṃkumayomayam ।  
yadi te trīṇi śaṃkūni na syurhi puruṣādhama ।। 26.107 ।।  
  
pituścāparitoṣeṇa gurordogdhrīvadhena ca।  
aproṣitopayogācca trividhaste vyatikramaḥ ।। 26. 108 ।।  
  
evaṃ sa trīṇi śaṃkūni dṛṣṭvā tasya mahā tapāḥ।  
triśaṅkuriti hovāca triśaṅkustena sa smṛtaḥ ।। 26.109 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrastu dārāṇāmāgato bharaṇe kṛte।  
tatastasmai varaṃ prādāttadā prītastriśaṅkave ।। 26.110 ।।  
  
chandyamāno vareṇātha guruṃ vrave nṛpātmajaḥ।  
anāvṛṣṭibhaye tasmin gate dvādaśavārṣike ।। 26.111 ।।  
  
abhiṣicya rājye pitrye yājayāmāsa taṃ muniḥ।  
miṣatāṃ daivatānāñca vasiṣṭhasya ca kauśikaḥ।  
saśarīraṃ tadā taṃ vai divamāropayat prabhuḥ ।। 26.112 ।।  
  
miṣatastu vasiṣṭhasya tadadbhutamivābhavat।  
atrāpyudāharantīmau ślokau paurāṇikā janāḥ ।। 26.113 ।।  
  
viśvāmitraprasādena triśaṅkurdivi rājate ।  
devai sārddhaṃ mahātejānugrahāttasya dhīmataḥ ।। 26.114 ।।  
  
śanairyātyabalā ramyā hemante candramaṇḍitā।  
alaṃkṛtā tribhirbhāvaistriśaṅkugrahabhūṣitā ।। 26.115 ।।  
  
tasya satyaratā nāma bhāryyā kekayavaṃśajā।  
kumāraṃ janayāmāsa hariścandramakalmaṣam ।। 26.116 ।।  
  
sa tu rājā hariścandrastraiśaṅkava iti śrutaḥ ।  
āharttā rājasūyasya samrāḍiti pariśrutaḥ ।। 26.117 ।।  
  
hariścandrasya tu suto rohito nāma vīryyavān।  
harito rohitasyātha caṃcuhārīta ucyate ।। 26.118 ।।  
  
vijayaśca sudevaśca caṃcuputrau babhūvatuḥ।  
jetā sarvvasya kṣatrasya vijayastena sa smṛtaḥ ।। 26.119 ।।  
  
rurukastanayastatra rājā dharmmārthakovidaḥ।  
rurukāddhṛtakaḥ putrastasmādbāhuśca jajñivān ।। 26.120 ।।  
  
haihayaistālajaṅghaiśca nirasto vyasanī nṛpaḥ।  
śakairyavanakāmbojaiḥ pāradaiḥ pahlavaistathā ।। 26.121 ।।  
  
nātyarthaṃ dhārmmiko'bhūt sa dharmmye satyayuge tathā।  
sagarastu suto bāhorjajñe saha gareṇa vai।  
bhṛgorāśramamāsādya turveṇa parirakṣitaḥ ।। 26.122 ।।  
  
āgneyamastraṃ labdhvā tu bhārgavāt sagaro nṛpaḥ।  
jaghāna pṛthivīṅgatvā tālajaṃghān sahaihayān ।। 26.123 ।।  
  
śakānāṃ pahlavānāñca dharmmānnirasadacyutaḥ।  
kṣatriyāṇāṃ tathā teṣāṃ pāradānāñca dharmmavit ।। 26.124 ।।  
  
         ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
kathaṃ sa sagaro rājā gareṇa saha jajñivān।  
kimarthañca śakādīnāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mahaujasām।  
dharmmān kulocitān kruddho rājā nirasadacyutaḥ ।। 26.125 ।।  
  
             sūta uvāca।।  
bāhorvyasaninastasya hṛtaṃ rājyaṃ purā kila।  
haihayaistālajaṃvaiśca śakaiḥ sārddhaṃ samāgataiḥ ।। 26.126 ।।  
  
yavanāḥ pāradāścaiva kāmbojāḥ pahlavāstathā।  
haihayārthaṃ parākrāntā ete pañcagaṇāstadā ।। 26.127 ।।  
  
hṛtaṃ rājyaṃ balīyobhirebhiḥ kṣatriyapuṅgavaiḥ ।  
hṛtarājyastadā bāhuḥ saṃnyasya nu tadā nṛpaḥ।  
vanaṃ praviśya dharmmātmā saha patnyā tapo'carat ।। 26.128 ।।  
  
kasyacittvatha kālasya toyārthaṃ prasthito nṛpaḥ।  
vṛddhatvāddurbbalatvācca antarā sa mamāra ca ।। 26.129 ।।  
  
patnī tu yādavī tasya sagarbhā pṛṣṭhato'nvagāt ।  
sapatnyā tu garastasyai datto garbhajighāṃsayā ।। 26.130 ।।  
  
sā tu bhartuścitāṃ kṛtvā vahnau taṃ samarohayat।  
aurvastāṃ bhārgavo dṛṣṭvā kāruṇyādvinyavarttayat ।। 26.131 ।।  
  
tasyāśrame tu taṅgarbhaṃ sāgareṇa tadā saha।  
vyajāyata mahābāhuṃ sagaraṃ nāma dhārmikam ।। 26.132 ।।  
  
aurvastu jātakarmādīn kṛtvā tasya mahātmanaḥ।  
adhyāpya vedaśāstrāṇi tato'straṃ pratyapādayat ।। 26.133 ।।  
  
jāmadagnyāttadāgneyamasurairapi duḥsaham।  
sa tenāstrabalenaiva balena ca samanvitaḥ ।  
jaghāna haihayān kruddho rudraḥ paśugaṇāniva ।। 26.134 ।।  
  
tataḥ śakān sayavanān kāmbojān pāradāṃstathā।  
pahlavāṃścaiva niḥśeṣān kartuṃ vyavasito nṛpaḥ ।। 26.135 ।।  
  
te vadhyamānā vīreṇa sagareṇa mahātmanā।  
vasiṣṭhaṃ śaraṇaṃ sarvve prapannāḥ śaraṇaiṣiṇaḥ ।। 26.136 ।।  
  
vasiṣṭhastān tathetyuktvā samayena mahāmuniḥ ।  
sagaraṃ vārayāmāsa teṣāndattvā'bhayantadā ।। 26.137 ।।  
  
sagaraḥ svāmpratijñāñca gurorvāsyaṃ niśamya ca।  
dharmmaṃ jaghāna teṣāṃ vai veṣānyatvaṃ cakāra ha ।। 26.138 ।।  
  
arddhaṃ śakānāṃ śiraso muṇḍayitvā vyasarjayat।  
yavanānāṃ śiraḥ sarvaṃ kāmbojānāntathaiva ca।। 26.139 ।।  
  
pāradā muktakeśāśca pahlavāḥ śmaśru dhāriṇaḥ।  
niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārāḥ kṛtāstena mahātmanā ।। 26.140 ।।  
  
śakā yavanakāmbojāḥ pahlavāḥ pāradaiḥ saha।  
kelisparśā māhiṣikā dārvāścolāḥ khasāstathā ।। 26.141 ।।  
  
sarvve te kṣatriyagaṇā dharmmasteṣāṃ nirākṛtaḥ।  
vasiṣṭhavacanātpūrvaṃ sagareṇa mahātmanā ।। 26.142 ।।  
  
sa dharmavijayī rājā vijityemāṃ vasundharām।  
aśvaṃ vicārayāmāsa vājimedhāya dīkṣitaḥ ।। 26.143 ।।  
  
tasya cārayataḥ so'śvaḥ samudre pūrvadakṣiṇe।  
velāsamīpe'pahṛto bhūmiñcaiva praveśitaḥ ।। 26.144 ।।  
  
sa tandeśaṃ sutaiḥ sarvaiḥ khanayāmāsa pārthivaḥ।  
āseduśca tatastasmiṃstadantaste mahārṇave ।। 26.145 ।।  
  
tamādipuruṣaṃ devaṃ hariṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prajāpatim।  
viṣṇuṃ kapilarūpeṇa haṃsaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।। 26.146 ।।  
  
tasya cakṣuḥ samāsādya tejastat pratipadyate।  
dagdhāḥ putrāstadā sarve catvārastvavaśeṣitāḥ ।। 26.147 ।।  
  
barhiketuḥ saketuśca tathā dharmmaratastrayaḥ।  
śūraḥ pañcavanaścaiva tasya vaṃśakarāḥ prabho ।। 26.148 ।।  
  
prādācca tasya bhagavān harirnārāyaṇo varān।  
akṣayatvaṃ svavaṃśasya vājimedhaśataṃ tathā।  
vibhuṃ putraṃ samudrañca svarge vāsaṃ tathākṣayam ।। 26.149 ।।  
  
sa samudro'śvamādāya vandade (?) saritāṃpatiḥ।  
sāgaratvaṃ ca lebhe sa karmaṇā tena tasya vai ।। 26.150 ।।  
  
taṃ cāśvamedhikaṃ so'śvaṃ samudrāt prāpya pārthivaḥ।  
ājahārāśvamedhānāṃ śataṃ caiva punaḥ punaḥ ।। 26.151 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi dagdhānyaśvānusāriṇām।  
teṣāṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tejaḥ praviṣṭānāṃ mahātmanām।  
putrāṇāntu sahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭistu iti naḥ śrutam ।। 26.152 ।।  
  
        ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।.  
sagarasyātmajā rājñaḥ kathaṃ jātā mahābalāḥ।  
vikrāntāḥ ṣaṣṭisāhasrā vidhinā kena vā vada ।। 26.153 ।।  
  
            sūta uvāca।।  
dve patnyau sagarasyāstāṃ tapasā dagdhakilbiṣe।  
jyeṣṭā vidarbhaduhitā keśinī nāma nāmataḥ ।। 26.154 ।।  
  
kanīyasī tu yā tasya patnī paramadharmiṇī।  
ariṣṭanemiduhitā rūpeṇāpratimā bhuvi ।। 26.155 ।।  
  
aurvastābhyāṃ varaṃ prādāt tapasārādhitaḥ prabhuḥ।  
ekā janiṣyate putraṃ vaṃśakarttāramīpsitam।  
ṣaṣṭiputraṃ sahasrāṇi dvitīyā janayiṣyati ।। 26.156 ।।  
  
munestu vacanaṃ śrutvā keśinī putramekakam।  
vaṃśasya kāraṇaṃ śreṣṭā jagrāha nṛpasaṃsadi ।। 26.157 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi suparṇabhaginī tathā।  
mahātmanastu jagrāha sumatiḥ poṣaṇe nṛpaḥ ।। 26.158 ।।  
  
atha kāle gate jyeṣṭā jyeṣṭhaṃ putraṃ vyajāyata।  
asamañja iti khyātaṃ kākutsthaṃ sagarātmajam ।। 26.159 ।।  
  
sumatistvapi jajñe vai garbhantumbaṃ yaśasvinī।  
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi tumbamadhyādviniḥsṛtāḥ ।। 26.160 ।।  
  
ghṛtapūrṇeṣu kumbheṣu tān garbhān nyadadhattataḥ।  
dhātrīścaikaikaśaḥ prādāt tāvatīḥ poṣaṇe nṛpaḥ ।। 26.161 ।।  
  
tato navasu māseṣu samuttasthuryathāsukham।  
kumārāste mahābhāgāḥ sagaraprītivarddhanāḥ ।। 26.162 ।।  
  
kālena mahatā caiva cauvanaṃ pratipedire।  
ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi teṣāmaśvānusāriṇām ।। 26.163 ।।  
  
sa tu jyeṣṭo naravyāghraḥ sagarasyātmasambhavaḥ।  
asamañja iti khyāto barhiketurmahābalaḥ ।। 26.164 ।।  
  
paurāṇāmahite yuktaḥ pitrā nirvāsitaḥ purā।  
tasya putroṃ'śumānnāma asamañjasya vīryavān ।। 26.165 ।।  
  
tasya putrastu dharmātmā dilīpa iti viśrutaḥ।  
dilīpāttu mahātejā vīro jāto bhagīrathaḥ ।। 26.166 ।।  
  
yena gaṅgā saricchreṣṭā vimānairupaśobhitā ।  
ījā'nena samudrādvai duhitṛtvena kalpitā।  
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ ślokaṃ paurāṇikā janāḥ ।। 26.167 ।।  
  
bhagīrathastu tāṃ gaṅgāmānayāmāsa karmabhiḥ ।  
tasmādbhāgīrathī gaṅgā kathyate vaṃśavittamaiḥ ।। 26.168 ।।  
  
bhagīrathasutaścāpi śruto nāma babhūva ha।  
nābhāgastasya dāyādo nityaṃ dharmaparāyaṇaḥ ।। 26.169 ।।  
  
ambarīṣaḥ sutastasya sindhudvīpastato'bhavat।  
evaṃ vaṃśapurāṇajñā gāyantīti pariśrutam ।। 26.170 ।।  
  
nābhāgerambarīṣasya bhujābhyāṃ paripālitā।  
babhūva vasudhātyarthaṃ tāpatrayavivarjitā ।। 26.171 ।।  
  
ayutāyuḥ sutastasya sindhudvīpasya vīryavān।  
ayutāyostu dāyāda ṛtuparṇo mahāyaśāḥ ।। 26.172 ।।  
  
divyākṣahṛdajño'sau rājā nalasakho balī।  
nalau dvāviti vikhyātau purāṇeṣu dṛḍhavratau ।। 26.173 ।।  
  
vīrasenātmajaścaiva yaścekṣvākukulodvahaḥ।  
ṛtuparṇasya putro'bhūt sarvvakāmo janeśvaraḥ ।। 26.174 ।।  
  
sudāsastasya tanayo rājā haṃsamukho'bhavat।  
sudāsasya sutaḥ proktaḥ saudāso nāma pārthivaḥ ।। 26.175 ।।  
  
khyātaḥ kalmāṣapādo vai nāmnā mitrasahaśca saḥ ।  
vasiṣṭhastu mahātejāḥ kṣetre kalmāṣapādake।  
aśmakaṃ janayāmāsa ikṣvākukulavṛddhaye ।। 26.176 ।।  
  
aśmakasyorakāmastu mūlakastatsuto'bhavat।  
atrāpyudāharantīmaṃ mūlakaṃ vai nṛpaṃ prati ।। 26.177 ।।  
  
sa hi rāmabhayādrājā strībhiḥ parivṛto'vasat।  
vivastrastrāṇamicchan vai nārīkavacamīśvaraḥ ।। 26.178 ।।  
  
mūlakasyāpi dharmātmā rājā śatarathaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
tasmācchatarathājjajñe rājā caiḍiviḍo balī ।। 26.179 ।।  
  
āsīttvaiḍiviḍaḥ śrīmān kṛtaśarmā pratāpavān।  
putro viśvamahattasya putrīkasya vyajāyata ।। 26.180 ।।  
  
dilīpastasya putro'bhūt khaṭvāṅga iti viśrutaḥ।  
yena svargādihāgamya muhūrttaṃ prāpya jīvitam।  
trayo'bhisaṃhitā lokā buddhyā satyena caiva hi ।। 26.181 ।।  
  
dīrgabāhuḥ sutastasya raghustasmādajāyata।  
ajaḥ putro raghoścāpi tasmājjajñe sa vīryavān।  
rājā daśaratho nāma ikṣvākukulanandanaḥ ।। 26.182 ।।  
  
rāmo dāśarathirvīro dharmajño lokaviśrutaḥ।  
bharato lakṣmaṇaścaiva śatrughnaśca mahābalaḥ ।। 26.183 ।।  
  
mādhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ hatvā gatvā madhuvanañca tat।  
śatrughnena purī tasya mathurā sanniveśitā ।। 26.184 ।।  
  
subāhuḥ śūrasenaśca śatrughnasahitāvubhau।  
pālayāmāsatuḥ sūnū vaidehyau mathurāṃ purīm ।। 26.185 ।।  
  
aṅgadaścāndraketuśca lakṣmaṇasyātmajāvubhau।  
himavatparvatābhyāśe sphītau janapadau tayoḥ ।। 26.186 ।।  
  
ahgadasyāṅgadīyā tu deśe kārapathe purī।  
candraketostu mallasya candravaktā purī śubhā ।। 26.187 ।।  
  
bharatasyātmajau vīrau takṣaḥ puṣkara eva ca।  
gāndhāraviṣaye siddhe tayoḥ puryau mahātmanoḥ ।। 26.188 ।।  
  
takṣasya dikṣu vikhyātā ramyā takṣaśilā purī।  
puṣkarasyāpi vīrasya vikhyātā puṣkarāvatī ।। 26.189 ।।  
  
gāthāṃ caivātra gāyanti ye purāṇavido jatāḥ।  
rāme nibaddhāssattvārthā māhātmyāttasya dhīmataḥ ।। 26.190 ।।  
  
śyāmo yuvā lohitākṣo dīptāsyo mitabhāṣitaḥ।  
ājānubāhuḥ sumukhaḥ siṃhaskandho mahābhujaḥ ।। 26.191 ।।  
  
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi rāmo rājyamakārayat।  
ṛksāmayajuṣāṃ ghoṣo jyāghoṣaśca mahāsvanaḥ ।। 26.192 ।।  
  
avicchinno'bhavadrāṣṭre dīyatāṃ bhujyatāmiti।  
janasthāne vasan kāryaṃ tridaśānāñcakārasaḥ ।। 26.193 ।।  
  
tamāgaskāriṇaṃ pūrvaṃ paulastyaṃ manujarṣabhaḥ।  
sītāyāḥ padamanvicchan nijaghāna mahāyaśāḥ ।। 26.194 ।।  
  
sattvavān guṇasampanno dīpyamānaḥ sva tejasā।  
atisūryañca vahniñca rāmo dāśarathirbabhau ।। 26.195 ।।  
  
evameva mahābāhurikṣvākukulanandanaḥ ।  
rāvaṇaṃ sagaṇaṃ hatvā divamācakrame vibhuḥ ।। 26.196 ।।  
  
śrīrāmasyātmajo jajñe kuśa ityabhidhīyate।  
lavaścānyo mahāvīryastayordeśau nibodhata ।। 26.197 ।।  
  
kuśasya kośalā rājyaṃ purī vāpi kuśasthalī।  
ramyā niveśitā tena vindhyaparvatasānuṣu ।। 26.198 ।।  
  
uttarākośale rājyaṃ lavasya ca mahātmanaḥ।  
śrāvastī lokavikhyātā kuśavaṃśaṃ nibodhata ।। 26.199 ।।  
  
kuśasya putro dharmātmā hyatithiḥ supriyātithiḥ।  
atitherapi vikhyāto niṣadho nāma pārthivaḥ ।। 26.200 ।।  
  
niṣadhasya nalaḥ putro nabhaḥ putro nalasya tu।  
nabhasaḥ puṇḍarīkastu kṣemadhanvā tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 26.201 ।।  
  
kṣemadhanvasuto rājā devānīkaḥ pratāpavān।  
āsīdahīnagurnāma devānī kātmajaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 26.202 ।।  
  
ahīnagostu dāyādaḥ pāriyātro mahāyaśāḥ।  
dalastasyātmajaścāpi tasmājjajñe balo nṛpaḥ ।। 26.203 ।।  
  
auṅko nāma sa dharmātmā balaputro babhūva ha।  
vajranābhaḥ sutastasya śaṅkhaṇastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 26.204 ।।  
  
śaṃkhaṇasya suto vidvān dhyuṣitāśca iti śrutaḥ ।  
dhyuṣitāśca sutaścāpi rājā viśvasahaḥ kila ।। 26.205 ।।  
  
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo vasiṣṭhastatsuto'bhavat।  
pautrasya jaimineḥ śiṣyaḥ smṛtaḥ sarveṣu śarmasu ।। 26.206 ।।  
  
śatāni saṃhitānāntu pañca yo'dhītavāṃstataḥ।  
tasmādadhigato yogo yājñavalkyena dhīmatā ।। 26.207 ।।  
  
puṣyastasya suto vidvān dhruvasandhiśca tatsutaḥ।  
sudarśanastasya suto agnivarṇaḥ sudarśanāt ।। 26.208 ।।  
  
agnivarṇasya śīghrastu śīghrakasya manuḥ smṛtaḥ।  
manustu yogamāsthāya kalāpagrāmamāsthitaḥ।  
ekonaviṃśaprayuge kṣatraprāvarttakaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 26.209 ।।  
  
prasuśruto manoḥ putraḥ susandhistasya cātmajaḥ।  
susandheśca tathāmarṣaḥ sahasvānnāma nāmataḥ ।। 26.210 ।।  
  
āsītsahasvataḥ putro rājā viśrutavāniti।  
tasyāsīdviśrutavataḥ putro rājā bṛhadbalaḥ ।। 26.211 ।।  
  
ete ikṣvākudāyādā rājānaḥ prāyaśaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
vaṃśe pradhānā ye te'smin prādhānyena tu kīrttitāḥ ।। 26.212 ।।  
  
paṭhan samyagimāṃ sṛṣṭimādityasya vivasvataḥ।  
prajāvāneti sāyujyaṃ manorvaivasvatasya saḥ ।। 26.213 ।।  
  
śrāddhadevasya devasya prajānāṃ puṣṭidasya ca।  
vipāpmā virajāścaiva āyuṣmān bhavate'cyutaḥ ।। 26.214 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte vaivasvatamanuvaṃśavarṇanaṃ nāma ṣaḍ‌viṃśodhyāyaḥ ।। 26 ।। *  
   


---
title: 027

---
          ।।sūta uvāca।।  
anujasya vikukṣestu nimervaṃśaṃ nibodhata।  
yo'sau niveśayāmāsa purandevapuropamam ।। 27.1 ।।  
  
jayantamitivikhyātaṃ gautamasyāśramābhitaḥ।  
yasyānvavāye yajñe vai janakādṛṣisattamāt ।। 27.2 ।।  
  
nemirnāma sudharmātmā sarvasatvanamaskṛtaḥ।  
āsīt putro mahāprājña ikṣvākorbhūritejasaḥ ।। 27.3 ।।  
  
sa śāpena vasiṣṭhasya videhaḥ samapadyata।  
tasya putro mithirnāma janitaḥ parvabhistribhiḥ ।। 27.4 ।।  
  
araṇyāṃ mathyamānāyāṃ prādurbhūto mahāyaśāḥ।  
nāmnā mithiriti khyāto jananājjanako'bhavat ।। 27.5 ।।  
  
mithirnāma mahāvīryo yenāsau mithilābhavat।  
rājāsau janako nāma janakāccāpyudāvasuḥ ।। 27.6 ।।  
  
udāvasoḥ sudharmātmā janito nandivarddhanaḥ।  
nandivarddhanataḥ śūraḥ suketurnāma dhārmikaḥ ।। 27.7 ।।  
  
suketorapi dharmātmā devarāto mahābalaḥ।  
devarātasya dharmātmā bṛhaduccha iti śrutiḥ ।। 27.8 ।।  
  
bṛhaducchasya tanayo mahāvīryaḥ pratāpavān ।  
mahāvīryasya dhṛtimān sudhṛtistasya cātmajaḥ ।। 27.9 ।।  
  
sudhṛterapi dharmātmā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ parantapaḥ।  
dhṛṣṭaketu sutaścāpi haryaśvo nāma viśrutaḥ ।। 27.10 ।।  
  
haryaśvasya maruḥ putro maroḥ putraḥ pratitvakaḥ।  
pratitvakasya dharmātmā rājā kīrttirathaḥ sutaḥ ।। 27.11 ।।  
  
putraḥ kīrttirathasyāpi devamīḍha iti śrutaḥ ।  
devamīḍhasya vibudho vibudhasya suto dhṛtiḥ ।। 27.12 ।।  
  
mahādhṛtisuto rājā kīrttirājaḥ pratāpavān ।  
kīrtti rājātmajo vidvān mahārometi viśrutaḥ ।। 27.13 ।।  
  
mahāromṇastu vikhyātaḥ svarṇaromā vyajāyata।  
svarṇaromātmajaścāpi hrasvaromābhavanṛpaḥ ।। 27.14 ।।  
  
hrasvaromātmajo vidvān sīradhvaja iti śrutiḥ।  
udbhinnā kṛṣatā yena sītā rājñā yaśasvinī।  
rāmasya mahiṣī sādhvī suvratātipativratā ।। 27.15 ।।  
  
        śāṃśapāyana uvāca।।  
kathaṃ sītā samutpannā kṛṣyamāṇā yaśasvinī।  
kimarthañcākṛṣadrājā kṣetraṃ yasmin babhūva ha ।। 27.16 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
agnikṣetre kṛṣyamāṇe aśvamedhe mahātmanaḥ।  
vidhinā suprayuktena tasmātsā tu samutthitā ।। 27.17 ।।  
  
sīradhvajāttu jātastu bhānumānnāma maithilaḥ।  
bhrātā kuśadhvajastasya sa kāśyadhipatirnṛpaḥ ।। 27.18 ।।  
  
tasya bhānumataḥ putraḥ pradyumnaśca pratāpavān।  
munistasya sutaścāpi tasmādūrjavahaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 27.19 ।।  
  
ūrjavahāt sutadvājaḥ śakunistasya cātmajaḥ।  
svāgataḥ śakuneḥ putraḥ suvarccāstatsutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 27.20 ।।  
  
śruto yastasya dāyādaḥ suśrutastasya cātmajaḥ।  
suśrutasya jayaḥ putro jayasya vijayaḥ sutaḥ ।। 27.21 ।।  
  
vijayasya ṛtaḥ putra ṛtasya sunayaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
sunayādvītahavyastu vītahavyātmajo dhṛtiḥ ।। 27.22 ।।  
  
dhṛtestu bahulāśvo'bhūdbahulāśvasutaḥ kṛtiḥ।  
tasmin santiṣṭate vaṃśo janakānāṃ mahātmanām।  
ityete maithilāḥ proktāḥ somasyāpi nibodhata ।। 27.23 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte vaivasvatamanuvaṃśakīrttanaṃ nāma saptaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 27 ।।  
  
      vāyūmahāpurāṇam -  
       uttarārddham - 28  
       ।।sūta uvāca ।।  
  
pitā somasya vaiviprā jajñe'trirbhagavānṛṣiḥ।  
so'ti tasthau sarvalokānbhagavāntsvena tejasā ।। 28.1 ।।  
  
karmaṇā manasā vācā śubhānyeva samācaran।  
kāṣṭhakuḍyaśilābhūta ūrddhvabāhurmahādyutiḥ ।। 28.2 ।।  
  
suduścaraṃ nāma tapo yena taptaṃ mahatpurā।  
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi divyānīti hi naḥ śrutam ।। 28.3 ।।  
  
tasyorddhvaretasastatra sthitasyānimiṣaspṛham।  
somatvantanurāpede mahābuddhiḥ sa vai dvijaḥ ।। 28.4 ।।  
  
ūrddhvamācakrame tasya somatvaṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ।  
somaḥ susrāva netrābhyāṃ daśa vā dyotayan diśaḥ ।। 28.5 ।।  
  
taṃ garbhaṃ vidhinādiṣṭā daśa devyo dadhustadā।  
sametya dhārayāmāsurna ca tāḥ samaśaknuvan ।। 28.6 ।।  
  
sa tābhyaḥ sahasaivātha digbhyo garbhaḥ prabhānvitaḥ।  
yathāvabhāsayaṃllokāñjhītāṃśuḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ।। 28.7 ।।  
  
yadā na dhāraṇe śaktāstasya garbhasya tāḥ striyaḥ।  
tataḥ sa tābhiḥ śītāṃśurnipapāta vasundharām ।। 28.8 ।।  
  
patantaṃ somamālokya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।  
rathamāropayāmāsa lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 28.9 ।।  
  
sa hi devamayo viprā dharmmārthī satyasaṅgaraḥ।  
yukto vājisahasreṇa siteneti hi naḥ śrutam ।। 28.10 ।।  
  
tasminnipatite devāḥ putre'treḥ paramātmani।  
tuṣṭuvurbrahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ mānasāḥ sapta viśrutāḥ ।। 28.11 ।।  
  
tatraivāṅgirasastasya bhṛgoścaivātmajastathā।  
ṛgbhiryajurbhirbahubhiratharvāṅgirasairapi ।। 28.12 ।।  
  
tataḥ saṃstūyamānasya tejaḥ somasya bhāsvataḥ।  
āpyāyamānaṃ lokāṃstrīn bhāvayāmāsa sarvvaśaḥ ।। 28.13 ।।  
  
samena rathamukhyena sāgarāntāṃ vasundharām।  
triḥsaptakṛtvo vipula ścakārābhipradakṣiṇam ।। 28.14 ।।  
  
tasya yaccāpi tattejaḥ pṛthivīmanvapadyata।  
oṣadhyastāḥ samudbhūtāstejasā saṃjvalantyuta ।। 28.15 ।।  
  
tābhirdhāryatyayaṃ lokān prajāścāpi caturvidhāḥ।  
poṣṭā hi bhagavān somo jagato hi dvijottamāḥ ।। 28.16 ।।  
  
sa labdhatejāstapasā saṃstavaistaiśca karmmabhiḥ।  
tapastepe mahābhāgaḥ pajhānāṃ daśatīrdaśa ।। 28.17 ।।  
  
hiraṇyavarṇā yā devyo dhārayantyātmanā jagat।  
vibhustāsāmbhavetsomaḥ prakhyātaḥ svena karmmaṇā ।। 28.18 ।।  
  
tatastasmai dadau rājyaṃ brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।  
bījauṣadhiṣu viprāṇāmapāñca dvijasattamāḥ ।। 28.19 ।।  
  
so'bhiṣikto mahātejā mahārājyena rājarāṭ ।  
lokānāṃ bhāvayāmāsa svabhāvāttapatāṃ varaḥ ।। 28.20 ।।  
  
saptaviṃśatirindostu dākṣāyaṇyo mahāvratāḥ।  
dadau prācetaso dakṣo nakṣatrāṇīti yā viduḥ ।। 28.21 ।।  
  
sa tatprāpya mahadrājayaṃ somaḥ somavatāṃ prabhuḥ।  
samājajñe rājasūyaṃ sahasraśatadakṣiṇam ।। 28.22 ।।  
  
hiraṇyagarbhaścodgātā brahmā brahmatvameyivān।  
sadasyastatra bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।  
sanatkumārapramukhairādyairbrahmarṣibhirvṛtaḥ ।। 28.23 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇāmadadatsomastrīlloँkāniti naḥ śrutam।  
tebhyo brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaśca vai dvijāḥ ।। 28.24 ।।  
  
taṃ sinī ca kuhūścaiva vapuḥ puṣṭiḥ prabhāvasuḥ।  
kīrttirdhṛtiśca lakṣmīśca nava devyaḥ siṣevire ।। 28.25 ।।  
  
prāpyāvabhṛthamavyagraḥ sarvvadevarṣipūjitaḥ।  
atirājātirājendro daśadhātāpayaddiśaḥ ।। 28.26 ।।  
  
tadā tat prāpya duṣprāpamaiśvaryamṛṣisaṃstutam।  
sa vibhramamatirviprā vinaye vinayo hataḥ ।। 28.27 ।।  
  
bṛhaspateḥ sa vai bhāryāntārāṃ nāma yaśasvinīm।  
jahāra sahasā sarvvānavamatyāṅgiraḥsutān ।। 28.28 ।।  
  
sa yācyamāno devaiśca tathā devarṣibhiśca ha।  
naiva vyasarjayattārāṃ tasmāyāṅgirase tadā ।। 28.29 ।।  
  
uśanāstasya jagrāha pārṣṇimaṅgiraso dvijāḥ।  
sa hi śiṣyo mahātejāḥ pituḥ pūrvaṃ bṛhaspateḥ ।। 28.30 ।।  
  
tena snehena bhagavān rudrastasya bṛhaspateḥ।  
pārṣṇigrāho'bhavaddevaḥ pragṛhyājagavandhanuḥ ।। 28.31 ।।  
  
tena brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ paramāstraṃ mahātmanā।  
uddiśya devānutsṛṣṭaṃ yenaiṣāṃ nāśitaṃ yaśaḥ ।। 28.32 ।।  
  
tatra tadyuddhamabhavat pratyakṣantārakāmayam।  
devānāṃ dānavānāñca lokakṣayakaraṃ mahat ।। 28.33 ।।  
  
tatra śiṣṭāstrayo devāstuṣitāścaiva ye smṛtāḥ।  
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmurādidevaṃ pitāmaham ।। 28.34 ।।  
  
tato nivāryośanasaṃ rudraṃ jyeṣṭhañca śaṅkaram।  
dadāvāṅgirase tārāṃ svayameva pitāmahaḥ ।। 28.35 ।।  
  
antarvatnīṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tārāntārādhipānanām।  
garbhamutsṛjase na tvaṃ vipraḥ prāha bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 28.36 ।।  
  
madīyāyāṃ tanau yonau garbho dhāryaḥ kathañcana।  
atho nāvasṛjattantu kumāraṃ dasyuhantamam ।। 28.37 ।।  
  
īṣikāstambamāsādya jvalantamiva pāvakam।  
jātamātro'tha bhagavān devānāmākṣipadvapuḥ ।। 28.38 ।।  
  
tataḥ saṃśayamāpannāstārāmakathayan surāḥ।  
satyaṃ brūhi sutaḥ kasya somasyātha bṛhaspateḥ ।। 28.39 ।।  
  
hrīyamāṇā yadā devānnāha sā sādhvasādhu vā ।  
tadā tāṃ śaptumārabdhaḥ kumāro dasyuhantamaḥ ।। 28.40 ।।  
  
sannivārya tadā brahmā tārāṃ candrasya saṃśayaḥ।  
yadatra tathyantad‌brūhi tāre kasya sutastvayam ।। 28.41 ।।  
  
sā prāñjaliruvācedaṃ brahmāṇaṃ varadaṃ prabhum।  
somasyeti mahātmānaṃ kumārandasyuhantamam ।। 28.42 ।।  
  
tataḥ sa tamupāghāya somo dātā prajāpatiḥ।  
budha ityakaronnāma tasya putrasya dhīmataḥ ।। 28.43 ।।  
  
pratipūrvvañca gamane samabhyuttiṣṭhate budhaiḥ।  
utpādayāmāsa tadā putraṃ vai rājaputrikā ।। 28.44 ।।  
  
tasya putro mahātejā babhūvailaḥ purūravāḥ ।  
urvaśyāṃ jajñire tasya putrāḥ ṣaṭ sumahaujasaḥ ।। 28.45 ।।  
  
prasahya dharṣitastatra vivaśo rājayakṣmaṇā ।  
tato yakṣmābhibhūtastu somaḥ prakṣīṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।  
jagāma śaraṇāyātha pitaraṃ so'trimeva tu ।। 28.46 ।।  
  
tasya tatpāpaśamanaṃ cakārātrirmahāyaśāḥ।  
sa rājayakṣmaṇā muktaḥ śriyā jajvāla sarvvaśaḥ ।। 28.47 ।।  
  
etatsomasya vai janma kīrttitaṃ dvijasattamāḥ।  
vaṃśantasya dvijaśreṣṭāḥ kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। 28.48 ।।  
  
dhanyamārogyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ kalmaṣaśodhanam।  
somasya janma śrutvaiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 28.49 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte śomotpattirnāmāṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 28 ।। *  
      vāyūmahāpurāṇam -  
        uttarārddham - 29  
        sūta uvāca ।।  
  
somasya tu budhaḥ putro budhasya tu purūravāḥ।  
tejasvī dānaśīlaśca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। 29.1 ।।  
  
brahmavādī parākrāntaḥ śatrubhiryudhi durjayaḥ।  
āharttā cāgnihotrasya yajvanāñca dadau mahīm ।। 29.2 ।।  
  
satyavāk karmmabuddhiśca kāntaḥ saṃvṛtamaithunaḥ।  
atīva putro lokeṣu rūpeṇāpratimo'bhavat ।। 29.3 ।।  
  
taṃ brahmavādinaṃ dāntaṃ dharmajñaṃ satyavādinam।  
urvaśī varayāmāsa hitvā mānaṃ yaśasvinī ।। 29.4 ।।  
  
tayā sahāvasadrājā daśavarṣāṇi cāṣṭa ca।  
sapta ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa cāṣṭau ca vīryavān ।। 29.5 ।।  
  
vane caitrarathe ramye tathā mandākinītaṭe।  
alakāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ nandane ca vanottame ।। 29.6 ।।  
  
gandhamādanapādeṣu meruśrṛṅge nagottame।  
uttarāṃśca kurūn prāpya kalāpagrāmameva ca ।। 29.7 ।।  
  
eteṣu vanasukhyeṣu surairācariteṣu ca।  
urvaśyā sahito rājā reme paramayā mudā ।। 29.8 ।।  
  
          ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
gandharvā corvaśī devī rājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ katham।  
devānutsṛjya samprāptā tanno brūhi bahuśruta ।। 29.9 ।।  
  
      sūta uvāca।।  
brahmaśāpābhibhūtā sā mānuṣaṃ samupasthitā।  
ailaṃ tu taṃ varārohā samayena vyavasthitā ।। 29.10 ।।  
  
ātmanaḥ śāpamokṣārthaṃ niyamaṃ sā cakāra tu ।  
anagnadarśanañcaiva akāmāta saha maithunam ।। 29.11 ।।  
  
dvau meṣau śayanābhyāśe sa tāvad vyavatiṣṭhate।  
ghṛtamātraṃ tathāhāraḥ kālamekantu pārthiva ।। 29.12 ।।  
  
yadyeṣa samayo rājan yāvatkālañca te dṛḍham।  
tāvatkālantu vatsyāmi eṣa naḥ samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 29.13 ।।  
  
tasyāstaṃ samayaṃ sarvaṃ sa rājā paryapālayat।  
evaṃ sā cāvasat tasmin purūravasi bhāminī ।। 29.14 ।।  
  
varṣāṇyatha catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tadbhaktyā śāpamohitā।  
urvaśī mānuṣaṃ prāptā gandharvvā ścintayānvitāḥ ।। 29.15 ।।  
  
         gandharvvā ūcuḥ।  
cintayadhvaṃ mahābhāgā yathā sā tu varāṅganā।  
āgacchettu punarddevānurvaśī svargabhūṣaṇā ।। 29.16 ।।  
  
tato viśvāvasurnāma tatrāha vadatāṃ varaḥ।  
tayā tu samayastatra kriyamāṇo mato'naghaḥ ।। 29.17 ।।  
  
samayanyutkramāt sā vai rājānaṃ tyakṣyate yathā।  
tadahaṃ vacmi vaḥ sarvaṃ yathā tyakṣyati sā nṛpam ।। 29.18 ।।  
  
sahasā yogameṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ kāryasiddhaye।  
evamuktvā gatastatra pratiṣṭānaṃ mahāyaśāḥ ।। 29.19 ।।  
  
sa niśāyāmathāgamya meṣamekaṃ jahāra vai।  
mātṛvadvarttate sā tu meṣayoścāruhāsinī ।। 29.20 ।।  
  
gandharvāgamanaṃ jñātvā śayanasthā yaśasvinī।  
rājānamabravītsā tu putro me hriyateti vai ।। 29.21 ।।  
  
evamukto viniścitya nagnastiṣṭhati vai nṛpaḥ ।  
nagnaṃ drakṣyati māṃ devī samayo vitatho bhavet ।। 29.22 ।।  
  
tato bhūyastu gandharvvā dvitīyaṃ meṣamādaduḥ।  
dvitīye'pahṛte meṣe ailaṃ devī tamabravīt ।। 29.23 ।।  
  
putrau mama hṛtau rājannanāthāyā iva prabho।  
evamuktastadotthāya nagno rājā pradhāvitaḥ ।। 29.24 ।।  
  
meṣābabhyāṃ padavīṃ rājan gandharvvairvyutthitāmatha।  
utpāditā tu mahatī māyā tadbhavanaṃ mahat ।। 29.25 ।।  
  
prakāśitantu sahasā tato nagnamavekṣya sā।  
nagnaṃ dṛṣṭvā tiro'bhūtsā apsarā kāmarūpiṇī ।। 29.26 ।।  
  
tirobhūtāntu tāṃ jñātvā gandharvāstatra tāvubhau।  
meṣau tyaktvā ca te sarve tatraivāntarhitābhavan ।। 29.27 ।।  
  
utsṛṣṭāvuraṇau dṛṣṭvā rājā gṛhyāgataḥ prabhuḥ।  
apaśyaṃstāṃ tu vai rājā vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ ।। 29.28 ।।  
  
cacāra pṛthivīṃ caiva mārgamāṇastatastataḥ।  
athāpaśyacca tāṃ rājā kurukṣetre mahābalaḥ ।। 29.29 ।।  
  
plakṣatīrthe puṣkariṇyāṃ vigāḍhenāmbunāplutām।  
krīḍantīmapsarobhiśca pañcabhiḥ saha śobhanām ।। 29.30 ।।  
  
apaśyatsā tataḥ subhrū rājānamavidūrataḥ।  
urvaśī tāḥ sakhīḥ prāha ayaṃ sa puruṣottamaḥ ।। 29.31 ।।  
  
yasminnahamavātsaṃ hi darśayāmāsa taṃ nṛpam ।  
tata āvirbabhūvustāḥ pañcacūḍāpsarāstu tāḥ ।। 29.32 ।।  
  
dṛṣṭvā tu rājā tāṃ prītaḥ pralāpān kurute bahūn।  
āyāhi tiṣṭha manasā ghore vacasi tiṣṭha he ।। 29.33 ।।  
  
evamādīni sūkṣmāṇi parasparamabhāṣata।  
urvvaśī tvabravīccailaṃ sagarbhāhaṃ tvayā prabho ।। 29.34 ।।  
  
saṃvatsarāt kumāraste bhavitā nava saṃśayaḥ।  
niśāmekāntu vai rājā hyavasattu tayā saha ।। 29.35 ।।  
  
samprahṛṣṭo jagāmātha svapurantu mahāyaśāḥ।  
gate saṃvatsare rājā urvvaśīṃ punarāgamat ।। 29.36 ।।  
  
uṣitvā tu tayā sārddhamekarātraṃ mahāmanāḥ।  
kāmārttaścā bravīddīno bhava nityaṃ mameti vai ।। 29.37 ।।  
  
urvvaśyathābravīccailaṃ gandharvāste varaṃ daduḥ।  
taṃ vṛṇīṣva mahārāja brūhi caitāṃstvameva hi ।। 29.38 ।।  
  
vṛṇe nityaṃ hi sālokyaṃ gandharvāṇāṃ mahātmanām।  
tathetyuktvā varaṃ vavre gandharvāśca tathāstviti ।। 29.39 ।।  
  
sthālīmagneḥ pūrayitvā gandharvvāśca tamabruvan।  
anena iṣṭvā lokantaṃ prāpsyasi tvaṃ narādhipa ।। 29.40 ।।  
  
tamādāya kumārantu nagarāyopacakrame।  
niḥkṣipya tamaraṇyāñca sa putrantu gṛhaṃ yayau ।। 29.41 ।।  
  
punarādāya dṛśyāgnimaśvatthaṃ tatra dṛṣṭavān।  
samīpatastu taṃ dṛṣṭvā hyaśvatthaṃ tatra vismitaḥ ।। 29.42 ।।  
  
gandharvvebhyastathākhyātumagninā gāṃ gatastu saḥ ।  
śrutvā tamarthamaśilamaraṇiṃ tu samādiśat ।। 29.43 ।।  
  
aśvatthādaraṇiṃ kṛtvā mathitvāgniṃ yathāvidhi।  
teneṣṭvā tu salokaṃ naḥ prāpsyasi tvaṃ narādhipa।  
mathitvāgniṃ tridhā kṛtvā hyayajatsa narādhipaḥ ।। 29.44 ।।  
  
iṣṭvā yajñairbahuvidhairgatasteṣāṃ salokatām।  
vāsāya ca sa gandharvvastretāyāṃ sa mahārathaḥ।  
eko'gniḥ pūrvamāsīdvai ailastrīṃstānakalpayat ।। 29.45 ।।  
  
evaṃprabhāvo rājāsīdailastu dvijasattamāḥ।  
deśe puṇyatame caiva maharṣibhiralaṃkṛte ।। 29.46 ।।  
  
rājyaṃ sa kārayāmāsa prayāge pṛthivī patiḥ।  
uttare yāmune tīre pratiṣṭāne mahāyaśāḥ ।। 29.47 ।।  
  
tasya putrā babhūvurhi ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ।  
gandharvvaloke viditā āyurddhīmānamāvasuḥ ।। 29.48 ।।  
  
viśvāyuśca śatāyuśca gatāyuścorvaśīsutāḥ।  
amāvasostu vai jāto bhīmo rājātha viśvajit ।। 29.49 ।।  
  
śrīmān bhīmasya dāyādo rājāsītkāñcanaprabhaḥ।  
vidvāṃstu kāñcanasyāpi suhotro'bhūnmahābalaḥ ।। 29.50 ।।  
  
suhotrasyābhajjahnuḥ keśikāgarbhasambhavaḥ।  
pratigatya tato gaṅgā vitato yajñakarmmaṇi ।। 29.51 ।।  
  
plāvayāmāsa taṃ deśaṃ bhāvino'rthasya darśanāt।  
gaṅgayā plāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭaṃ samantataḥ ।। 29.52 ।।  
  
sauhotrirvaradaḥ kruddho gaṅgāṃ saṃraktalocanaḥ।  
asya gaṅge'valepasya sadyaḥ phalamavāpnuhi ।। 29.53 ।।  
  
etatte viphalaṃ sarvvaṃ pītamambhaḥ karomyaham।  
rājarṣiṇā tataḥ pītāṃ gaṅgāṃ dṛṣṭvā surarṣayaḥ ।। 29.54 ।।  
  
upaninyurmahābhāgā duhitṛtvena jāhnavīm।  
yauvanāśvasya pautrīntu kāverīñjahnurāvahat ।। 29.55 ।।  
  
yuvanāśvasya śāpena gaṅgā yena vinirmame ।  
kāverīṃ saritāṃ śreṣṭāṃ jahnubhāryyāmaninditām ।। 29.56 ।।  
  
jahnuśca dayitaṃ putraṃ suhotraṃ nāma dhārmikam।  
kāveryyāṃ janayāmāsa ajakastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 29.57 ।।  
  
ajakasya tu dāyādo balākāśvo mahāyaśāḥ।  
babhūvuśca gayaḥ śīlaḥ kuśastasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 29.58 ।।  
  
kuśaputrā babhūvuśca catvāro vedavarcasaḥ।  
kuśāśvaḥ kuśanābhaśca amūrttārayaśovasuḥ ।। 29.59 ।।  
  
kuśastambastapastepe putrārthī rājasattamaḥ।  
pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai śatakratumapaśyata ।। 29.60 ।।  
  
tamugratapasaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaḥ purandaraḥ।  
samarthaḥ putrajanane svayamevāsya śāśvataḥ ।। 29.61 ।।  
  
putratvaṃ kalpayāmāsa svayameva purandaraḥ।  
gādhirnāmābhavatputraḥ kauśikaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 29.62 ।।  
  
paurukutsābhavadbhāryā gādhistasyāmajāyata।  
pūrvvaṃ kanyāṃ mahābhāgāṃ nāmnā satyavatīṃ śubhām।  
tāṃ gādhiputraḥ kāvyāya ṛcīkāya dadau prabhuḥ ।। 29.63 ।।  
  
tasyāṃ putrastu vai bharttā bhārgavo bhṛgunandanaḥ।  
putrārthe sādhayāmāsa caruṃ gādhestathaiva ca ।। 29.64 ।।  
  
tathā cāhūya sudhṛtiṛcīko bhārgavastadā।  
upayojyaścarurayaṃ tvayā mātrā ca teśubhe ।। 29.65 ।।  
  
tasyāṃ janiṣyate putro dīptimān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ।  
ajeyaḥ kṣatriyairyuddhe kṣatriyarṣabhasūdanaḥ ।। 29.66 ।।  
  
tavāpi putraṃ kalyāṇi dhṛtintaṃ tapodhanam।  
śamātmakaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ carureṣa vidhāsyati ।। 29.67 ।।  
  
evamuktvā tu tāṃ bhāryyāmṛcīko bhṛgunandanaḥ।  
tapasyābhirato nityamaraṇyaṃ praviveśa ha ।। 29.68 ।।  
  
gādhiḥ sadārastu tadā ṛcīkāśramamabhyagāt।  
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena sutāṃ draṣṭuṃ nareśvaraḥ ।। 29.69 ।।  
  
carudvayaṃ gṛhītvā tu ṛṣeḥ satyavatī sadā।  
bhartturvacanamavyagrā hṛṣṭā mātre nyavedayat ।। 29.70 ।।  
  
mātā tu tasyai daivena duhitre svaṃ caruṃ dadau ।  
tasyāścarumathājñānādātmanaḥ sā cakāra ha ।। 29.71 ।।  
  
atha satyavatī garbhaṃ kṣatriyāntakaraṃ śubham।  
dhārayāmāsa dīptena vapuṣā ghoradarśanā ।। 29.72 ।।  
  
tamṛcīkastato dṛṣṭvā yogenāpyanumṛśya ca।  
tadābravīddvijaśreṣṭhaḥ svāṃ bhāryyāṃ varavarṇinīm ।। 29.73 ।।  
  
mātuḥ siddhyati te bhadre caruvyatyāsahetunā।  
janiṣyati hi putraste krūrakarmātidāruṇaḥ ।। 29.74 ।।  
  
mātā janiṣyate vāpi tathābhūtaṃ tapodhanam ।  
viśvaṃ hi brahma tapasā mayā tatra samarpitam ।। 29.75 ।।  
  
evamuktā mahābhāgā bhartrā satyavatī tadā।  
prasādayāmāsa patiṃ suto me nedṛśo bhavet।  
brāhmaṇāpasadastvanya ityukto munirabravīt ।। 29.76 ।।  
  
naiṣa saṅkalpitaḥ kāmo mayā bhadre tathā tvayā ।  
ugrakarmā bhavet putraḥ piturmātuśca kāraṇāt ।। 29.77 ।।  
  
punaḥ satyavatī vākyamevamuktābravīdidam।  
icchaँllokānapi mune sṛjethāḥ kiṃ punaḥ sutam ।। 29.78 ।।  
  
śamātmakamṛjuṃ bharttaḥ putraṃ me dātumarhasi।  
kāmamevaṃvidhaḥ putro mama syāttu vada prabho ।। 29.79 ।।  
  
mayyanyathā na śakyaṃ vai kartumeva dvijottama।  
tataḥ prasādamakarot sa tasyāstapaso balāt ।। 29.80 ।।  
  
putre nāsti viśeṣo me pautre vā varavarṇini।  
tvayā yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ tathā bhadre bhaviṣyati ।। 29.81 ।।  
  
tasmāt satyavatī putraṃ janayāmāsa bhārgavam।  
tapasyabhiratandāntaṃ jamadagniḥ śamātmakam ।। 29.82 ।।  
  
bhṛgoścaruviparyāse raudravaiṣṇavayoḥ purā।  
yamanādvaiṣṇavasyāgnerjamadagnirajāyata ।। 29.83 ।।  
  
viśvāmitraṃ tu dāyādaṃ gādhiḥ kuśikanandanaḥ।  
prāpya brahmarṣisahito (savitā) jagāma brahmaṇāvṛtaḥ ।। 29.84 ।।  
  
sā hi satyavatī puṇyā satyavrataparāyaṇā।  
kauśikīti samākhyātā pravṛtteyaṃ mahānadī ।। 29.85 ।।  
  
parisrutā mahābhāgā kauśikī saritāṃ varā।  
ikṣvākuvaṃśe tvabhavatsuveṇurnāma pārthivaḥ ।। 29.86 ।।  
  
tasya kanyā mahābhāgā kāmalī nāma reṇukā।  
reṇu kāyāntu kāmalyāṃ tapodhṛtisamanvitaḥ।  
ārcīko janayāmāsa jamadagniḥ sudāruṇam ।। 29.87 ।।  
  
sarvavidyāntagaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanurvedasya pāragam।  
rāmaṃ kṣatriya hantāraṃ pradīptamiva pāvakam ।। 29.88 ।।  
  
aurvvasyaivamṛcīkasya satyavatyāṃ mahāmanāḥ।  
jamadagnistato vīryyājjajñe brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।  
madhyamaśca śunaḥśephaḥ śunaḥpucchaḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ ।। 29.89 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrastu dharmātmā nāmnā viśvarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
jajñe bhṛguprasādena kauśikādvaṃśavarddhanaḥ ।। 29.90 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrasya putrastu śunaḥśepho'bhavanmuniḥ।  
hariścandrasya yajñe tu paśutve niyutaḥ savai।  
devairdattaḥ sa vai yasmāddevarātastato'bhavat ।। 29.91 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrasya putrāṇāṃ śunaḥ śepho'grajaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
madhucchando nayaścaiva kṛtadevau dhruvāṣṭakau ।। 29.92 ।।  
  
kacchapaḥ pūraṇaścaiva viśvāmitrasutāstu vai।  
teṣāṃ gotrāṇi bahudhā kauśikānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 29.93 ।।  
  
pārthivā devarātāśca yājñavalkyā samarṣaṇāḥ ।  
udumbarā udumlānāstārakā yamamuñcatāḥ ।। 29.94 ।।  
  
lohiṇyo reṇavaścaiva tathā kārīṣavaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
babhravaḥ pāṇinaścaiva dhyāvajapyāstathaiva ca ।। 29.95 ।।  
  
śālāvatyā hiraṇyākṣāḥ syaṅkṛtā gālavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
devalā yāmadūtāśca śālaṅkāyanabāṣkalāḥ ।। 29.96 ।।  
  
dadāti bādarāścānye viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ।  
ṛṣyantaravivāṅyāste bahavaḥ śauśikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 29.97 ।।  
  
kauśikāsośrumāścaiva tathānye saidhavāyanāḥ।  
pauroravasya puṇyasya brahmarṣeḥ kauśikasya tu ।। 29.98 ।।  
  
dṛṣadvatīsutaścāpi viśvāmitrāttathāṣṭakaḥ।  
aṣṭakasya suto yo hi prokto jahnugaṇomayā ।। 29.99 ।।  
  
        ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
kiṃ lakṣaṇena dharmeṇa tapaseha śrutena vā।  
brāhmaṇyaṃ samanuprāptaṃ viśvāmitrādibhirnṛpaiḥ ।। 29.100 ।।  
  
yena yonābhidhā nena brāhmaṇyaṃ kṣatriyā gatāḥ ।  
viśeṣaṃ jñātumicchāmi tapasā dānatastathā ।। 29.101 ।।  
  
evamuktastato vākyamabravīdidamarthavat।  
anyāyopagatairdravyairāhṛtya yajane dhiyā।  
dharmābhikāṃkṣī yajate na dharmaphalamaśnute ।। 29.102 ।।  
  
dharmmaṃ caitaṃ samākhyāya pāpātmā puruṣādhamaḥ।  
dadāti dānaṃ viprebhyo lokānāṃ dambhakāraṇāt ।। 29.103 ।।  
  
japaṃ kṛtvā tathā tīvraṃ dhanalobhānniraṅkuśaḥ।  
rāgamohānvito hyante pāvanārthaṃ dadāti yaḥ ।। 29.104 ।।  
  
tena dattāni dānāni aphalāni bhavantyuta।  
tasya dharmmapravṛttasya hiṃsakasya durātmanaḥ ।। 29.105 ।।  
  
evaṃ labdhvā dhanaṃ mohāddadato yajataśca ha।  
sakliṣṭakarmaṇo dānaṃ na tiṣṭhati durātmanaḥ ।। 29.106 ।।  
  
nyāyāgatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ tīrthe sampratipādanam।  
kāmānanabhisandhāya yajate ca dadāti ca ।। 29.107 ।।  
  
sa dānaphalamāpnoti tacca dānaṃ sukhodayam।  
dānena bhogānāpnoti svargaṃ satyena gacchati ।। 29.108 ।।  
  
tapasā tu sutaptena lokān viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati ।  
viṣṭabhya sa tu tejasvī lokeṣvānantyamaśnute ।। 29.109 ।।  
  
dānācchreyāṃstathā yajño yajñācchreyastathā tapaḥ।  
saṃnyāsastapasaḥ śreyāṃstasmājjñānaṃ guruḥ smṛtam ।। 29.110 ।।  
  
śrṛyante hi tapaḥsiddhāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।  
viśvāmitro narapatirmāndhātā saṃkṛtiḥ kapiḥ ।। 29.111 ।।  
  
kapeśca purukutsaśca satyaścānṛhavānṛthuḥ  
ārṣṭiṣeṇo'mīḍhaśca bhāgānyonyastathaiva ca ।। 29.112 ।।  
  
kakṣīvaścaiva śijayastathānye ca mahārathāḥ।  
rathītaraśca rundaśca viṣṇuvṛddhādayo nṛpāḥ ।। 29.113 ।।  
  
kṣātropetāḥ smṛtā hyete tapasā ṛṣitāṅgatāḥ ।  
ete rājarṣayaḥ sarvve siddhiṃ sumahatīṅgatāḥ।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ayorvaṃśaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। 29.114 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte candravaṃśakīrtanaṃ nāmonatriśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 29 ।। 


---
title: 028

---
       uttarārddham - 28  
       ।।sūta uvāca ।।  
  
pitā somasya vaiviprā jajñe'trirbhagavānṛṣiḥ।  
so'ti tasthau sarvalokānbhagavāntsvena tejasā ।। 28.1 ।।  
  
karmaṇā manasā vācā śubhānyeva samācaran।  
kāṣṭhakuḍyaśilābhūta ūrddhvabāhurmahādyutiḥ ।। 28.2 ।।  
  
suduścaraṃ nāma tapo yena taptaṃ mahatpurā।  
trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi divyānīti hi naḥ śrutam ।। 28.3 ।।  
  
tasyorddhvaretasastatra sthitasyānimiṣaspṛham।  
somatvantanurāpede mahābuddhiḥ sa vai dvijaḥ ।। 28.4 ।।  
  
ūrddhvamācakrame tasya somatvaṃ bhāvitātmanaḥ।  
somaḥ susrāva netrābhyāṃ daśa vā dyotayan diśaḥ ।। 28.5 ।।  
  
taṃ garbhaṃ vidhinādiṣṭā daśa devyo dadhustadā।  
sametya dhārayāmāsurna ca tāḥ samaśaknuvan ।। 28.6 ।।  
  
sa tābhyaḥ sahasaivātha digbhyo garbhaḥ prabhānvitaḥ।  
yathāvabhāsayaṃllokāñjhītāṃśuḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ।। 28.7 ।।  
  
yadā na dhāraṇe śaktāstasya garbhasya tāḥ striyaḥ।  
tataḥ sa tābhiḥ śītāṃśurnipapāta vasundharām ।। 28.8 ।।  
  
patantaṃ somamālokya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ।  
rathamāropayāmāsa lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।। 28.9 ।।  
  
sa hi devamayo viprā dharmmārthī satyasaṅgaraḥ।  
yukto vājisahasreṇa siteneti hi naḥ śrutam ।। 28.10 ।।  
  
tasminnipatite devāḥ putre'treḥ paramātmani।  
tuṣṭuvurbrahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ mānasāḥ sapta viśrutāḥ ।। 28.11 ।।  
  
tatraivāṅgirasastasya bhṛgoścaivātmajastathā।  
ṛgbhiryajurbhirbahubhiratharvāṅgirasairapi ।। 28.12 ।।  
  
tataḥ saṃstūyamānasya tejaḥ somasya bhāsvataḥ।  
āpyāyamānaṃ lokāṃstrīn bhāvayāmāsa sarvvaśaḥ ।। 28.13 ।।  
  
samena rathamukhyena sāgarāntāṃ vasundharām।  
triḥsaptakṛtvo vipula ścakārābhipradakṣiṇam ।। 28.14 ।।  
  
tasya yaccāpi tattejaḥ pṛthivīmanvapadyata।  
oṣadhyastāḥ samudbhūtāstejasā saṃjvalantyuta ।। 28.15 ।।  
  
tābhirdhāryatyayaṃ lokān prajāścāpi caturvidhāḥ।  
poṣṭā hi bhagavān somo jagato hi dvijottamāḥ ।। 28.16 ।।  
  
sa labdhatejāstapasā saṃstavaistaiśca karmmabhiḥ।  
tapastepe mahābhāgaḥ pajhānāṃ daśatīrdaśa ।। 28.17 ।।  
  
hiraṇyavarṇā yā devyo dhārayantyātmanā jagat।  
vibhustāsāmbhavetsomaḥ prakhyātaḥ svena karmmaṇā ।। 28.18 ।।  
  
tatastasmai dadau rājyaṃ brahmā brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।  
bījauṣadhiṣu viprāṇāmapāñca dvijasattamāḥ ।। 28.19 ।।  
  
so'bhiṣikto mahātejā mahārājyena rājarāṭ ।  
lokānāṃ bhāvayāmāsa svabhāvāttapatāṃ varaḥ ।। 28.20 ।।  
  
saptaviṃśatirindostu dākṣāyaṇyo mahāvratāḥ।  
dadau prācetaso dakṣo nakṣatrāṇīti yā viduḥ ।। 28.21 ।।  
  
sa tatprāpya mahadrājayaṃ somaḥ somavatāṃ prabhuḥ।  
samājajñe rājasūyaṃ sahasraśatadakṣiṇam ।। 28.22 ।।  
  
hiraṇyagarbhaścodgātā brahmā brahmatvameyivān।  
sadasyastatra bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।  
sanatkumārapramukhairādyairbrahmarṣibhirvṛtaḥ ।। 28.23 ।।  
  
dakṣiṇāmadadatsomastrīlloँkāniti naḥ śrutam।  
tebhyo brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ sadasyebhyaśca vai dvijāḥ ।। 28.24 ।।  
  
taṃ sinī ca kuhūścaiva vapuḥ puṣṭiḥ prabhāvasuḥ।  
kīrttirdhṛtiśca lakṣmīśca nava devyaḥ siṣevire ।। 28.25 ।।  
  
prāpyāvabhṛthamavyagraḥ sarvvadevarṣipūjitaḥ।  
atirājātirājendro daśadhātāpayaddiśaḥ ।। 28.26 ।।  
  
tadā tat prāpya duṣprāpamaiśvaryamṛṣisaṃstutam।  
sa vibhramamatirviprā vinaye vinayo hataḥ ।। 28.27 ।।  
  
bṛhaspateḥ sa vai bhāryāntārāṃ nāma yaśasvinīm।  
jahāra sahasā sarvvānavamatyāṅgiraḥsutān ।। 28.28 ।।  
  
sa yācyamāno devaiśca tathā devarṣibhiśca ha।  
naiva vyasarjayattārāṃ tasmāyāṅgirase tadā ।। 28.29 ।।  
  
uśanāstasya jagrāha pārṣṇimaṅgiraso dvijāḥ।  
sa hi śiṣyo mahātejāḥ pituḥ pūrvaṃ bṛhaspateḥ ।। 28.30 ।।  
  
tena snehena bhagavān rudrastasya bṛhaspateḥ।  
pārṣṇigrāho'bhavaddevaḥ pragṛhyājagavandhanuḥ ।। 28.31 ।।  
  
tena brahmarṣimukhyebhyaḥ paramāstraṃ mahātmanā।  
uddiśya devānutsṛṣṭaṃ yenaiṣāṃ nāśitaṃ yaśaḥ ।। 28.32 ।।  
  
tatra tadyuddhamabhavat pratyakṣantārakāmayam।  
devānāṃ dānavānāñca lokakṣayakaraṃ mahat ।। 28.33 ।।  
  
tatra śiṣṭāstrayo devāstuṣitāścaiva ye smṛtāḥ।  
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmurādidevaṃ pitāmaham ।। 28.34 ।।  
  
tato nivāryośanasaṃ rudraṃ jyeṣṭhañca śaṅkaram।  
dadāvāṅgirase tārāṃ svayameva pitāmahaḥ ।। 28.35 ।।  
  
antarvatnīṃ ca tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tārāntārādhipānanām।  
garbhamutsṛjase na tvaṃ vipraḥ prāha bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 28.36 ।।  
  
madīyāyāṃ tanau yonau garbho dhāryaḥ kathañcana।  
atho nāvasṛjattantu kumāraṃ dasyuhantamam ।। 28.37 ।।  
  
īṣikāstambamāsādya jvalantamiva pāvakam।  
jātamātro'tha bhagavān devānāmākṣipadvapuḥ ।। 28.38 ।।  
  
tataḥ saṃśayamāpannāstārāmakathayan surāḥ।  
satyaṃ brūhi sutaḥ kasya somasyātha bṛhaspateḥ ।। 28.39 ।।  
  
hrīyamāṇā yadā devānnāha sā sādhvasādhu vā ।  
tadā tāṃ śaptumārabdhaḥ kumāro dasyuhantamaḥ ।। 28.40 ।।  
  
sannivārya tadā brahmā tārāṃ candrasya saṃśayaḥ।  
yadatra tathyantad‌brūhi tāre kasya sutastvayam ।। 28.41 ।।  
  
sā prāñjaliruvācedaṃ brahmāṇaṃ varadaṃ prabhum।  
somasyeti mahātmānaṃ kumārandasyuhantamam ।। 28.42 ।।  
  
tataḥ sa tamupāghāya somo dātā prajāpatiḥ।  
budha ityakaronnāma tasya putrasya dhīmataḥ ।। 28.43 ।।  
  
pratipūrvvañca gamane samabhyuttiṣṭhate budhaiḥ।  
utpādayāmāsa tadā putraṃ vai rājaputrikā ।। 28.44 ।।  
  
tasya putro mahātejā babhūvailaḥ purūravāḥ ।  
urvaśyāṃ jajñire tasya putrāḥ ṣaṭ sumahaujasaḥ ।। 28.45 ।।  
  
prasahya dharṣitastatra vivaśo rājayakṣmaṇā ।  
tato yakṣmābhibhūtastu somaḥ prakṣīṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।  
jagāma śaraṇāyātha pitaraṃ so'trimeva tu ।। 28.46 ।।  
  
tasya tatpāpaśamanaṃ cakārātrirmahāyaśāḥ।  
sa rājayakṣmaṇā muktaḥ śriyā jajvāla sarvvaśaḥ ।। 28.47 ।।  
  
etatsomasya vai janma kīrttitaṃ dvijasattamāḥ।  
vaṃśantasya dvijaśreṣṭāḥ kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ।। 28.48 ।।  
  
dhanyamārogyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ kalmaṣaśodhanam।  
somasya janma śrutvaiva sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। 28.49 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte śomotpattirnāmāṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 28 ।। 


---
title: 029

---
        sūta uvāca ।।  
  
somasya tu budhaḥ putro budhasya tu purūravāḥ।  
tejasvī dānaśīlaśca yajvā vipuladakṣiṇaḥ ।। 29.1 ।।  
  
brahmavādī parākrāntaḥ śatrubhiryudhi durjayaḥ।  
āharttā cāgnihotrasya yajvanāñca dadau mahīm ।। 29.2 ।।  
  
satyavāk karmmabuddhiśca kāntaḥ saṃvṛtamaithunaḥ।  
atīva putro lokeṣu rūpeṇāpratimo'bhavat ।। 29.3 ।।  
  
taṃ brahmavādinaṃ dāntaṃ dharmajñaṃ satyavādinam।  
urvaśī varayāmāsa hitvā mānaṃ yaśasvinī ।। 29.4 ।।  
  
tayā sahāvasadrājā daśavarṣāṇi cāṣṭa ca।  
sapta ṣaṭ sapta cāṣṭau ca daśa cāṣṭau ca vīryavān ।। 29.5 ।।  
  
vane caitrarathe ramye tathā mandākinītaṭe।  
alakāyāṃ viśālāyāṃ nandane ca vanottame ।। 29.6 ।।  
  
gandhamādanapādeṣu meruśrṛṅge nagottame।  
uttarāṃśca kurūn prāpya kalāpagrāmameva ca ।। 29.7 ।।  
  
eteṣu vanasukhyeṣu surairācariteṣu ca।  
urvaśyā sahito rājā reme paramayā mudā ।। 29.8 ।।  
  
          ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
gandharvā corvaśī devī rājānaṃ mānuṣaṃ katham।  
devānutsṛjya samprāptā tanno brūhi bahuśruta ।। 29.9 ।।  
  
      sūta uvāca।।  
brahmaśāpābhibhūtā sā mānuṣaṃ samupasthitā।  
ailaṃ tu taṃ varārohā samayena vyavasthitā ।। 29.10 ।।  
  
ātmanaḥ śāpamokṣārthaṃ niyamaṃ sā cakāra tu ।  
anagnadarśanañcaiva akāmāta saha maithunam ।। 29.11 ।।  
  
dvau meṣau śayanābhyāśe sa tāvad vyavatiṣṭhate।  
ghṛtamātraṃ tathāhāraḥ kālamekantu pārthiva ।। 29.12 ।।  
  
yadyeṣa samayo rājan yāvatkālañca te dṛḍham।  
tāvatkālantu vatsyāmi eṣa naḥ samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। 29.13 ।।  
  
tasyāstaṃ samayaṃ sarvaṃ sa rājā paryapālayat।  
evaṃ sā cāvasat tasmin purūravasi bhāminī ।। 29.14 ।।  
  
varṣāṇyatha catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ tadbhaktyā śāpamohitā।  
urvaśī mānuṣaṃ prāptā gandharvvā ścintayānvitāḥ ।। 29.15 ।।  
  
         gandharvvā ūcuḥ।  
cintayadhvaṃ mahābhāgā yathā sā tu varāṅganā।  
āgacchettu punarddevānurvaśī svargabhūṣaṇā ।। 29.16 ।।  
  
tato viśvāvasurnāma tatrāha vadatāṃ varaḥ।  
tayā tu samayastatra kriyamāṇo mato'naghaḥ ।। 29.17 ।।  
  
samayanyutkramāt sā vai rājānaṃ tyakṣyate yathā।  
tadahaṃ vacmi vaḥ sarvaṃ yathā tyakṣyati sā nṛpam ।। 29.18 ।।  
  
sahasā yogameṣyāmi yuṣmākaṃ kāryasiddhaye।  
evamuktvā gatastatra pratiṣṭānaṃ mahāyaśāḥ ।। 29.19 ।।  
  
sa niśāyāmathāgamya meṣamekaṃ jahāra vai।  
mātṛvadvarttate sā tu meṣayoścāruhāsinī ।। 29.20 ।।  
  
gandharvāgamanaṃ jñātvā śayanasthā yaśasvinī।  
rājānamabravītsā tu putro me hriyateti vai ।। 29.21 ।।  
  
evamukto viniścitya nagnastiṣṭhati vai nṛpaḥ ।  
nagnaṃ drakṣyati māṃ devī samayo vitatho bhavet ।। 29.22 ।।  
  
tato bhūyastu gandharvvā dvitīyaṃ meṣamādaduḥ।  
dvitīye'pahṛte meṣe ailaṃ devī tamabravīt ।। 29.23 ।।  
  
putrau mama hṛtau rājannanāthāyā iva prabho।  
evamuktastadotthāya nagno rājā pradhāvitaḥ ।। 29.24 ।।  
  
meṣābabhyāṃ padavīṃ rājan gandharvvairvyutthitāmatha।  
utpāditā tu mahatī māyā tadbhavanaṃ mahat ।। 29.25 ।।  
  
prakāśitantu sahasā tato nagnamavekṣya sā।  
nagnaṃ dṛṣṭvā tiro'bhūtsā apsarā kāmarūpiṇī ।। 29.26 ।।  
  
tirobhūtāntu tāṃ jñātvā gandharvāstatra tāvubhau।  
meṣau tyaktvā ca te sarve tatraivāntarhitābhavan ।। 29.27 ।।  
  
utsṛṣṭāvuraṇau dṛṣṭvā rājā gṛhyāgataḥ prabhuḥ।  
apaśyaṃstāṃ tu vai rājā vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ ।। 29.28 ।।  
  
cacāra pṛthivīṃ caiva mārgamāṇastatastataḥ।  
athāpaśyacca tāṃ rājā kurukṣetre mahābalaḥ ।। 29.29 ।।  
  
plakṣatīrthe puṣkariṇyāṃ vigāḍhenāmbunāplutām।  
krīḍantīmapsarobhiśca pañcabhiḥ saha śobhanām ।। 29.30 ।।  
  
apaśyatsā tataḥ subhrū rājānamavidūrataḥ।  
urvaśī tāḥ sakhīḥ prāha ayaṃ sa puruṣottamaḥ ।। 29.31 ।।  
  
yasminnahamavātsaṃ hi darśayāmāsa taṃ nṛpam ।  
tata āvirbabhūvustāḥ pañcacūḍāpsarāstu tāḥ ।। 29.32 ।।  
  
dṛṣṭvā tu rājā tāṃ prītaḥ pralāpān kurute bahūn।  
āyāhi tiṣṭha manasā ghore vacasi tiṣṭha he ।। 29.33 ।।  
  
evamādīni sūkṣmāṇi parasparamabhāṣata।  
urvvaśī tvabravīccailaṃ sagarbhāhaṃ tvayā prabho ।। 29.34 ।।  
  
saṃvatsarāt kumāraste bhavitā nava saṃśayaḥ।  
niśāmekāntu vai rājā hyavasattu tayā saha ।। 29.35 ।।  
  
samprahṛṣṭo jagāmātha svapurantu mahāyaśāḥ।  
gate saṃvatsare rājā urvvaśīṃ punarāgamat ।। 29.36 ।।  
  
uṣitvā tu tayā sārddhamekarātraṃ mahāmanāḥ।  
kāmārttaścā bravīddīno bhava nityaṃ mameti vai ।। 29.37 ।।  
  
urvvaśyathābravīccailaṃ gandharvāste varaṃ daduḥ।  
taṃ vṛṇīṣva mahārāja brūhi caitāṃstvameva hi ।। 29.38 ।।  
  
vṛṇe nityaṃ hi sālokyaṃ gandharvāṇāṃ mahātmanām।  
tathetyuktvā varaṃ vavre gandharvāśca tathāstviti ।। 29.39 ।।  
  
sthālīmagneḥ pūrayitvā gandharvvāśca tamabruvan।  
anena iṣṭvā lokantaṃ prāpsyasi tvaṃ narādhipa ।। 29.40 ।।  
  
tamādāya kumārantu nagarāyopacakrame।  
niḥkṣipya tamaraṇyāñca sa putrantu gṛhaṃ yayau ।। 29.41 ।।  
  
punarādāya dṛśyāgnimaśvatthaṃ tatra dṛṣṭavān।  
samīpatastu taṃ dṛṣṭvā hyaśvatthaṃ tatra vismitaḥ ।। 29.42 ।।  
  
gandharvvebhyastathākhyātumagninā gāṃ gatastu saḥ ।  
śrutvā tamarthamaśilamaraṇiṃ tu samādiśat ।। 29.43 ।।  
  
aśvatthādaraṇiṃ kṛtvā mathitvāgniṃ yathāvidhi।  
teneṣṭvā tu salokaṃ naḥ prāpsyasi tvaṃ narādhipa।  
mathitvāgniṃ tridhā kṛtvā hyayajatsa narādhipaḥ ।। 29.44 ।।  
  
iṣṭvā yajñairbahuvidhairgatasteṣāṃ salokatām।  
vāsāya ca sa gandharvvastretāyāṃ sa mahārathaḥ।  
eko'gniḥ pūrvamāsīdvai ailastrīṃstānakalpayat ।। 29.45 ।।  
  
evaṃprabhāvo rājāsīdailastu dvijasattamāḥ।  
deśe puṇyatame caiva maharṣibhiralaṃkṛte ।। 29.46 ।।  
  
rājyaṃ sa kārayāmāsa prayāge pṛthivī patiḥ।  
uttare yāmune tīre pratiṣṭāne mahāyaśāḥ ।। 29.47 ।।  
  
tasya putrā babhūvurhi ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ।  
gandharvvaloke viditā āyurddhīmānamāvasuḥ ।। 29.48 ।।  
  
viśvāyuśca śatāyuśca gatāyuścorvaśīsutāḥ।  
amāvasostu vai jāto bhīmo rājātha viśvajit ।। 29.49 ।।  
  
śrīmān bhīmasya dāyādo rājāsītkāñcanaprabhaḥ।  
vidvāṃstu kāñcanasyāpi suhotro'bhūnmahābalaḥ ।। 29.50 ।।  
  
suhotrasyābhajjahnuḥ keśikāgarbhasambhavaḥ।  
pratigatya tato gaṅgā vitato yajñakarmmaṇi ।। 29.51 ।।  
  
plāvayāmāsa taṃ deśaṃ bhāvino'rthasya darśanāt।  
gaṅgayā plāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñavāṭaṃ samantataḥ ।। 29.52 ।।  
  
sauhotrirvaradaḥ kruddho gaṅgāṃ saṃraktalocanaḥ।  
asya gaṅge'valepasya sadyaḥ phalamavāpnuhi ।। 29.53 ।।  
  
etatte viphalaṃ sarvvaṃ pītamambhaḥ karomyaham।  
rājarṣiṇā tataḥ pītāṃ gaṅgāṃ dṛṣṭvā surarṣayaḥ ।। 29.54 ।।  
  
upaninyurmahābhāgā duhitṛtvena jāhnavīm।  
yauvanāśvasya pautrīntu kāverīñjahnurāvahat ।। 29.55 ।।  
  
yuvanāśvasya śāpena gaṅgā yena vinirmame ।  
kāverīṃ saritāṃ śreṣṭāṃ jahnubhāryyāmaninditām ।। 29.56 ।।  
  
jahnuśca dayitaṃ putraṃ suhotraṃ nāma dhārmikam।  
kāveryyāṃ janayāmāsa ajakastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 29.57 ।।  
  
ajakasya tu dāyādo balākāśvo mahāyaśāḥ।  
babhūvuśca gayaḥ śīlaḥ kuśastasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 29.58 ।।  
  
kuśaputrā babhūvuśca catvāro vedavarcasaḥ।  
kuśāśvaḥ kuśanābhaśca amūrttārayaśovasuḥ ।। 29.59 ।।  
  
kuśastambastapastepe putrārthī rājasattamaḥ।  
pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai śatakratumapaśyata ।। 29.60 ।।  
  
tamugratapasaṃ dṛṣṭvā sahasrākṣaḥ purandaraḥ।  
samarthaḥ putrajanane svayamevāsya śāśvataḥ ।। 29.61 ।।  
  
putratvaṃ kalpayāmāsa svayameva purandaraḥ।  
gādhirnāmābhavatputraḥ kauśikaḥ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 29.62 ।।  
  
paurukutsābhavadbhāryā gādhistasyāmajāyata।  
pūrvvaṃ kanyāṃ mahābhāgāṃ nāmnā satyavatīṃ śubhām।  
tāṃ gādhiputraḥ kāvyāya ṛcīkāya dadau prabhuḥ ।। 29.63 ।।  
  
tasyāṃ putrastu vai bharttā bhārgavo bhṛgunandanaḥ।  
putrārthe sādhayāmāsa caruṃ gādhestathaiva ca ।। 29.64 ।।  
  
tathā cāhūya sudhṛtiṛcīko bhārgavastadā।  
upayojyaścarurayaṃ tvayā mātrā ca teśubhe ।। 29.65 ।।  
  
tasyāṃ janiṣyate putro dīptimān kṣatriyarṣabhaḥ।  
ajeyaḥ kṣatriyairyuddhe kṣatriyarṣabhasūdanaḥ ।। 29.66 ।।  
  
tavāpi putraṃ kalyāṇi dhṛtintaṃ tapodhanam।  
śamātmakaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ carureṣa vidhāsyati ।। 29.67 ।।  
  
evamuktvā tu tāṃ bhāryyāmṛcīko bhṛgunandanaḥ।  
tapasyābhirato nityamaraṇyaṃ praviveśa ha ।। 29.68 ।।  
  
gādhiḥ sadārastu tadā ṛcīkāśramamabhyagāt।  
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena sutāṃ draṣṭuṃ nareśvaraḥ ।। 29.69 ।।  
  
carudvayaṃ gṛhītvā tu ṛṣeḥ satyavatī sadā।  
bhartturvacanamavyagrā hṛṣṭā mātre nyavedayat ।। 29.70 ।।  
  
mātā tu tasyai daivena duhitre svaṃ caruṃ dadau ।  
tasyāścarumathājñānādātmanaḥ sā cakāra ha ।। 29.71 ।।  
  
atha satyavatī garbhaṃ kṣatriyāntakaraṃ śubham।  
dhārayāmāsa dīptena vapuṣā ghoradarśanā ।। 29.72 ।।  
  
tamṛcīkastato dṛṣṭvā yogenāpyanumṛśya ca।  
tadābravīddvijaśreṣṭhaḥ svāṃ bhāryyāṃ varavarṇinīm ।। 29.73 ।।  
  
mātuḥ siddhyati te bhadre caruvyatyāsahetunā।  
janiṣyati hi putraste krūrakarmātidāruṇaḥ ।। 29.74 ।।  
  
mātā janiṣyate vāpi tathābhūtaṃ tapodhanam ।  
viśvaṃ hi brahma tapasā mayā tatra samarpitam ।। 29.75 ।।  
  
evamuktā mahābhāgā bhartrā satyavatī tadā।  
prasādayāmāsa patiṃ suto me nedṛśo bhavet।  
brāhmaṇāpasadastvanya ityukto munirabravīt ।। 29.76 ।।  
  
naiṣa saṅkalpitaḥ kāmo mayā bhadre tathā tvayā ।  
ugrakarmā bhavet putraḥ piturmātuśca kāraṇāt ।। 29.77 ।।  
  
punaḥ satyavatī vākyamevamuktābravīdidam।  
icchaँllokānapi mune sṛjethāḥ kiṃ punaḥ sutam ।। 29.78 ।।  
  
śamātmakamṛjuṃ bharttaḥ putraṃ me dātumarhasi।  
kāmamevaṃvidhaḥ putro mama syāttu vada prabho ।। 29.79 ।।  
  
mayyanyathā na śakyaṃ vai kartumeva dvijottama।  
tataḥ prasādamakarot sa tasyāstapaso balāt ।। 29.80 ।।  
  
putre nāsti viśeṣo me pautre vā varavarṇini।  
tvayā yathoktaṃ vacanaṃ tathā bhadre bhaviṣyati ।। 29.81 ।।  
  
tasmāt satyavatī putraṃ janayāmāsa bhārgavam।  
tapasyabhiratandāntaṃ jamadagniḥ śamātmakam ।। 29.82 ।।  
  
bhṛgoścaruviparyāse raudravaiṣṇavayoḥ purā।  
yamanādvaiṣṇavasyāgnerjamadagnirajāyata ।। 29.83 ।।  
  
viśvāmitraṃ tu dāyādaṃ gādhiḥ kuśikanandanaḥ।  
prāpya brahmarṣisahito (savitā) jagāma brahmaṇāvṛtaḥ ।। 29.84 ।।  
  
sā hi satyavatī puṇyā satyavrataparāyaṇā।  
kauśikīti samākhyātā pravṛtteyaṃ mahānadī ।। 29.85 ।।  
  
parisrutā mahābhāgā kauśikī saritāṃ varā।  
ikṣvākuvaṃśe tvabhavatsuveṇurnāma pārthivaḥ ।। 29.86 ।।  
  
tasya kanyā mahābhāgā kāmalī nāma reṇukā।  
reṇu kāyāntu kāmalyāṃ tapodhṛtisamanvitaḥ।  
ārcīko janayāmāsa jamadagniḥ sudāruṇam ।। 29.87 ।।  
  
sarvavidyāntagaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanurvedasya pāragam।  
rāmaṃ kṣatriya hantāraṃ pradīptamiva pāvakam ।। 29.88 ।।  
  
aurvvasyaivamṛcīkasya satyavatyāṃ mahāmanāḥ।  
jamadagnistato vīryyājjajñe brahmavidāṃ varaḥ।  
madhyamaśca śunaḥśephaḥ śunaḥpucchaḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ ।। 29.89 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrastu dharmātmā nāmnā viśvarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
jajñe bhṛguprasādena kauśikādvaṃśavarddhanaḥ ।। 29.90 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrasya putrastu śunaḥśepho'bhavanmuniḥ।  
hariścandrasya yajñe tu paśutve niyutaḥ savai।  
devairdattaḥ sa vai yasmāddevarātastato'bhavat ।। 29.91 ।।  
  
viśvāmitrasya putrāṇāṃ śunaḥ śepho'grajaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
madhucchando nayaścaiva kṛtadevau dhruvāṣṭakau ।। 29.92 ।।  
  
kacchapaḥ pūraṇaścaiva viśvāmitrasutāstu vai।  
teṣāṃ gotrāṇi bahudhā kauśikānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 29.93 ।।  
  
pārthivā devarātāśca yājñavalkyā samarṣaṇāḥ ।  
udumbarā udumlānāstārakā yamamuñcatāḥ ।। 29.94 ।।  
  
lohiṇyo reṇavaścaiva tathā kārīṣavaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
babhravaḥ pāṇinaścaiva dhyāvajapyāstathaiva ca ।। 29.95 ।।  
  
śālāvatyā hiraṇyākṣāḥ syaṅkṛtā gālavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
devalā yāmadūtāśca śālaṅkāyanabāṣkalāḥ ।। 29.96 ।।  
  
dadāti bādarāścānye viśvāmitrasya dhīmataḥ।  
ṛṣyantaravivāṅyāste bahavaḥ śauśikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 29.97 ।।  
  
kauśikāsośrumāścaiva tathānye saidhavāyanāḥ।  
pauroravasya puṇyasya brahmarṣeḥ kauśikasya tu ।। 29.98 ।।  
  
dṛṣadvatīsutaścāpi viśvāmitrāttathāṣṭakaḥ।  
aṣṭakasya suto yo hi prokto jahnugaṇomayā ।। 29.99 ।।  
  
        ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
kiṃ lakṣaṇena dharmeṇa tapaseha śrutena vā।  
brāhmaṇyaṃ samanuprāptaṃ viśvāmitrādibhirnṛpaiḥ ।। 29.100 ।।  
  
yena yonābhidhā nena brāhmaṇyaṃ kṣatriyā gatāḥ ।  
viśeṣaṃ jñātumicchāmi tapasā dānatastathā ।। 29.101 ।।  
  
evamuktastato vākyamabravīdidamarthavat।  
anyāyopagatairdravyairāhṛtya yajane dhiyā।  
dharmābhikāṃkṣī yajate na dharmaphalamaśnute ।। 29.102 ।।  
  
dharmmaṃ caitaṃ samākhyāya pāpātmā puruṣādhamaḥ।  
dadāti dānaṃ viprebhyo lokānāṃ dambhakāraṇāt ।। 29.103 ।।  
  
japaṃ kṛtvā tathā tīvraṃ dhanalobhānniraṅkuśaḥ।  
rāgamohānvito hyante pāvanārthaṃ dadāti yaḥ ।। 29.104 ।।  
  
tena dattāni dānāni aphalāni bhavantyuta।
