tasya dharmmapravṛttasya hiṃsakasya durātmanaḥ ।। 29.105 ।।  
  
evaṃ labdhvā dhanaṃ mohāddadato yajataśca ha।  
sakliṣṭakarmaṇo dānaṃ na tiṣṭhati durātmanaḥ ।। 29.106 ।।  
  
nyāyāgatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ tīrthe sampratipādanam।  
kāmānanabhisandhāya yajate ca dadāti ca ।। 29.107 ।।  
  
sa dānaphalamāpnoti tacca dānaṃ sukhodayam।  
dānena bhogānāpnoti svargaṃ satyena gacchati ।। 29.108 ।।  
  
tapasā tu sutaptena lokān viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhati ।  
viṣṭabhya sa tu tejasvī lokeṣvānantyamaśnute ।। 29.109 ।।  
  
dānācchreyāṃstathā yajño yajñācchreyastathā tapaḥ।  
saṃnyāsastapasaḥ śreyāṃstasmājjñānaṃ guruḥ smṛtam ।। 29.110 ।।  
  
śrṛyante hi tapaḥsiddhāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।  
viśvāmitro narapatirmāndhātā saṃkṛtiḥ kapiḥ ।। 29.111 ।।  
  
kapeśca purukutsaśca satyaścānṛhavānṛthuḥ  
ārṣṭiṣeṇo'mīḍhaśca bhāgānyonyastathaiva ca ।। 29.112 ।।  
  
kakṣīvaścaiva śijayastathānye ca mahārathāḥ।  
rathītaraśca rundaśca viṣṇuvṛddhādayo nṛpāḥ ।। 29.113 ।।  
  
kṣātropetāḥ smṛtā hyete tapasā ṛṣitāṅgatāḥ ।  
ete rājarṣayaḥ sarvve siddhiṃ sumahatīṅgatāḥ।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ayorvaṃśaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।। 29.114 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte candravaṃśakīrtanaṃ nāmonatriśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 29 ।। 


---
title: 030

---
           sūta uvāca।।  
ete putrā mahātmānaḥ pañcaivāsan mahābalāḥ।  
svarbhānutanayā viprāḥ prabhāyāṃ jajñire nṛpāḥ ।। 30.1 ।।  
  
nahuṣaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ putradharmmā tataḥ smṛtaḥ।  
dharmmavṛddhātmajaścaiva sutahotro mahāyaśāḥ ।। 30.2 ।।  
  
sutahotrasya dāyādāstrayaḥ paramadhārmmikāḥ।  
kāśaḥ śalaśca dvāvetau tathā gṛtsamadaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 30.3 ।।  
  
putro gṛtsamadasyāpi śunako yasya śaunakaḥ।  
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva vaiśyāḥ śūdrāstathaiva ca ।। 30.4 ।।  
  
etasya vaṃśe sambhūtā vicitraiḥ karmmabhirdvijāḥ।  
śalātmajo hyārṣṭiṣeṇaścarantastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 30.5 ।।  
  
śaunakāścārṣṭiṣeṇāśca kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।  
kāśasya kāśayo rāṣṭaḥ putro dīrghatapāstathā ।। 30.6 ।।  
  
dharmmaśca dīrghatapaso vidvān dhanvantaristataḥ।  
tapasā sumahātejā jāto vṛddhasya dhīmataḥ।  
athainamṛṣayaḥ procuḥ sūtaṃ vākyamimaṃ punaḥ ।। 30.7 ।।  
  
       ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
kathaṃ dhanvantarirddevo mānuṣeṣviha jajñivān।  
etadveditumicchāmastato brūhi priyaṃ tathā ।। 30.8 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
dhanvantareḥ sambhavo'yaṃ śrūyatāmiha vai dvijāḥ।  
sa sambhūtaḥ samudrānte mathyamāne'mṛte purā ।। 30.9 ।।  
  
utpannaḥ sakalāt pūrvvaṃ sarvvataśca śriyāvṛtaḥ।  
sarvvasaṃsiddhakāyaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣṭambhitaḥ sthitaḥ।  
ajastvamiti hovāca tasmādajastu saḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 30.10 ।।  
  
ajaḥ provāca viṣṇuṃ taṃ tanayo'smi tava prabho।  
vidhatsva bhāgaṃ sthānañca mama loke surottama ।। 30.11 ।।  
  
evamuktaḥ sudṛṣṭvā tu tathā provāca sa prabhuḥ ।  
kṛto yajñavibhāgastu yajñiyaurhe suraistathā ।। 30.12 ।।  
  
vedeṣu vidhiyuktañca vidhihotraṃ maharṣibhiḥ।  
na śakyamiha homo vai tulyaṃ karttuṃ kadācana ।। 30.13 ।।  
  
arvāksuto'si he deva nāmamantro'si vai prabho।  
dvitīyāyāntu sambhūtyāṃ loke khyātiṅgamiṣyasi ।। 30.14 ।।  
  
aṇimādiyutā siddhirgarbhasthasya bhaviṣyati।  
tenaiva ca śarīreṇa devatvaṃ prāpsyasi prabho।  
cārumantrairghṛtairgandhairyakṣyanti tvāṃ dvijātayaḥ ।। 30.15 ।।  
  
atha ca tvaṃ punaścaiva āyurvedaṃ vidhāsyasi।  
avaśyambhāvī hyartho'yaṃ prāgdiṣṭastvabjayoninā ।। 30.16 ।।  
  
dvitīyaṃ dvāparaṃ prāpya bhavitā tvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ।  
tasmāt tasmai varaṃ dattvā viṣṇurantardaghe tataḥ ।। 30.17 ।।  
  
dvitīye dvāpare prāpte saunahotraḥ sa kāśirāṭ।  
putrakāma stapastepe nṛpo dīrghatapāstathā ।। 30.18 ।।  
  
ajaṃ devantu putrārthe hyārirādhayiṣurnṛpaḥ।  
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa prīto dhanvantarirnṛpam ।। 30.19 ।।  
  
        nṛpa uvāca।।  
bhagavan yadi tuṣṭastvaṃ putro me dhṛtimān bhava।  
tatheti samanujñāya tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 30.20 ।।  
  
tasya gehe samutpanno devo dhanvantaristadā।  
kāśirājo mahārājaḥ sarvvarogapraṇāśanaḥ ।। 30.21 ।।  
  
āyurvedaṃ bharadvājaścakāra sabhiṣakkriyam।  
tamaṣṭadhā punarvyasya śiṣyebhyaḥ pratyapādayat ।। 30.22 ।।  
  
dhanvantarisutaścāpi ketumāniti viśrutaḥ।  
atha ketumataḥ putro vibho bhīmaratho nṛpaḥ।  
divodāsa iti khyāto vārāṇasyadhipo'bhavat ।। 30.23 ।।  
  
etasminneva kāle tu purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ purā।  
śūnyāṃ viveśayāmāsa kṣeṇako nāma rākṣasaḥ ।। 30.24 ।।  
  
śaptā hi sā purī pūrvvaṃ nikumbhena mahātmanā।  
śūnyā varṣasahasraṃ vai bhavitrīti punaḥ punaḥ ।। 30.25 ।।  
  
tasyāntu śaptamātrāyāṃ divodāsaḥ prajeśvaraḥ।  
viṣayānte purīṃ ramyāṃ gomatyāṃ sannyaveśayat ।। 30.26 ।।  
  
          ṛṣa ūcuḥ।।  
vārāṇasīṃ kimarthantāṃ nikumbhaḥ śaptavān purā।  
nikumbhaścāpi dharmmātmā siddhakṣetraṃ śaśāpa yaḥ ।। 30.27 ।।  
  
             sūta uvāca।।  
divodāsastu rājarṣirnagarīṃ prāpya pārthivaḥ।  
vasate sa mahātejāḥ sphītāyāṃ vai narādhipaḥ ।। 30.28 ।।  
  
etasminneva kāle tu kṛtadāro maheśvaraḥ।  
devyāḥ sa priyakāmastu vasānaśca surāntike ।। 30.29 ।।  
  
devājñayā pāriṣadā viśvarūpāstapodhanāḥ।  
pūrvoktai rūpaviśeṣastoṣayanti maheśvarīm ।। 30.30 ।।  
  
hṛṣyati tairmahādevo menā naiva tu hṛṣyati।  
jugupsate sā nityañca devaṃ devīṃ tathaiva ca ।। 30.31 ।।  
  
mama pārśve tvanācārastava bharttā maheśvaraḥ।  
daridraḥ sarva eveha akliṣṭaṃ laḍate'naghe ।। 30.32 ।।  
  
mātrā tathoktā vacasā strīsvabāvānnacākṣamat।  
smitaṃ kṛtvā tu varadā harapārśvamathāgamat ।। 30.33 ।।  
  
viṣaṇṇavadanā devī mahādevamabhāṣata।  
neha vatsyāmyahaṃ deva naya māṃ svaṃ niveśanam ।। 30.34 ।।  
  
tathoktastu mahādevaḥ sarvāṃllokānavekṣya ha।  
vāsārthaṃ rocayāmāsa pṛthivyāṃ tu dvijottamāḥ।  
vārāṇasīṃ mahātejāḥ siddhakṣetraṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। 30.35 ।।  
  
divo dāsena tāṃ jñātvā niviṣṭānnagarīṃ bhavaḥ।  
pārśvāsthaṃ sa samāhūya gaṇeśaṃ kṣemakaṃ bravīt ।। 30.36 ।।  
  
gaṇeśvara purīṅgatvā sūnyāṃ vārāṇasīṃ kuru।  
mṛdunā cābyupāyena ativīryaḥ sa pārthivaḥ ।। 30.37 ।।  
  
tato gatvā nikumbhastu purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ purā ।  
svapne sandarśayāmāsa maṅkanaṃ nāma nāpitam ।। 30.38 ।।  
  
śreyaste'haṃ kariṣyāmi sthānaṃ me rocayānagha।  
madrūpāṃ pratimāṃ kṛtvā nagaryyante niveśaya ।। 30.39 ।।  
  
tathā svapne yathā dṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ kāritavān dvijāḥ।  
nagarīdvāryanujñāpya rājānantu yathāvidhi ।। 30.40 ।।  
  
pūjā tu mahatī caiva nityameva prayujyate।  
gandhairdhūpaiśca mālyaiśca prekṣaṇīyaistathaiva ca ।। 30.41 ।।  
  
annapradānayuktaiśca atyadbhutamivābhavat।  
evaṃ sampūjyate tatra nityameva gaṇeśvaraḥ ।। 30.42 ।।  
  
tato varasahasrāṇi nagarāṇāṃ prayacchati ।  
putrān hiraṇyamāyūṃṣi sarvvakāmāṃstathaiva ca ।। 30.43 ।।  
  
rājñastu mahiṣī śreṣṭā suyaśā nāma viśrutā।  
putrārthamāgatā sādhvī rājñā devī pracoditā ।। 30.44 ।।  
  
pūjāntu vipulāṃ kṛtvā devī putrānayācata।  
punaḥ punarathāgamya bahuśaḥ putrakāraṇāt ।। 30.45 ।।  
  
na prayacchati putrāṃstu nikumbhaḥ kāraṇena tu।  
rājā yadi tat krudhyeta tataḥ kiñcit pravarttate ।। 30.46 ।।  
  
atha dīrgheṇa kālena krodho rājānamāviśat।  
bhūtaṃ tvidaṃ mahādvāri nagarāṇāṃ prayacchati ।। 30.47 ।।  
  
prītyā varāṃśca śataśo na kiñcittu pravarttate।  
māmakaiḥ pūjyate nityaṃ nagaryāṃ mama caiva tu ।। 30.48 ।।  
  
tatrārccitaśca bahuśo devyā me tatra kāraṇāt ।  
na dadāti ca putraṃ me kṛtaghno bahubhojanaḥ ।। 30.49 ।।  
  
ato nārhati pūjāntu matsakāśāt kathañcana।  
tasmāttu nāśayiṣyāmi tasya sthānaṃ durātmanaḥ ।। 30.50 ।।  
  
evaṃ tu saviniścitya durātmā rāja kilbiṣī।  
sthānaṃ gaṇapatestasya nāśayāmāsa durmatiḥ ।। 30.51 ।।  
  
bhagnamāyatanaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājānamagamat prabhuḥ।  
yasmādṛte'parādhaṃ me tvayā sthānaṃ vinā śitam ।। 30.52 ।।  
  
akasmāt tu purī śūnyā bhavitrī te narādhipa।  
tatastena tu śāpena śūnyā vārāṇasī tathā ।। 30.53 ।।  
  
śaptāṃ purīṃ nikumbhastu mahādevamathānayat।  
śūnyāṃ purīṃ mahādevo nirmmame paramātmanā ।। 30.54 ।।  
  
tulyāṃ devavibhūtyāstu devyāścaiva mahātmanaḥ।  
ramate tatra vai devī ramamāṇe maheśvaraḥ ।। 30.55 ।।  
  
na ratiṃ tatra vai devī labhate gṛhavismayāt।  
devyāḥ krīḍārthamīśāno devo vākyamathābravīt ।। 30.56 ।।  
  
nāhaṃ veśma vimokṣyāmi avimuktaṃ hi me gṛham।  
prahasyaināmathovāca avimuktaṃ hi me gṛham ।। 30.57 ।।  
  
nāhaṃ devi gamiṣyāmi gacchasveha ramāmyaham।  
tasmāttadavimuktaṃ hi proktaṃ devena vai svayam ।। 30.58 ।।  
  
evaṃ vārāṇasī śaptā avimuktaṃ ca kīrttitam।  
yasmin vasati vai devaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ।  
yugeṣu triṣu dharmātmā saha devyā maheśvaraḥ ।। 30.59 ।।  
  
antarddhānaṃ kalau yāti tatpurantu mahātmanaḥ।  
antarhite pure tasmin purī sā vasate punaḥ ।। 30.60 ।।  
  
evaṃ vārāṇasī śaptā niveśaṃ punarāgatā।  
bhadraśreṇyasya putrāṇāṃ śatamuttamadhanvinām ।। 30.61 ।।  
  
hatvā niveśayāmāsa divodāso narādhipaḥ।  
bhadraśreṇyasya rājyantu hṛtantena balīyasā ।। 30.62 ।।  
  
bhadraśreṇyasya putrastu durdamo nāma nāmataḥ।  
divodāsena bāleti ghṛṇayā sa vivarjitaḥ ।। 30.63 ।।  
  
divodāsādṝṣadvatyāṃ vīro jajñe pratarddanaḥ।  
tena putreṇa bālena prahṛtaṃ tasya vai punaḥ ।। 30.64 ।।  
  
vairasyāntaṃ mahārājñā tadā tena vidhatsatā।  
pratarddanasya putrau dvau vatso gargaśca viśrutaḥ ।। 30.65 ।।  
  
vatsaputro hyalarkastu sannatistasya cātmajaḥ ।  
alarkaṃ prati rājarṣirgītaślokau purātanau ।। 30.66 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭivarṣaśatāni ca।  
yuvā rūpeṇa sampanno hyalarkaḥ kāśisattamaḥ ।। 30.67 ।।  
  
lopāmudrā prasādena paramāyuravāptavān ।। 30.68 ।।  
  
śāpasyānte mahābāhurhatvā kṣemakarākṣasam।  
ramyāmāvāsayāmāsa purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ nṛpaḥ ।। 30.69 ।।  
  
sannaterapi dāyādaḥ sunītho nāma dhārmikaḥ।  
sunīthasya tu dāyādaḥ suketurnāma dhārmmikaḥ ।। 30.70 ।।  
  
suketutanayaścāpi dharmaketuriti śrutiḥ।  
dharmaketostu dāyādaḥ satyaketurmahārathaḥ ।। 30.71 ।।  
  
satyaketusutaścāpi vibhurnāma prajeśvaraḥ।  
suvibhustu vibhoḥ putraḥ sukumārastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 30.72 ।।  
  
sukumārasya putrastu dhṛṣṭaketuḥ sa dhārmmikaḥ।  
dhuṣṭaketostu dāyādo veṇuhotraḥ prajeśvaraḥ ।। 30.73 ।।  
  
veṇuhotrasutaścāpi gārgyo vai nāma viśrutaḥ।  
gārgyasya gargabhūmistu vātsyo vatsasya dhīmataḥ ।। 30.74 ।।  
  
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva tayoḥ putrāḥ sudhārmmikāḥ।  
vikrāntā balavantaśca siṃhatulyaparākramāḥ ।। 30.75 ।।  
  
ityete kāśyapāḥ proktā rajerapi nibodhata।  
rajeḥ putraśatānyāsan pañca vīryavato bhuvi।  
rājeyamiti vikhyātaṃ kṣatramindrabhayāvaham ।। 30.76 ।।  
  
tadā daivāsure yuddhe samutpanne sudāruṇe।  
devāścaivāsurāścaiva pitāmahamathābruvan ।। 30.77 ।।  
  
āvayorbhagavān yuddhe vijetā ko bhaviṣyati।  
brūhi naḥ sarvvalokeśa śrotumicchāmahe vayam ।। 30.78 ।।  
  
       brahmovāca।।  
yeṣāmarthāya saṃgrāme rajirāttāyudhaḥ prabhuḥ।  
yotsyate te vijeṣyanti trīlloँkānnātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 30.79 ।।  
  
rajiryatastato lakṣmīryato lakṣmīstato dhṛtiḥ।  
yato dhṛtistato dharmo yato dharmastato jayaḥ ।। 30.80 ।।  
  
taddevā dānavāḥ sarve tataḥ śrutvā rajerjayam।  
abhyayurjayamicchantaḥ stuvanto rājasattamam ।। 30.81 ।।  
  
te hṛṣṭamanasaḥ śarve rājānaṃ devadānavāḥ।  
ūcurasmajjayāya tvaṃ gṛhāṇa varakārmukam ।। 30.82 ।।  
  
       rajiruvāca।।  
ahañjeṣyāmi no yuddhe devān śakrapurogamān।  
indro bhavāmi dharmātmā tato yotsyāmi saṃyuge ।। 30.83 ।।  
  
         dānavā ūcuḥ।।  
asmākamindraḥ prahlādastasyārthe vijayāmahe।  
asmistu samaye rājaṃstiṣṭethādeva no'diteḥ ।। 30.84 ।।  
  
sa tatheti bruvanneva devairapyabhicoditaḥ।  
bhaviṣyasīndro jitveti devairapi nimantritaḥ ।। 30.85 ।।  
  
jaghāna dānavān sarvvān samakṣaṃ vajrapāṇinaḥ।  
sa vipranaṣṭāṃ devānāṃ paramaśrīḥ śriyaṃ vaśī ।। 30.86 ।।  
  
nihatya dānavān sarvvān vyājahāra rajiḥ prabhuḥ।  
taṃ tathā tu rajhiṃ tatra devaissaha śatakratuḥ ।। 30.87 ।।  
  
rajiputro'hamityuktvā punarevābravīdvacaḥ।  
īndro'si rājan devānāṃ sarveṣānnātra saṃśayaḥ।  
yasyāhamindraputraste khyātiṃ yāsyāmi śatruhan ।। 30.88 ।।  
  
sa tu śakravacaḥ śrutvā vañcitastena māyayā।  
tathetyevābravīdrājā prīyamāṇaḥ śatakratum ।। 30.89 ।।  
  
tasmiṃstu devasadṛśe divaṃ prāpte mahīpatau।  
dāyādyamindrādājahrurācāraṃ tanayā rajeḥ ।। 30.90 ।।  
  
tāni putraśatānyasya tacca sthānaṃ śacīpateḥ।  
samakrāmanta bahudhā svargalokaṃ triviṣṭapam ।। 30.91 ।।  
  
tataḥ kāle bahutithe satīte mahābalaḥ।  
hṛtarājyo'bravīcchakro hṛtabhāgo bṛhaspatim ।। 30.92 ।।  
  
badarīphalamātraṃ vai puroḍāśaṃ vidhatsva me।  
brahmarṣe yena tiṣṭeyaṃ tejasāpyāyitastataḥ ।। 30.93 ।।  
  
brahman kṛśo'yaṃ vimanā hṛtarājyo hṛtāśanaḥ।  
hataujā durbalo mūḍho rajiputraiḥ prasīda me ।। 30.94 ।।  
  
        bṛhaspatiruvāca।।  
yadyevaṃ coditaḥ śakra tvayā syāṃ pūrvvameva hi।  
nābhaviṣyat tvatpriyārthaṃ nākarttavyaṃ mamānagha ।। 30.95 ।।  
  
prayatiṣyāmi devendra taddhitārthaṃ mahādyute।  
yathā bhāgañca rājyañca acirāt pratipatsyase ।। 30.96 ।।  
  
tathā śakra gamiṣyāmi mābhūtte viklavaṃ manaḥ।  
tataḥ karmma cakārāsya tejaḥsaṃvarddhanaṃ mahat ।। 30.97 ।।  
  
teṣāñca buddhisaṃmohamakarodbuddhisattamaḥ।  
te yadā sasutā mūḍhā rāgotpanna vidharmmiṇaḥ ।। 30.98 ।।  
  
brahmadviṣaśca saṃvṛttā hatavīryyaparākramāḥ।  
tato lebhe suraiśvaryamaindrasthānaṃ tathottamam ।। 30.99 ।।  
  
hatvā rajisutān sarvānkāmakrodhaparāyaṇān।  
ya idaṃ pāvanaṃ sthānaṃ pratiṣṭānaṃ śatakratoḥ।  
śrṛṇuyādvā rajervāpi na sa daurātmyamāpnuyāt ।। 30.100 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte rajiyuddhaṃ nāma triṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 30 ।। 


---
title: 031

---
        ।।ṛṣayaḥ ūcuḥ।।  
marutena kathaṃ kanyā rājñe dattā mahātmanā।  
kiṃvīryāśca mahātmāno jātā marutakanyakāḥ ।। 31.1 ।।  
  
         ।।sūta uvāca।।  
āhavan taṃ marutsomamannakāmaḥ prajeśvaram।  
māsi māsi mahātejāḥ ṣaṣṭisaṃvatsarānnṛpaḥ ।। 31.2 ।।  
  
tena te marutastasya marutsomena toṣitāḥ।  
akṣayyānnaṃ daduḥ prītāḥ sarvakāmaparicchadam ।। 31.3 ।।  
  
annaṃ tasya sakṛtpakvamahorātre na kṣīyate।  
koṭiśo dīyamānaṃ ca sūryyasyodayanādapi ।। 31.4 ।।  
  
mitrājyotistu kanyāyāṃ marutasya ca dhīmataḥ।  
tasmājjātā mahāsattvā dharmajñā mokṣadarśinaḥ ।। 31.5 ।।  
  
saṃnyasya gṛhadharmāṇi vairāgyaṃ samupasthitāḥ।  
yatidharmamavāpyeha brahmabhūyāya te gatāḥ ।। 31.6 ।।  
  
anapāyastato jātastadā dharmapradattavān।  
kṣatradharmastato jātaḥ pratipakṣo mahātapāḥ ।। 31.7 ।।  
  
pratipakṣasutaścāpi sañjayo nāma viśrutaḥ।  
sañjayasya jayaḥ putro vijayastasya jagmivān ।। 31.8 ।।  
  
vijayasya jayaḥ putrastasya haryandvataḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
haryandutastato rājā sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ।। 31.9 ।।  
  
sahadevasya dharmātmā adīna iti viśrutaḥ।  
adīnasya jayatsenastasya putro'tha saṃkṛtiḥ ।। 31.10 ।।  
  
saṃkṛterapi dharmātmā kṛtadharmā mahāyaśāḥ।  
ityete kṣatra dharmāṇo nahuṣasya nibodhata ।। 31.11 ।।  
  
nahuṣasya tu dāyādāḥ ṣaḍindropamatejasaḥ।  
utpannāḥ pitṛkanyāyāṃ virajāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।। 31.12 ।।  
  
yatiryayātiḥ saṃyātirāyātiḥ pañca tudvayaḥ।  
yatirjyeṣṭhastu teṣāṃ vai yayātistu tato'varaḥ ।। 31.13 ।।  
  
kākutsthakanyāṃ gāṃ nāma lebhe patnīṃ yatistadā।  
saṃyātirmo kṣamāsthāya brahmabhūto'bhavanmuniḥ ।। 31.14 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ madhye tu pañcānāṃ yayātiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ।  
devayānimuśanasaḥ sutāṃ bhāryāmavāpa ha ।। 31.15 ।।  
  
śarmiṣṭā māsurīṃ caiva tanayāṃ vṛṣaparvaṇaḥ।  
yaduṃ ca turvasuṃ caiva devayānirvyajāyata ।। 31.16 ।।  
  
druhyuñcānuñca pūruñca śarmiṣṭā vārṣaparvaṇī ।  
ajījananmahāvīryān sutāndevasutopamān ।। 31.17 ।।  
  
rathantasmai dadau rudraḥ prītaḥ paramabhāsvaram।  
asaṅgaṃ kāñcanaṃ divyamakṣayau ca maheṣudhī ।। 31.18 ।।  
  
yuktaṃ mano javairaśvairyena kanyāṃ samudvahat।  
sa tena rathamukhyena jigāya ca tato mahīm ।। 31.19 ।।  
  
yayātiryudhi durddharṣo devadānavamānavaiḥ ।  
pauravāṇāṃ nṛpāṇāñca sarveṣāṃ so'bhavadrathaḥ ।। 31.20 ।।  
  
yovatsudeśaprabhavaḥ kauravo janamejayaḥ।  
kuroḥ putrasya rājñastu rājñaḥ pārikṣitasya ha।  
jagāma sa ratho nāśaṃ śāpādgārgyasya dhīmataḥ ।। 31.21 ।।  
  
gārgyasya hi sutaṃ bālaḥ sa rājā janamejayaḥ।  
durbuddhirhiṃsayāmāsa lohagandhaṃ narādhipam ।। 31.22 ।।  
  
sa lohagandho rājarṣiḥ paridhāvannitastataḥ।  
paurajānapadaistyakto na lebhe śarma karhicit ।। 31.23 ।।  
  
tataḥ sa duḥkhasantapto nālabhatsaṃvidaṃ kvacit।  
śaśāpa hetukamṛṣiṃ śaraṇyaṃ vyathitastadā ।। 31.24 ।।  
  
īndroto nāma vikhyāto yo'sau munirudāradhīḥ।  
yojayāmāsa cendrotaḥ śaunako janamejayam।  
aśvamedhena rājānaṃ pāvanārthaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। 31.25 ।।  
  
sa lohagandho vyanaśattasyāvasathametya ha।  
sa ca divyo rathastasmādvasoścedipatestathā ।। 31.26 ।।  
  
tataḥ śakreṇa tuṣṭena lebhe tasmādbṛhadrathaḥ।  
tato hatvā jarāsandhaṃ bhīmastaṃ rathamuttamam।  
pradadau vāsudevāya prītyā kauravanandanaḥ ।। 31.27 ।।  
  
sa jarāṃ prāpya rājarṣiryayātirnahuṣātmajaḥ।  
putraṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ variṣṭhañca yadumityabravīdvacaḥ ।।31.28 ।।  
  
jarāvalī ca māṃ tāta palitāni ca paryaguḥ ।  
kāvyasyośanasaḥ śāpānna ca tṛpto'smi yauvane ।। 31.29 ।।  
  
tvaṃ yado pratipadyasva pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha।  
jarāṃ me pratigṛhṇīṣva taṃ yaduḥ pratyuvāca ha ।। 31.30 ।।  
  
anirdiṣṭā mayā bhikṣā brāhmaṇasya pratiśrutā ।  
sā ca vyāyāmasādhyā vai na grahīṣyāmi te jarām ।। 31.31 ।।  
  
jarāyā bahavo doṣā pānabhojanakāriṇaḥ।  
tasmājjarānna te rājan grahītumahamutsahe ।। 31.32 ।।  
  
sitaśmaśrudharo dīno jarayā śithilīkṛtaḥ।  
balī sannatagātraśca durddaśo durbalākṛtiḥ ।। 31.33 ।।  
  
aśaktaḥ kāryakaraṇe paribhūtastu yauvane।  
mahopabhītibhiścaiva tāṃ jarānnābhikāmaye ।। 31.34 ।।  
  
santi te bahavaḥ putrā mattaḥ priyatarā nṛpa।  
pratigṛhṇantu dharmajña putramanyaṃ vṛṇīṣva vai ।। 31.35 ।।  
  
sa evamukto yadunā tīvrakopasamanvitaḥ।  
uvāca vadatāṃ śreṣcho jyeṣṭhaṃ taṃ garhayan sutam ।। 31.36 ।।  
  
āśramaḥ kaśca vānyo'sti ko vā dharmavidhistava।  
māmanādṛtya durbuddhe yadāttha navadeśika ।। 31.37 ।।  
  
evamuktvā yaduṃ rājā śaśāpainaṃ sa manyumān ।  
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svaṃ na prayacchasi ।। 31.38 ।।  
  
tasmānna rājyabhāg mūḍha prajā te vai bhaviṣyati।  
turvaso pratipadyasva pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ।। 31.39 ।।  
  
        turvasuruvāca।।  
na kāmaye jarāṃ tāta sāmabhogapraṇāśinīm।  
jarāyā bahavo doṣāḥ pānabhojanakāriṇaḥ।  
tasmājjarāṃ na te rājan grahītumahamutsahe ।। 31.40 ।।  
  
       yayātiruvāca।।  
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svanna prayacchasi।  
tasmāt prajā samucchedaṃ turvaso tava yāsyati ।। 31.41 ।।  
  
asaṅkīrṇā ca dharmeṇa pratilomavareṣu ca।  
piśitādiṣu cānyeṣu mūḍha rājā bhaviṣyasi ।। 31.42 ।।  
  
guru dāraprasakteṣu tiryagyonigateṣu vā।  
paśudharmeṣu mleccheṣu bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।। 31.43 ।।  
  
          sūta uvāca।  
evantu turvasuṃ śaptvā yayātiḥ sutamātmanaḥ।  
śarmiṣṭāyāḥ sutaṃ druhyumidaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। 31.44 ।।  
  
druhyo tvaṃ pratipadyasva varṇarūpavināśinīm।  
jarāṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai yauvanaṃ svandadasva me ।। 31.45 ।।  
  
pūrṇe varṣasahasre te pratidāsyāmi yauvanam।  
svañcādāsyāmi būyo'haṃ pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha ।। 31.46 ।।  
  
       druhyuruvāca।।  
na gajaṃ na rathaṃ nāśvaṃ jīrṇo bhuṅkte na ca striyam ।।  
  
na saṅgaścāsya bhavati na jarāṃ tena kāmaye ।। 31.47 ।।  
  
              yayātiruvāca।।  
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svanna prayacchasi।  
tasmād druhyo priyaḥ kāmo na te sampatsyate kvacit ।। 31.48 ।।  
  
nauplavottarasañcārastatra nityaṃ bhaviṣyati।  
arājabhrājavaṃśastvaṃ tatra nityaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। 31.49 ।।  
  
ano tvaṃ pratipadyasva pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha।  
evaṃ varṣasahasrantu careyaṃ yauvanena te ।। 31.50 ।।  
  
       anuruvāca।।  
jīrṇaḥ śiśuvaraṃ datte jarayā hyaśuciḥ sadā।।  
na juhoti sa kāle'gni tāṃ jarānnābikāmaye ।। 31.51 ।।  
  
          yayātiruvāca।।  
yastvaṃ me hṛdayājjāto vayaḥ svanna prayacchasi।  
jarādoṣastvayokto'yaṃ tasmātte pratipatsyate ।। 31.52 ।।  
  
prajā ca yauvanaṃ prāptā vinaśiṣyatyatastava।  
agnipraskandanaparastvaṃ cāpyeva bhaviṣyasi ।। 31.53 ।।  
  
pūro tvaṃ pratipadyasva pāpmānañjarayā saha।  
jarāvalī ca māntāta palitāni ca paryaguḥ ।। 31.54 ।।  
  
kāvyasyośanasaḥ śāpānna ca tṛpto'smi yauvane।  
kañcitkālañjareyaṃ vai viṣayān vayasā tava ।। 31.55 ।।  
  
pūrṇeṃ varṣasahasre te pratidāsyāmi yauvanam।  
svañcaiva pratipatsyāmi pāpmānañjarayā saha ।। 31.56 ।।  
  
             sūta uvāca।।  
evamuktaḥ pratyuvāca putraḥ pitaramañjasā।  
yathānumanyase tāta kariṣyāmi tathaiva ca ।। 31.57 ।।  
  
pratipatsyāmi te rājan pāpmānaṃ jarayā saha।  
gṛhāṇa yauvanaṃ mattaścara kāmān yathepsitān ।। 31.58 ।।  
  
jarayāhaṃ praticchanno vayorūpadharastava।  
yauvanaṃ bhavate dattvā cariṣyāmi yathārtavat ।। 31.59 ।।  
  
          yayātiruvāca।।  
pūro prīto'smi bhadrante prītaścedaṃ dadāmi te।  
sarvakāmasamṛddhā te prajā rājye bhaviṣyati ।। 31.60 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
pūroranumato rājā yayātiḥ svāṃ jarāntataḥ।  
saṃkrāmayāmāsa tadā prasādādbhārgavasya tu ।। 31.61 ।।  
  
yauvanenātha vayasā yayātiranahuṣātmajaḥ ।  
prītiyukto naraśreṣṭhaścacāra viṣayān svakān ।। 31.62 ।।  
  
yathākāmaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathākālaṃ yathāsukham।  
dharmmāvirodhādrājendro yathārhati sa eva hi ।। 31.63 ।।  
  
devānatarpayadyajñaiḥ pitṝñchrāddhaistathaiva ca।  
dīnāṃścānugrahairiṣṭaiḥ kāmaiśca dvijasattamān ।। 31.64 ।।  
  
atithīnannapānaiśca vaiśyāṃśca paripālanaiḥ।  
ānṛśaṃsyena śūdrāṃśca dasyūn saṃnigraheṇa ca ।। 31.65 ।।  
  
dharmmeṇa ca prajāḥ sarvvā yathāvadanurañjayan।  
yayātiḥ pālayāmāsa sākṣādindra ivāparaḥ ।। 31.66 ।।  
  
sa rājā siṃhavikrānto yuvā viṣayagocaraḥ।  
avirodhena dharmasya cacāra sukhamuttamam ।। 31.67 ।।  
  
sa mārgamāṇaḥ kāmānāmantardoṣanidarśanāt।  
viśvāsaheto reme vai vaibrāje nandane vane ।। 31.68 ।।  
  
apaśyatsa yadā tāṃ vai varddhamānāṃ nṛpastadā।  
gatvā pūroḥ sakāśaṃ vai svāṃ jarā pratyapadyata ।। 31.69 ।।  
  
sa samprāpya tu tān kāmāṃstṛptaḥ khinnaśca pārthivaḥ।  
kālaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai sasmāra manujādhipaḥ। ।। 31.70 ।।  
  
parisaṅkhyāya kālañca kalākāṣṭāstathaiva ca।  
pūrṇaṃ mattvā tataḥ kālaṃ pūruṃ putramuvāca ha ।। 31.71 ।।  
  
yathāsukhaṃ yathotsāhaṃ yathākālamariṃdama।  
sevitā viṣayāḥ putra yauvanena mayā tava ।। 31.72 ।।  
  
pūro prīto'smi bhadraṃ te gṛhāṇa tvaṃ svayauvanam।  
rāṣṭrañca nṛpaṃ pūruṃ putraṃ kanīyasam।  
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। 31.73 ।।  
  
pratipede jarāṃ rājā yayātirnahuṣātmajaḥ।  
yauvanaṃ pratipede ca pūruḥ svaṃ punarātmanaḥ ।। 31.74 ।।  
  
abhiṣektukāmañca nṛpaṃ pūruṃ putraṃ kanīyasam।  
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇā idaṃ vacanamabruvan ।। 31.75 ।।  
  
kathaṃ śukrasya naptāraṃ devayānyāḥ sutaṃ prabho।  
śreṣṭhaṃ yadumatikramya pūro rājyaṃ pradāsyasi ।। 31.76 ।।  
  
yadurjyeṣṭhastava suto jātastamanu turvasuḥ।  
śarmiṣṭāyāḥ suto druhyustano'nuḥ pūrureva ca ।। 31.77 ।।  
  
kathaṃ jyeṣṭānatikramya kanīyān rājyamarhati ।  
ataḥ sambodhayāmi tvāṃ dharmmaṃ samanupālaya ।। 31.78 ।।  
  
          yayātiruvāca।।  
brāhmaṇapramukhā varṇāḥ sarve śrṛṇvantu me vacaḥ।  
jyeṣṭaṃ prati yathā rārṣṭraṃ na deyaṃ me kathañcana ।। 31.79 ।।  
  
mātā pitrorvacanakṛtsa hi putraḥ praśasyate ।  
mama jyeṣṭena yadunā niyogo nānupālitaḥ ।। 31.80 ।।  
  
pratikūlaṃ pituryaśca na sa putraḥ satāṃ mataḥ।  
sa putraḥ putravad yaśca varttate pitṛmātṛṣu ।। 31.81 ।।  
  
yadunāhamavajñātastathā turvasunāpi ca।  
druhyuṇā cānunā caivamapyavajñā kṛtā bhṛśam ।। 31.82 ।।  
  
pūruṇā tu kṛtaṃ vākyaṃ mānitaśca viśeṣataḥ।  
kanīyān mama dāyādo jarā yena dhṛtā mama।  
sarvakāmaḥ sarvakṛtaḥ pūruṇā putrakāriṇā ।। 31.83 ।।  
  
śukreṇa ca varo dattaḥ kāvye nośanasā svayam।  
putro yastvānuvartteta sa rājā te mahāmate ।। 31.84 ।।  
  
bhavato'numatopyevaṃ pūru rāṣṭre'bhiṣicyatām ।  
yaḥputro guṇasampanno mātāpitrorhitaḥ sadā।  
sarvamarhati kalyāṇaṃ kanīyānapi sa prabhuḥ ।। 31.85 ।।  
  
arhaḥ pūruridaṃ rāṣṭraṃ yaḥ priyaḥ priyakṛttava।  
varadānena śukrasya na śakyaṃ vaktumuttaram ।। 31.86 ।।  
  
paurajānapadaistuṣṭairityukto nāhuṣastadā।  
abhiṣicya tataḥ pūruṃ svarāṣṭre sutamātmanaḥ ।। 31.87 ।।  
  
diśi dakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ turvasuṃ tu nyaveśayat।  
dakṣiṇāparato rājā yaduṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nyaveśayat ।। 31.88 ।।  
  
pratīcyāmuttarasyāñca druhyuñcānuñca tāvubhau।  
saptadvīpāṃ yayātistu jittvā pṛthvīṃ sasāgarām।  
vyabhajat pañcadhā rājā putrebhyo nāhuṣastadā ।। 31.89 ।।  
  
tairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā।  
yathāpradeśaṃ dharmajñairdharmmeṇa pratipālyate ।। 31.90 ।।  
  
evaṃ visṛjya pṛthivīṃ putrebhyo nāhuṣastadā।  
putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīstu prītimānabhavannṛpaḥ ।। 31.91 ।।  
  
dhanurnyasya pṛṣatkāṃśca rājyañcaiva suteṣu tu।  
prītimānabhavadrājā bhāramāveśya bandhuṣu ।। 31.92 ।।  
  
atra gāthā mahārājñā purā gītā yayātinā।  
yo'bhipretyāharan kāmān kūrmoṅgānīva sarvaśaḥ ।। 31.93 ।।  
  
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānāmupabhogena śāmyati।  
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivarddhate ।। 31.94 ।।  
  
yat pṛthivyāṃ vrīhiyavaṃ hiraṇyaṃ paśavaḥ striyaḥ ।  
nālamekasya tatsarvamiti paśyanna muhyati ।। 31.95 ।।  
  
yadā tu kurute bhāvaṃ sarvvabhūteṣu pāvakam।  
karmmaṇā manasā vācā brahma sampadyate tadā ।। 31.96 ।।  
  
yadā parānna bibheti yadā tvasmānna bibhyati।  
yadā necchati na dveṣṭi brahma sampadyate tadā ।। 31.97 ।।  
  
yā dustyajā durmmatibhiryā na jīryati jīryyataḥ।  
doṣāprāṇāntiko rāgastāṃ tṛṣṇāntyajataḥ sukham ।। 31.98 ।।  
  
jīryyanti jīryataḥ kośā dantā jīryanti jaryitaḥ।  
jīvitāśā dhanāśā ca jīryyatopi na jīryati ।। 31.99 ।।  
  
yaccākāmasukhaṃ loke yacca divyaṃ mahat sukham।  
tṛṣṇāsya ca sukhasyaiva kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm ।। 31.100 ।।  
  
evamuktvā sa rājarṣiḥ sadāraḥ prasthito vanam।  
bhṛgutuṅge tapastaptvā tatraiva ca mahāyaśāḥ।  
pālayitvā vrataśataṃ tatraiva svargamāpnuyāt ।। 31.101 ।।  
  
tasya vaṃśāstu pañcaite puṇyā devarṣisatkṛtāḥ।  
yairvyāptā pṛthivī kṛtsnā sūryasyeva gabhastibhiḥ ।। 31.102 ।।  
  
dhanyaḥ prajāvānāyuṣmān kīrtimāṃśca bhavennaraḥ।  
yayāteścaritaṃ sarvaṃ paṭhañchṛṇvan dvijottamaḥ ।। 31.103 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte candra vaṃśakīrttanaṃ nāmaikatriṃśo'dyāyaḥ ।। 31 ।।


---
title: 032

---
           ।।sūrya uvāca।।  
yadorvaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmi śreṣṭhasyottamatejhasaḥ।  
vistareṇānupūrvyeṇa gadato me nibodhata ।। 32.1 ।।  
  
yadoḥ putrā babhūvurhi pañca devasutopamāḥ।  
sahasrajidatha śreṣṭhaḥ kroṣṭurnīlo jito laghuḥ ।। 32.2 ।।  
  
sahasrajitsutaḥ śrīmāñchatajinnāma pārthivaḥ।  
satajitsutā vikhyā tāstrayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ ।। 32.3 ।।  
  
haihayaśca hayaścaiva rājā veṇuhayaśca yaḥ।  
haihayasya tu dāyādo dharmmatattva iti śrutiḥ ।। 32.4 ।।  
  
dharmmatantrastu kīrttistu saṃjñeyastasya cātmajaḥ।  
saṃjñeyasya tu dāyādo mahiṣmānnāma pārthivaḥ ।। 32.5 ।।  
  
āsīnmahiṣmataḥ putro bhadraśreṇyaḥ pratāpavān।  
vārāṇasyadhipo rājā kathitaḥ pūrva eva hi ।। 32.6 ।।  
  
bhadraśreṇyasya dāyādo durmado nāma pārthivaḥ।  
durmadasya tato dhīmān kanko nāma viśrutaḥ ।। 32.7 ।।  
  
kanakasya tu dāyādāścatvāro lokaviśrutāḥ।  
kṛta vīryaḥ kārtavīryaḥ kṛtavarmā tathaiva ca ।। 32.8 ।।  
  
kṛto jātaścaturtho'bhūtkṛtaviryāttato'rjunaḥ।  
jajñe bāhusahasreṇa saptadvīpeśvaro nṛpaḥ ।। 32.9 ।।  
  
sa hi varṣāyutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ paramaduścaram।  
dattamārādhayāmāsa kārttavīryo'trisambhavam ।। 32.10 ।।  
  
tasmai datto varān prādāccaturo bhūritejasaḥ।  
pūrvvaṃ bāhusahasrantu sa vavre prathamaṃ varam ।। 32.11 ।।  
  
adharmme dīyamānasya sadbhistasmānnivāraṇam।  
dharmmeṇa pṛthivīñjitvā dharmmeṇaivānupālanam ।। 32.12 ।।  
  
saṃgrāmāṃstu bahūn jittvā hatvā cārīn sahasraśaḥ।  
saṃgrāme yuddhayamānasya vadhaḥ syādadhikādraṇe ।। 32.13 ।।  
  
teneyaṃ pṛthivī kṛtsnā saptadvīpā sapattanā ।  
saptodadhiparikṣiptā kṣātreṇa vidhinā janāḥ ।। 32.14 ।।  
  
tasya bāhusahasrantu yuddhyataḥ kila dhīmataḥ।  
yauddho dhvajo rathaścaiva prādurbhavati māyayā ।। 32.15 ।।  
  
daśayajñasahasrāṇi teṣu dvīpeṣu saptasu।  
nirargalāḥ sma nirvṛttāḥ śrūyante tasya dhīmataḥ ।। 32.16 ।।  
  
sarve yajñā mahābāhostasyāsan bhūritejasaḥ।  
sarve kāñcanavedīkāḥ sarve yūpaiśca kāñcanaiḥ ।। 32.17 ।।  
  
sarve devairmmāhābhāgairvimānasthairalaṃkṛtāḥ।  
gandharvvairapsarobhiśca nityamevopaśobhitāḥ ।। 32.18 ।।  
  
tasya rājño jagau gāthāṃ gandharvo nāradastathā।  
caritaṃ tasya rājarṣermahimānaṃ nirīkṣya ca ।। 32.19 ।।  
  
na nūnaṃ kārttavīryasya gatiṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ।  
yajñairdānaistapobhiśca vikrameṇa śrutena ca ।। 32.20 ।।  
  
dvīpeṣu saptasu sa vai khaḍgī varaśarāsanī।  
rathī rājāpyanucaro'nyo'gāccaivānudṛśyate ।। 32.21 ।।  
  
anaṣṭadravyaścaivāsīnna śoko na ca vibhramaḥ।  
prabhāveṇa mahārājñaḥ prajā dharmmeṇa rakṣataḥ ।। 32.22 ।।  
  
pañcāśītisahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ sa narādhipaḥ।  
sapta sapta vārān samrāṭ cakravarttī babhūva ha ।। 32.23 ।।  
  
sa eva paśupālo'bhūt kṣetrapālastathaiva ca।  
sa eva vṛṣṭyā parjanyo yogitvādarjjuno'bhavat ।। 32.24 ।।  
  
sa vai bāhusahasreṇa jyāghātakaṭinena ca ।  
bhāti raśmisahasreṇa śāradeneva bhāskaraḥ ।। 32.25 ।।  
  
sa hi nāgasahasreṇa māhiṣmatyāṃ narādhipaḥ।  
karkoṭakasabhāñjitvā purīṃ tatra nyaveśayat ।। 32.26 ।।  
  
sa vai vege samudrasya prāvṛṭkālāmbujekṣaṇaḥ ।  
krīḍanniva sukhodvignaḥ prāvṛṭkālañcakāra ha ।। 32.27 ।।  
  
lulitā krīḍatā tena hemasragdāmamālinī।  
ūrmmibhrūkuṭisannādā śaṅkitābhyeti narmadā ।। 32.28 ।।  
  
purā sa tāmanusarannavagāḍho mahārṇavam।  
cakāroddhṛttya velāntaṃ sa kālaḥ prāvṛṇodvanam ।। 32.29 ।।  
  
tasya bāhu sahasreṇa kṣobhyamāṇe mahādadhau।  
bhavanti līnā niśceṣṭāḥ pātālasthā mahāsurāḥ ।। 32.30 ।।  
  
cūrṇīkṛtamahāvīcilīnamīnamahāviṣāḥ।  
patitā viddhaphenaughamāvarttakṣiptadussaham ।। 32.31 ।।  
  
cakāra kṣobhayanrājā doḥsahasreṇa sāgaram।  
devāsuraparikṣiptaṃ kṣīrodamiva sāgaram ।। 32.32 ।।  
  
mandarakṣobhaṇakṛtā hyamṛtodakaśaṅki tāḥ।  
sahasotpāditā bhītā bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā nṛpottamam ।। 32.33 ।।  
  
nataniścalamūrddhāno babhūvuśca mahoragāḥ।  
sāyāhne kadalīṣaṇḍā nirvātastimitā iva ।। 32.34 ।।  
  
sa vai baddhvā dhanuryāna utsiktaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ।  
laṅkāyāṃ mohayitvā tu sabalaṃ rāvaṇaṃ balāt।  
nirjitya baddhvā cānīya māhiṣmatyāṃ babandha tam ।। 32.35 ।।  
  
tato gatvā pulastyastu arjunaṃ ca prasādayat।  
mumoca rājā paulastyaṃ pulastyenānupālitam ।। 32.36 ।।  
  
tasya bāhusahasrasya babhūva jyātalasvanaḥ।  
yugānte'mbudavṛkṣasya sphuṭitasyāśaneriva ।। 32.37 ।।  
  
aho mṛdhe mahāvīryaṃ bhārgavo yasya so'cchinat।  
mṛdhe sahasraṃ bāhūnāṃ hematālavanaṃ yathā ।। 32.38 ।।  
  
tṛṣitena kadācitsa bhikṣitaścitrabhānunā।  
sapta dvīpāṃścitrabhānoḥ prādādbhikṣāṃ viśāmpatiḥ ।। 32.39 ।।  
  
purāṇi ghoṣān grāmāṃśca pattanāni ca sarvvaśaḥ।।  
jajvāla tasya bāṇeṣu citrabhānurdidhakṣayā ।। 32.40 ।।  
  
sa tasya puruṣendrasya prabhāveṇa mahāyaśāḥ।  
dadāha kārtavīryasya śailāṃścāpi vanāni ca ।। 32.41 ।।  
  
sa śūnyamāśramaṃ sarvaṃ varuṇasyātmajasya vai।  
dadoha savanadvīpāṃścitrabhānuḥ sahaihayaḥ ।। 32.42 ।।  
  
saṃlebhe varuṇaḥ putraṃ purā bhāsvinamuttamam।  
vasiṣṭhanāmā sa muniḥ khyātaścāpaḥ śritaḥ śrutaḥ ।। 32.43 ।।  
  
tatrāpadastadā krodhādarjunaṃ śaptavānvibhuḥ।  
yasmānna varjitamidaṃ vanaṃ te mama haihaya ।। 32.44 ।।  
  
tasmāt te duṣkaraṃ karmma kṛtamanyo haniṣyati।  
arjuno nāma kaunteyo na ca rājā bhaviṣyati ।। 32.45 ।।  
  
arjuna tvāṃ mahāvīryo rāmaḥ praharatāṃ varaḥ।  
chittvā bāhusahasraṃ vai pramathya tarasā balīṃ ।। 32.46 ।।  
  
tapasvī brāhmaṇaścaiva vadhiṣyati mahābalaḥ।  
tasya rāmastadā hyāsīnmṛtyuśāpena dhīmataḥ ।। 32.47 ।।  
  
rājñā tena varaścaiva svayameva vṛtaḥ purā।  
tasya putraśataṃ hyāsīt pañca tatra mahārathāḥ ।। 32.48 ।।  
  
kṛtāstrā balinaḥ śūrā dharmmātmāno yaśasvanaḥ ।  
śūraśca śūrasenaśca vṛṣṭyādyaṃ vṛṣa eva ca ।। 32.49 ।।  
  
jayadhvajaśca vai putrā avantiṣu viśāṃpateḥ।  
jayadhvajasya putrastu tālajaṅghaḥ pratāpavān ।। 32.50 ।।  
  
tasya putraśataṃ hyeva tālajaṅghā iti śrutam।  
teṣāṃ pañca gaṇāḥ khyātā haihayānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 32.51 ।।  
  
vīrahotrā hyasaṅkhyātā bhojāścāvartayastathā।  
tuṇḍikerāśca vikrāntāstālajaṅghāstathaiva ca ।। 32.52 ।।  
  
vīrahotrasutaścāpi ananto nāma pārthivaḥ।  
durjayastasya putrastu babhūvāmitradarśanaḥ ।। 32.53 ।।  
  
anaṣṭadravyatā caiva tasya rājño babhūva ha।  
prabhāveṇa mahārājaḥ prajāstāḥ paryyapālayat ।। 32.54 ।।  
  
na tasya vittanāśaśca naṣṭaṃ pratilabheta saḥ।  
kārtavīryasya yo janma kathayediha dhīmataḥ ।। 32.55 ।।  
  
vittavān bhavatyatraiva dharmmaścāsya vivarddhate।  
yathā tvaṣṭā yathā dātā tathā svarge mahīyate ।। 32.56 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte kārttavīryyārjunotpattivivaraṇaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 32 ।


---
title: 033

---
          ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
kimarthaṃ bhuvanaṃ dagdhamapavasyaṃ mahātmanām।  
kārtavīryeṇa vikramya tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ।। 33.1 ।।  
  
rakṣitā sa tu rājarṣiḥ prajānāmiti naḥ śrutam।  
kathaṃ sa rakṣitā bhūtvānāśayattattapovanam ।। 33.2 ।।  
  
       sūta uvāca।।  
ādityo viprarūpeṇa kārtavīryamupasthitaḥ।  
tṛptikāmaḥ prayacchānnamādityo'haṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।। 33.3 ।।  
  
         rājovāca।।  
bhagavan kena te tuṣṭirbhavedbrūhi divākara।  
kīdṛśaṃ bhojanaṃ dajhi śrutvā ca vidadhāmyaham ।। 33.4 ।।  
  
         sūrya uvāca।।  
sthāvaraṃ dehi me sarvamāhāraṃ dadatāṃ vara।  
tena tṛpto bhaveyaṃ vai na tuṣye'nyena pārthiva ।। 33.5 ।।  
  
          rājovāca ।।  
  
na śakyaṃ sthāvaraṃ sarvvaṃ tejasā mānuṣeṇa tu।  
nirddagdhuṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭha tvāmeva praṇamāmyaham ।। 33.6 ।।  
  
          āditya uvāca।।  
tuṣṭaste'haṃ śarān dajhi akṣayān sarvataḥ sukhān।  
prakṣiptāḥ prajvaliṣyanti mama tejaḥsamanvitāḥ ।। 33.7 ।।  
  
ādiṣṭaṃ tejasā meghasāgaraṃ śoṣayiṣyati।  
śuṣkaṃ bhasma kariṣyāmi tena prīto narādhipa ।। 33.8 ।।  
  
tataḥ śarānathādityastvarjunāya prayacchati।  
tataḥ saṃprāpya sumahatsthāvaraṃ sarvvameva hi ।। 33.9 ।।  
  
āśramānatha grāmāṃśca ghoṣāṃśca nagarāṇi ca।  
tapovanāni ramyāṇi vanānyupavanāni ca ।। 33.10 ।।  
  
evaṃ prācīnamadahattataḥ sūryyapradakṣiṇam।  
nirvṛkṣā nistṛṇā bhūmirdagdhā sūryeṇa tejasā ।। 33.11 ।।  
  
etasminneva kāle tu apo nilayamāśritaḥ।  
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi jalavāsā mahānṛṣiḥ ।। 33.12 ।।  
  
pūrṇe vrate mahātejā udatiṣṭhattapodhanaḥ।  
so'paśyadāśramaṃ dagdhamarjunena mahānṛṣiḥ।  
krodhācchaśāpa rājarṣiṃ kīrttitaṃ vo yathā mayā ।। 33.13 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
kroṣṭoḥ śrṛṇuta rājarṣervaṃśamuttamapūruṣam।  
yasyānvavāye saṃbhūto vṛṣṇirvṛṣṇikulodvahaḥ ।। 33.14 ।।  
  
kroṣṭoreko'bhavat putro vṛjinīvān mahāyaśāḥ।  
vārjinīvatamicchanti svāhiṃ svāhovatāṃ varam ।। 33.15 ।।  
  
svāheḥ putro'bhavadrājā raśādurdadatāṃ varaḥ।  
ghṛtamprasūtamicchanti raśādoragryamātmajam ।। 33.16 ।।  
  
mahākratubhirīje sa vividhairāptadakṣiṇaiḥ।  
citraiścitrarathastasya putra karmmabhiranvitaḥ ।। 33.17 ।।  
  
evaṃ citraratho vīro yajñān vipuladakṣiṇān।  
śaśabinduḥ paraṃ vṛtto rājarṣīṇāmanuṣṭitaḥ ।। 33.18 ।।  
  
cakravarttī mahāsattvo mahāvīryo bahuprajaḥ।  
tatrānuvaṃśaśloko'yaṃ yasmin gītaḥ purāvidaiḥ ।। 33.19 ।।  
  
śaśabindostu putrāṇāṃ śatānāmabhavacchatam।  
dhīmatāmanurūpāṇāṃ bhūridraviṇatejasām ।। 33.20 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ ṣaṭ ca pradhānāstu pṛthuṣāṭkā mahābalāḥ।  
pṛthuśravā pṛthuyaśāḥ pṛthudharmmā pṛthuñjayaḥ ।। 33.21 ।।  
  
pṛthukīrttiḥ pṛthundātā rājānaḥ śāśibindavāḥ।  
śaṃsanti ca purāṇāni pārthaśravasamantaram।  
antaraḥ sa purā yastu yajñasya tanayo'bhavat ।। 33.22 ।।  
  
uśanā sutadharmmātmā avāpya pṛthivīmimām।  
ājahārāśvamedhānāṃ śatamuttamadhārmmikaḥ ।। 33.23 ।।  
  
maruttastasya tanayo rājarṣīṇāmanuṣṭitaḥ।  
vīraḥ kambalabarhistu maruttatanayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 33.24 ।।  
  
putrastu rukmakavaco vidvān kambalavarhiṣaḥ।  
nihatya rukmakavacaḥ purā kavacino raṇe ।। 33.25 ।।  
  
dhanvino niśitairbāṇairavāpa śriyamuttamām।  
brāhmaṇebhyo dadau vittamaśvamedhamahāyaśāḥ ।। 33.26 ।।  
  
rājñastu rukmakavacādaparāvṛttya vīrahāḥ।  
jajñire pañca putrāstu mahāsattvā mahābalāḥ ।। 33.27 ।।  
  
rukmeṣuḥ pṛthurukmaśca jyāmaghaḥ parigho hariḥ।  
parighañca hariñcaiva videhe sthāpayatpitā ।। 33.28 ।।  
  
brahmeṣurabhavadrājā pṛthurukmastadāśrayaḥ।  
tebhyaḥ pravrajito rājyā jjyāmagho'bhavadāśrame ।। 33.29 ।।  
  
praśāntastu vane ghore brāhmaṇenāvabodhitaḥ।  
jagāma dhanurādāya deśamadhyaṃ rathī dhvajī ।। 33.30 ।।  
  
narmmadānūpa ekākī mekalāvṛttikā api।  
ṛkṣavantaṃ giriṃ gatvā śuktimanyāmathāviśat ।। 33.31 ।।  
  
jyāmaghasyābhavadbhāryā śaibhyā balavatī bhṛśam।  
aputro'pi sa vai rājā bhāryāmanyāṃ na vindati ।। 33.32 ।।  
  
tasyāsīdvijayo yuddhe tataḥ kanyāmavāpa saḥ।  
bhāryāmuvāca rājā sa snuṣeti tu nareśvaraḥ ।। 33.33 ।।  
  
evamuktābravīdevaṃ kāmye yante snuṣeti sā।  
yaste janiṣyate putrastasya bhāryā bhaviṣyati ।। 33.34 ।।  
  
tasya sā tapasogreṇa śaibyā vaiśaṃ prasūyata ।  
putraṃ vidarbhaṃ subhagā śaibyā pariṇatā satī ।। 33.35 ।।  
  
rājaputrau tu vidvāṃsau snuṣāyāṃ krathukauśikau।  
putrau vidarbho'janayacchūrau raṇaviśāradau ।। 33.36 ।।  
  
lomapādaṃ tṛtīyantu paścājjajñe sudhārmikaḥ।  
loma pādātmajovasturāhṛtistasya cātmajaḥ ।। 33.37 ।।  
  
kauśikasya cidiḥ putrastasmāccaidyā nṛpāḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
krathorvidarbhaputrastu kuntistasyātmajo'bhavat ।। 33.38 ।।  
  
kunterdhṛṣṭasuto jajñe purodhṛṣṭaḥ pratāpavān ।  
dhṛṣṭasya putro dharmātmā nirvṛtiḥ paravīrahā ।। 33.39 ।।  
  
tasya putro daśārhastu mahābalaparākramaḥ।  
daśarhasya suto vyomā tato jīmūta ucyate ।। 33.40 ।।  
  
jīmūtaputro vikṛtistasya bhīmarathaḥ sutaḥ.  
atha bhīmarathasyāsīt putro rathavaraḥ kila ।। 33.41 ।।  
  
dātā dharmmarato nityaṃ śīlasatyaparāyaṇaḥ।  
tasya putro navarathastato daśarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 33.42 ।।  
  
tasya caikādaśarathaḥ śakunistasya cātmajaḥ।  
tasmāt karambhako dhanvī devarāto'bhavattataḥ ।। 33.43 ।।  
  
devakṣatro'bhavadrājā devarātirmmahāyaśāḥ।  
devakṣatrasuto jajñe devanaḥ kṣatranandanaḥ ।। 33.44 ।।  
  
devanāt sa madhurjajñe yasya medhārthasambhavaḥ।  
madhoścāpi mahātejā manurmanuvaśastathā ।। 33.45 ।।  
  
nandanaśca mahātejā mahāpuruvaśastathā।  
āsīt puruvaśāt putraḥ purudvān puruṣottamaḥ ।। 33.46 ।।  
  
jajñe purudvataḥ putro bhadravatyāṃ purūdvahaḥ।  
aikṣākī tvabhavadbhāryā sattvastasyāmajāyata।  
sattvāt sattvaguṇo petaḥ sāttvataḥ kīrtivarddhanaḥ ।। 33.47 ।।  
  
imāṃ visṛṣṭiṃ vijñāya jyāmaghasya mahātmanaḥ।  
prajāvāneti sāyujyaṃ rājñaḥ somasya dhīmataḥ ।। 33.48 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahā purāṇe vāyuprokte jyāmaghavṛttāntakathanaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 33 ।। 


---
title: 034

---
          sūta uvāca।।  
sātvatī rūpasampannaṃ kauśalyā suṣuve sutam।  
bhajinaṃ bhajamānaṃ ca divyaṃ devāvṛdhaṃ nṛpam ।। 34.1 ।।  
  
andhakañca sahābhojaṃ vṛṣṇiñca yadunandanam।  
teṣāṃ hi sargāścatvāraḥ śrṛṇudhvaṃ vistareṇa vai ।। 34.2 ।।  
  
bhajamānasya śrṛñjayyāṃ bāhyaścopari bāhyakaḥ।  
śrṛñjayasya sute dve tu bāhyakaste udāvahat ।। 34.3 ।।  
  
tasya bhārye bhaginyau te prāsūteti sutān bahūn।  
nimiśca paṇavaścaiva vṛṣṇiḥ parapurañjayaḥ ।। 34.4 ।।  
  
ye bāhyakāryyaśrṛñjayyāṃ bhajamānādvijajñire।  
ayutāyutasāhasra śatajidatha vāmakaḥ ।। 34.5 ।।  
  
bāhyakāryyābhaginyāṃ ye bhajamānā dvijajñire।  
teṣāṃ devāvṛdho rājā cacāra paramaṃ tapaḥ ।। 34.6 ।।  
  
putraḥ sarvaguṇopeto mama bhūyāditi sma ha।  
saṃyojyātmānamevaṃ savarṇā sā jalamaspṛśat ।। 34.7 ।।  
  
sā copasparśanāttasya cakāra ṛṣimāpagā।  
kalyāṇañca narapatestasya sā nimnagottamā ।। 34.8 ।।  
  
cintayābhiparītāṅgā jagāmātha viniścayam।  
nādhigacchāmi tāṃ nārīṃ yasyāmevaṃvidhaḥ sutaḥ ।। 34.9 ।।  
  
bhavetsarvaguṇopeto rājño devāvṛdhasya hi।  
tasmādasya svayaṃ cāhaṃ bhavāmyadya sahavratā।  
jajñe tasyāḥ svayaṃ hasto bhāvastasya yatheritaḥ ।। 34.10 ।।  
  
atha bhūtvā kumārī tu sāvitrī paramaṃ vacaḥ।  
cintayāmāsa rājānaṃ tāmiyeṣa sa parthivaḥ ।। 34.11 ।।  
  
tasyāmādhatta garbhaṃ sa tejasvinamudāradhīḥ।  
atha sā navame māsi suṣuve saritāṃvarā ।। 34.12 ।।  
  
putraṃ sarvaguṇopetaṃ yathā devāvṛdhepsitaḥ।  
tatra vaṃśe purāṇajñā gāthāṃ gāyanti vai dvijāḥ ।। 34.13 ।।  
  
guṇān devāvṛdhasyāpi kīrttayanto mahātmanaḥ।  
yathaiva śrṛṇute dūrāt saṃpaśyati tathāntikāt ।। 34.14 ।।  
  
babhruḥ śreṣṭo manuṣyāṇāṃ devairdevāvṛdhaḥ samaḥ।  
puruṣāḥ pañcaṣaṣṭiśca sahasrāṇi ca saptatiḥ।  
ye'mṛtatvamanuprāptā babhrurdevāvṛdhādapi ।। 34.15 ।।  
  
yajvā dānapatirvīro brahmaṇyaḥ satya vāg budhaḥ।  
kīrttimāṃśca mahābhāgaḥ sāttvatānāṃ mahārathaḥ ।। 34.16 ।।  
  
tasyānvavāye sumahābhojayemārtikāvalāḥ।  
gāndhārī caiva mādrī ca vṛṣṇerbhāryye babhūvatuḥ ।। 34.17 ।।  
  
gāndhārī janayāmāsa sumitraṃ mitranandanam।  
mādrī yudhājitaṃ putraṃ sā tu vai devamīḍhuṣam ।। 34.18 ।।  
  
anamitraṃ sutañcaiva tāvubhau puruṣottamau।  
anamitrasuto nighno nighnasya dvau babhūvatuḥ ।। 34.19 ।।  
  
prasenaśca mahābhāgaḥ śakrajicca sutāvubhau।  
tasya śakrajitaḥ pūrvaḥ sakhā prāṇasamo'bhavat ।। 34.20 ।।  
  
sa kadācinniśāpāye rathena rathināṃvaraḥ।  
toyakūlādapaḥ spraṣṭumupasthātuṃ yayau ravim ।। 34.21 ।।  
  
tasyopatiṣṭhataḥ sūryo vivasvānagrataḥ sthitaḥ।  
aspaṣṭamūrtirbhagavāṃ stejomaṇḍalavān vibhuḥ ।। 34.22 ।।  
  
atha rājā vivasvantamuvāca sthitamagrataḥ।  
yathaiva vyomni paśyāmi tvāmahaṃ jyotiṣāmpate ।। 34.23 ।।  
  
tejomaṇḍalinañcaiva tathaivāpyagrataḥ sthitam।  
ko viśeṣo vivasvaṃste sākṣādupagatena vai ।। 34.24 ।।  
  
etacchrutvā sa bhagavān maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।  
svakaṇṭādavamucyātha babandha nṛpatestadā ।। 34.25 ।।  
  
tato vigrahavantaṃ taṃ dadarśa nṛpatistadā।  
pratimāmatha tāṃ dṛṣṭvā muhūrttaṃ kṛtavāṃstathā ।। 34.26 ।।  
  
tamatiprasthitaṃ bhūyo vivasvantaṃ sa śakrajit।  
provācāgnisavarṇaṃ tvaṃ yena lokān prayāsyati।  
tadaiva maṇiratnaṃ tanmāṃ bhavān dātumarhati ।। 34.27 ।।  
  
syamantakaṃ nāma maṇiṃ dattavāṃstasya bhāskaraḥ।  
sa tamābaddhya nagaraṃ praviveśa mahīpatiḥ ।। 34.28 ।।  
  
taṃ janāḥ paryadhāvanta sūryo'yaṃ gacchatīti ha।  
sabhāṃ vismāyayitvātha purīmantaḥpuraṃ tathā ।। 34.29 ।।  
  
taṃ prasenijite divyaṃ maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।  
dadau bhrātre narapatiḥ premṇā śakrajiduttamam ।। 34.30 ।।  
  
syamantako nāma maṇiryasya rāṣṭre sthito bhevat ।  
kālavarṣī ca parjanyo na ca vyādhibhayaṃ tadā ।। 34.31 ।।  
  
lipsāṃ cakre prasenāttu maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।  
govindo na ca taṃ lebhe śakto'pi na jahāra ca ।। 34.32 ।।  
  
kadā cinmṛgayāṃ yātaḥ prasenastena bhūṣitaḥ।  
syamantakakṛte siṃhādvadhaṃ prāptaḥ sudāruṇam ।। 34.33 ।।  
  
jāmbavānṛkṣarājastu taṃ siṃhaṃ nijaghāna vai ।  
ādāya ca maṇiṃ divyaṃ svaṃ bilaṃ praviveśa ha ।। 34.34 ।।  
  
tatkarma kṛṣṇasya tato vṛṣṇyandhakamahattarāḥ।  
maṇaugṛdhnuntu manvānāstameva viśaśaṅkire ।। 34.35 ।।  
  
mithyābhiśastiṃ tebhyastāṃ balavānarisūdanaḥ।  
amṛṣyamāṇo bhagavān vanaṃ sa vicacāra ha ।। 34.36 ।।  
  
sa tu prasenamṛgayāmacarattatra cāpyatha।  
prasenasya padaṃ gṛhya puruṣai rāptakāribhiḥ ।। 34.37 ।।  
  
ṛkṣavantaṃ girivaraṃ vindhyañca nagamuttamam।  
anveṣaṇapariśrāntaḥ sa dadarśa mahāmanāḥ ।। 34.38 ।।  
  
sāśvaṃ hataṃ prasenaṃ taṃ nāvindattatra vai maṇim।  
atha siṃhaḥ prasenasya śarīrasyāvidūrataḥ ।। 34.39 ।।  
  
ṛkṣeṇa nihato dṛṣṭaḥ pādaiṛkṣasya sūcitām।  
padairanveṣayāmāsa guhāmṛkṣasya yādavaḥ ।। 34.40 ।।  
  
mahatyatibile vāṇīṃ śuśrāva pramaderitām।  
dhātryā kumāramādāya sutaṃ jāmbavato dvijāḥ।  
prītimatyātha maṇinā mārodīrityudīritām ।। 34.41 ।।  
  
         ।।dhātryuvāca।।  
prasenamavadhīt siṃhaḥ siṃho jāmbavatā hataḥ।  
sukumāraka mārodīstava hyeṣa syamantakaḥ ।। 34.42 ।।  
  
vyaktīkṛtañca śabdaṃ taṃ tūrṇaṃ so'pi yayau bilam।  
apaśyacca vilābhyāśe prasenamavadāritam।। 34.43 ।।  
  
praviśya cāpi bhagavāstadṛkṣabilamañjasā।  
dadarśa ṛkṣarājānaṃ jāmbavantamudāradhīḥ ।। 34.44 ।।  
  
yuyudhe vāsudevastu bile jāmbavatā saha।  
bāhubhyāmeva govindo divasānekaviṃśatim ।। 34.45 ।।  
  
praviṣṭe ca bilaṃ kṛṣṇe vāsudeva puraḥsarāḥ ।  
punardvāravatīmetya hataṃ kṛṣṇaṃ nyavedayan ।। 34.46 ।।  
  
vāsudevastu nirjitya jāmbavantaṃ mahābalam।  
lebhe jāmbavatīṃ kanyāmṛkṣarājasya sammatām ।। 34.47 ।।  
  
bhagavattejasā grasto jāmbavān prasabhaṃ maṇim।  
sutāṃ jāmbavatīmāśu viṣvaksenāya dattavān ।। 34.48 ।।  
  
maṇiṃ syamantakaṃ caiva jagrāhātma viśuddhaye।  
anunīya ṛkṣarājaṃ niryayau ca tadā bilāt ।। 34.49 ।।  
  
evaṃ sa maṇimādāya viśoddhyātmānamātmanā।  
dadau satrājite taṃ vai maṇiṃ sātvatasannidhau ।। 34.50 ।।  
  
kanyāṃ punarjāmbavatīmuvāca madhusūdanaḥ।  
tasmānmithyābhiśāpāt sa vyamucyata janārdanaḥ ।। 34.51 ।।  
  
imāṃ mithyābhiśastiṃ yaḥ kṛṣṇasyeha vyapohitām।  
veda mithyābhiśasteḥ sa nābhiśasyati karhicit ।। 34.52 ।।  
  
daśa svasṛbhyo bhāryyābhyaḥ śatrajittaḥ śataṃ sutāḥ।  
khyātimantastrayasteṣāṃ bhaṅgakārastu pūrvvajaḥ।  
vīro vratapatiścaiva hyapasvāntaśca supriyaḥ ।। 34.53 ।।  
  
atha dvāravatī nāma bhaṅgakārasya suprajā।  
suṣuve sā kumārīstu tisro rūpaguṇānvitāḥ ।। 34.54 ।।  
  
satya bhāmottamā strīṇāṃ vratinīva dṛḍhavratā।  
tathā tapasvinī caiva pitā kṛṣṇasya tāṃ dadau ।। 34.55 ।।  
  
yattat satrājite kṛṣṇo maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।  
prādāttadāharadratnaṃ bhojena śatadhanvanā ।। 34.56 ।।  
  
tadā hi prārthayāmāsa satyabhāmāmaninditām।  
akrūro ratnamanvicchan maṇiñcaiva syamantakam ।। 34.57 ।।  
  
bhadrakāraṃ tato hatvā śatadhanvā mahābalaḥ।  
rātrau taṃ maṇimādāya tato'krūrāya dattavān ।। 34.58 ।।  
  
akrūrastu tadā ratnamādāya sa nararṣabhaḥ।  
samayaṃ kāraṇaṃ cakre bodhyo nānyaistvayetyuta ।। 34.59 ।।  
  
vayamabhyupapatsyāmaḥ kṛṣṇena tvaṃ pradharṣitaḥ।  
mama ca dvārakāḥ sarvā vaśe tiṣṭantyasaṃśayam ।। 34.60 ।।  
  
hate pitari duḥśārttā satyabhāmā yaśasvinī।  
prayayau rathamāruhya nagaraṃ vāraṇāvatam ।। 34.61 ।।  
  
satyabhāmā tu tadvṛttaṃ bhojasya śatadhanvanaḥ।  
bharturnivedya duḥkhārttā pārśvasthāśrūṇyavartayat ।। 34.62 ।।  
  
pāṇḍavānāntu dagdhānāṃ hariḥ kṛtvodakakriyām ।  
tulyārthe caiva bhrātṝṇāṃ niyojayati sātyakim ।। 34.63 ।।  
  
tata stvaritamāgamya dvārakāṃ madhusūdanaḥ।  
pūrvvajaṃ halinaṃ śrīmānidaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। 34.64 ।।  
  
hataḥ prasenaḥ siṃhena satrājicchatadhanvanā।  
syamantakamahaṃ mārge tasya prahara he prabho ।। 34.65 ।।  
  
tadāroha rathaṃ śīghraṃ bhojaṃ hatvā mahābalam।  
syamantako mahābāho tadāsmākaṃ bhaviṣyati ।। 34.66 ।।  
  
tataḥ pravṛtte yuddhe tu tumule bhojakṛṣṇayoḥ।  
śatadhanvā na cākrūramavaikṣat sarvato diśi ।। 34.67 ।।  
  
anaṣṭāśvāvarohantu kṛtvā bhojajanārdanau।  
śakto'pi sādhyādvārddhakyānnākrūro'bhyupapadyata ।। 34.68 ।।  
  
apayāne tato buddhiṃ bhūyaścakre bhayānvitaḥ।  
yojanānāṃ śataṃ sāgraṃ yayā ca pratyapadyata ।। 34.69 ।।  
  
vijñātahṛdayā nāma śatayojanagāminī।  
bhojasya vaḍhavādityo yayā kṛṣṇamayodhayat ।। 34.70 ।।  
  
pravṛddhavegā vaḍavā tvadhvanāṃ śatayojanam।  
dṛṣṭā rathagatistasya śatadhanvānamarddayat ।। 34.71 ।।  
  
tatastasya hayāste tu śramāt khedācca vai dvijāḥ।  
khamutpetū rathaprāṇāḥ kṛṣṇo rāmamathābravīt ।। 34.72 ।।  
  
tiṣṭhasveha mahābāho dṛṣṭadoṣā mayā hayāḥ।  
padybhāṃ gatvā hariṣyāmi maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam ।। 34.73 ।।  
  
padbhyāmeva tato gatvā śatadhanvānamacyutaḥ।  
mithilādhipatiṃ taṃ vai jaghāna paramāstravit ।। 34.74 ।।  
  
syamantakaṃ na cāpaśyaddhatvā bhojaṃ mahābalam।  
nivṛttaṃ cābravīt kṛṣṇaṃ ratnaṃ dehīti lāṅgalī ।। 34.75 ।।  
  
nāstīti kṛṣṇaścovāca tato rāmo ruṣānvitaḥ।  
dhikchabdamasakṛt pūrvvaṃ pratyuvāca janārddanam ।। 34.76 ।।  
  
bhrātṛtvānmarṣayāmyeṣa svasti te'stu vrajāmyaham।  
kṛtyaṃ na me drārakayā na tvayā na ca vṛṣṇibhiḥ ।। 34.77 ।।  
  
praviveśa tato rāmo mithilāmarimarddanaḥ।  
sarvvakāmairupahṛtairmaithilenaiva pūjitaḥ ।। 34.78 ।।  
  
etasminneva kāle tu babhrurmatimatāṃvaraḥ।  
nānārūpān kratūn sarvvānājahāra nirargalān ।। 34.79 ।।  
  
dīkṣāmayaṃ sakavacaṃ rakṣārthaṃ praviveśa ha।  
syamantakakṛte rājā gādhiputro mahāyaśāḥ ।। 34.80 ।।  
  
arthān ratnāni cāgryāṇi dravyāṇi vividhāni ca ।  
ṣaṣṭivarṣagate kāle yajñeṣu vinyayojayat ।। 34.81 ।।  
  
akrūrayajña ityete khyātāstasya mahātmanaḥ।  
bahvannadakṣiṇāḥ sarvve sarvvakāmapradāyinaḥ ।। 34.82 ।।  
  
atha duryyodhano rājā gatvā'tha mithilāṃ prabhuḥ।  
gadāśikṣāṃ tato divyāṃ balabhadrādavāptavān ।। 34.83।  
prasādya tu tato viprā vṛṣṇyandhakamahārathaiḥ।  
ānīto dvārakāmeva kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā ।। 34.84 ।।  
  
akrūramandhakaiḥ sārddhamupāyāt puruṣarṣabhaḥ।  
yuddhe hatvā tu śatrugnaṃ saha bandhumatā balī ।। 34.85 ।।  
  
śvaphalkatanayāyāntu narāyāṃ narasattamau।  
bhaṅgakārasya tanayo viśrutau sumahābalau ।। 34.86 ।।  
  
jajñāte'ndhakamukhyasya śatrughno bandhumāṃśca tau।  
vadhārthaṃ bhaṅgakārasya kṛṣṇo na prītimān bhavet ।। 34.87 ।।  
  
jñāti bhedabhayādbhītaḥ samupekṣitavāṃstathā।  
apayāte tathākrūre nāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ।। 34.88 ।।  
  
anāvṛṣṭyā hataṃ rāṣṭramabhavattadvaghodyatam।  
tataḥ prasādayāmāsurakrūraṃ kukurāndhakāḥ ।। 34.89 ।।  
  
punardvāravatīṃ prāpte tadā dānapatau tathā।  
pravavarṣa sahasrākṣaḥ kukṣau jalanidhestataḥ ।। 34.90 ।।  
  
kanyāñca vāsudevāya svasāraṃ śīlasammatām।  
akrūraḥ pradadau śrīmān prītyarthaṃ yadupuṅgavaḥ ।। 34.91 ।।  
  
ata vijñāya yogena kṛṣṇo babhrugataṃ maṇim।  
sabhāmadhye tadā prāha tamakrūraṃ janārdanaḥ ।। 34.92 ।।  
  
yacca ratnaṃ maṇivaraṃ tava hastagataṃ prabho।  
tatprayacchasva mānārha vimatiñcātra mā kṛthāḥ ।। 34.93 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭivarṣagate kāle yadroṣo'bhūttadā mama।  
susaṃrūḍhaḥ sakṛt prāptastatkālāśritya sa mahān ।। 34.94 ।।  
  
tataḥ kṛṣṇasya vacanāt sarvvasātvatasaṃsadi।  
pradadau taṃ maṇiṃ babhrurakleśena mahāmatiḥ ।। 34.95 ।।  
  
tata ārjjavasaṃprāptababhruhastādarindamaḥ।  
dadau prahṛṣṭamanasā taṃ maṇiṃ babhrave punaḥ ।। 34.96 ।।  
  
sa kṛṣṇahastāt saṃprāpya maṇiratnaṃ syamantakam।  
ābaddhya gāndinīputro virarājāṃśumāniva ।। 34.97 ।।  
  
imāṃ mithyābhiśastiṃ yo viśuddhāmapi cottamām ।  
veda mithyābhi śastiṃ sa na vrajecca kathañcana ।। 34.98 ।।  
  
animitrācchinirjajñe kaniṣṭādvṛṣṇinandanāt ।। 34.99 ।।  
  
satyavāk satyasampannaḥ satyakastasya cātmajaḥ।  
sātyakiryuyudhānasya tasya bhūtiḥ suto'bhavat ।। 34.100 ।।  
  
bhūteryugandharaḥ putra iti bhautyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।  
jajñāte tanayau pṛśreḥ śvaphalkaścitrakaśca yaḥ ।। 34.101 ।।  
  
śvaphalkastu mahārājo dharmātmā yatra varttate।  
nāsti vyādhibhayaṃ tatra na cāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ tathā ।। 34.102 ।।  
  
kadācit kāśirājasya vibhostu dvijasattamāḥ।  
trīṇi varṣāṇi viṣaye nāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ।। 34.103 ।।  
  
sa tatra vāsayāmāsa śvaphalkaṃ paramārcitam।  
śvaphalkaparivāsena prāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ।। 34.104 ।।  
  
śvaphalkaḥ kāśirājasya sutāṃ bhāryāmaninditām।  
gāndinīṃ nāma gāṃ sā hi dadau viprāya nityaśaḥ ।। 34.105 ।।  
  
sā māturudarasthā vai bahuvarṣa śatān kila।  
vasati sma na vai jajñe sarbhasthāntāṃ pitābravīt ।। 34.106 ।।  
  
jāyasva śīghraṃ bhadrante kimarthaṃ cāpi tiṣṭhasi।  
provāca cainaṃ garbha sthā sā kanyā gaurdine dine ।। 34.107 ।।  
  
yadi dattā tadā syāṃ hi yadi syāmīhatāṃ pitaḥ।  
tathetyuvāca tāṃ tasyāḥ pitā kāmamapūpurat ।। 34.108 ।।  
  
dātā yajvā ca śūraśca śrutavānatithipriyaḥ।  
tasyāḥ putraḥ smṛto'krūraḥ śvaphalko bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ।। 34.109 ।।  
  
upamaṅgustathā maṅgurmṛduraścārimejayaḥ।  
girirakṣastatā yakṣaḥ śatrughno vārimarddanaḥ ।। 34.110 ।।  
  
dharmabhṛcca śrṛṣṭacayo vargamocastathāparaḥ।  
āvāhaprativāhau ca vasudevā varāṅganā ।। 34.111 ।।  
  
akrūrādugrasenyāntu sutau dvau kulanandinau।  
devaścānupadevaśca jajñāte devasaṃmitau ।। 34.112 ।।  
  
citrakasyābhavan putrāḥ pṛthurvipṛthureva ca।  
aśvagrīvo'śvabāhuśca supārśvakagaveṣaṇau ।। 34.113 ।।  
  
ariṣṭanemiraśvaśca suvarmā varmacarmabhṛt ।  
abhūmirbahubhūmiśca śraviṣṭāśravaṇe striyau ।। 34.114 ।।  
  
satyakāt kāśiduhitā lebhe sā caturaḥ sutān।  
kakudaṃ bhajamānañca śamīkabalabarhiṣau ।। 34.115 ।।  
  
kakudasya suto vṛṣṭirvṛṣṭestu tanayo'bhavat।  
kapotaromā tasyātha revato'bhavadātmajaḥ ।। 34.116 ।।  
  
tasyāsīttumburusakhā vidvān putro'bhavatkila।  
khyāyate yasya nāmnā sa candanodakadundubhiḥ ।। 34.117 ।।  
  
tasmāccābhijitaḥ putra utpannastu punarvasuḥ।  
aśvamedhantu putrārthe ājahāra narottamaḥ ।। 34.118 ।।  
  
tasya madhye'tirātrasya sadomadhyātsamutthitam।  
tatastu vidvān dharmajño dātā yajvā punarvasuḥ ।। 34.119 ।।  
  
tasyāpi putramithunaṃ bāhubāṇājitaḥ kila।  
āhukaścāhukī caiva khyātau matimatāṃvarau ।। 34.120 ।।  
  
imāṃścodāharantyatra ślokān prati tamāhukam।  
sopāsaṅgānukarṣāṇāṃ sadhvajānāṃ varūthinām ।। 34.121 ।।  
  
rathānāṃ meghaghoṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi daśaiva tu।  
nāsatyavādī tvāsīttu nāyajvā nāsahasradaḥ ।। 34.122 ।।  
  
nāśucirnāpyadharmātmā nāvidvānna kṛśo'bhavat।  
āhukasya dhṛtiḥ putra ityevamanu śuśrumaḥ ।। 34.123 ।।  
  
śvetena paricāreṇa kiśorapratimān hayān।  
aśītiyuktaniyutānyāhukapratimo'vrajat ।। 34.124 ।।  
  
pūrvasyāndiśi nāgānāṃ bhojasya pratirejire।  
rūpyakāñcanakakṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇyekaviṃśatiḥ ।। 34.125 ।।  
  
tāvantyeva sahasrāṇi uttarasyāntathā diśi।  
bhūmipālasya bhojasya uttiṣṭet kiṅkiṇī kila ।। 34.126 ।।  
  
āhukaścāhukāndhāya svasāraṃ tvāhukīndadau।  
āhukāndhasya duhitā dvau putrau sambabhūvatuḥ ।। 34.127 ।।  
  
devakaścograsenaśca devagarbhasamāvubhau ।  
devakasya sutā vīrā jajñire tridaśopamāḥ ।। 34.128 ।।  
  
devānāmapi devaśca sudevo devarañjitā।  
teṣāṃ svasāraḥ saptāsan vasudevāya saṃdadau ।। 34.129 ।।  
  
vṛkadevopadevā ca tathānyā devarakṣitā।  
śrīdevā śāntidevā ca mahādevā tathāparā ।। 34.130 ।।  
  
saptamī devakī tāsāṃ sunāmā cārudarśanā।  
navograsenasya sutāḥ kaṃsasteṣāntu pūrvajaḥ ।। 34.131 ।।  
  
nyagrodhaśca sunāmā ca kadvaśaṃkuśca bhūmayaḥ।  
sūtanū rāṣṭrapālaśca yuddhatuṣṭaḥ supuṣṭimān ।। 34.132 ।।  
  
teṣāṃ svasāraḥ pañcaiva karmadharmavatī tathā।  
śatāṅkrū rāṣṭrāpālā ca kaṅvā caiva varāṅganā ।। 34.133 ।।  
  
ugraseno mahāpatyo vikhyātaḥ kukurodbhavaḥ।  
kukurāṇāmimaṃ vaṃśaṃ dhārayannamitaujasām।  
ātmano vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ prajāvāṃśca bhavennaraḥ ।। 34.134 ।।  
  
bhajamānasya putrastu rathimukhyo vidūrathaḥ।  
rājyādhidevaḥ śūraśca viduraśca suto'bhavat ।। 34.135 ।।  
  
tasya śūrasya tu sutā jajñire balavattarāḥ ।  
vātaścaiva nivātaśca śoṇitaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। 34.136 ।।  
  
śamī ca gadavarmā ca nidātaḥ śakraśakrajit।  
śamiputraḥ pratikṣiptaḥ pratikṣiptasya cātmajaḥ ।। 34.137 ।।  
  
svayambhojaḥ svayambhojāddhṛdikaḥ sambabhūva ha।  
hṛdikasya sutāstvāsan daśa bhīmaparākramāḥ ।। 34.138 ।।  
  
kṛtavarmā kṛtasteṣāṃ śatadhanvā tu madhyamaḥ।  
devārhaśca vanārhaśca bhiṣag dvaitarathaśca yaḥ ।। 34.139 ।।  
  
sudāntaśca dhiyāntaśca nakavān kanakodbhavaḥ।  
devārhasya suto vidvān jajñe kambalabarhiṣaḥ ।। 34.140 ।।  
  
asamaujāḥ sutastasya sumahaujāśca viśrutaḥ।  
ajāvaputrāya tataḥ pradadāvasamaujase।  
sudaṃṣṭrañca surūpañca kṛṣṇa ityandhakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 34. 141 ।।  
  
andhakānāmimaṃ vaṃśaṃ kīrttayānastu nityaśaḥ।  
ātmāno vipulaṃ vaṃśaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। 34.142 ।।  
  
asmakyāṃ janayāmāsa śūro vai devamānuṣim।  
māṣyāntu janayāmāsa śūro vai devamīḍhuṣam ।। 34.143 ।।  
  
bhāṣyāntu jajñire śūrādbhojāyāṃ puruṣā daśa।  
vasudevo mahābāhuḥ pūrvamānakadundubhiḥ ।। 34.144 ।।  
  
jajñe tasya prasūtasya dundubhiḥ prāṇadaddivi।  
ānakānāñca saṃhrādaḥ sumahānabhavaddivi ।। 34.145 ।।  
  
papāta puṣpavarṣañca śūrasya bhavane mahat।  
manuṣyaloke kṛtsne'pi rūpe nāsti samo bhuvi ।। 34.146 ।।  
  
yasyāsīt puruṣāgryasya kīrttiścandramaso yathā।  
devabhāgastato jajñe tato devaśravāḥ punaḥ ।। 34.147 ।।  
  
anādṛṣṭikaḍaścaiva nandanaścaiva bhṛñjinaḥ।  
śyāmaḥ śamīko gaṇḍūṣaḥ catasrastu varāṅganāḥ ।। 34.148 ।।  
  
pṛthā ca śrutavedā ca śrutakīrttiḥ śrutaśravāḥ।  
rājādhidevī ca tathā pañcaitā vīramātaraḥ ।। 34.149 ।।  
  
pṛthāṃ duhitaraṃ cakre kunti stāṃ pāṇḍurāvahat।  
anapatyāya vṛddhāya kuntibhojāya tāṃ dadau ।। 34.150 ।।  
  
tasmāt kuntīti vikhyātā kuntībhojātmajā pṛthā।  
kuruvīraḥ pāṇḍumukhyastasmādbhāryāmavindata ।। 34.151 ।।  
  
pṛthā jajñe tataḥ putrān trīnagnisamatejasaḥ।  
loke'pratirathān vīrān śakratulyaparākramān ।। 34.152 ।।  
  
dharmādyudhiṣṭiraṃ putraṃ mārutācca vṛkodaram।  
īndrāddhanañjayañcaiva pṛthā putrānajījanat ।। 34.153 ।।  
  
mādravatyāntu janitāvāśvināviti viśrutam।  
nakulaḥ sahadevaśca rūpasattvaguṇānvitau ।। 34.154 ।।  
  
jajñe ca śrutadevāyāṃ tanayo vṛddhaśarmaṇaḥ।  
karūṣādhipatirvīro dantavakro mahābalaḥ ।। 34.155 ।।  
  
kaikeyāṃ śrutakīrtyāntu jajñe santardanaḥ punaḥ।  
cekitānabṛhatkṣatrau tathaivānyau mahābalau ।। 34.156 ।।  
  
vindānuvindāvāvantyau bhrātarau sumahābalau।  
śrutaśravāyāṃ caidyastu śiśupālo babhūva ha ।। 34.157 ।।  
  
damaghoṣasya rājarṣeḥ putro vikhyātapauruṣaḥ।  
yaḥ purāsīddaśagrīvaḥ saṃbabhūvārimardanaḥ ।। 34.158 ।।  
  
yaduśravānujastasya rujakanyo'nujastathā।  
patnyastu vasudevasya trayodaśa varāṅganāḥ ।। 34.159 ।।  
  
pauravī rohiṇī caiva madirā cāparā tathā।  
tathaiva bhadrā vaiśākhī devakī saptamī tathā ।। 34.160 ।।  
  
sugandhirvanarājī ca dve cānye paricārike।।  
rohiṇī pauravī caiva vālmīkasyātmajābhavat ।। 34.161 ।।  
  
jyeṣṭā patnī mahābhāgā dayitānakadundubheḥ ।  
jyeṣṭhaṃ lebhe sutaṃ rāmaṃ sāraṇaṃ niśavaṃ tathā ।। 34.162 ।।  
  
durddamaṃ damanaṃ śubhraṃ piṇḍārakakuśītakau।  
citrāṃ nāma kumārīñca rohiṇyaṣṭau vyajāyata ।। 34.163 ।।  
  
pautrau rāmasya jajñāte vijñātau niśitotsukau।  
pārśvī ca pārśvanandī ca śiśuḥ satyadhṛtistathā ।। 34.164 ।।  
  
mandabāhyo'tha rāmāṇagirikau gira eva ca।  
śuklagulmeti gulmaśca daridrāntaka eva ca ।। 34.165 ।।  
  
kumāryaścāpi pañcādyā nāmatastā nibodhata।  
arciṣmatī sunandā ca surasā suvacāstathā ।। 34.166 ।।  
  
tathā śatabalā caiva sāraṇasya sutāstvimāḥ।  
bhadrāśvo bhadraguptiśca bhadravighnastathaiva ca ।। 34.167 ।।  
  
bhadrabāhurbhadraratho bhadrakalpastathaiva ca।  
supārśvakaḥ kīrttimāṃśca rohitāśvaśca bhadrajaḥ ।। 34.168 ।।  
  
durmmadaścābhibhūtaśca rohiṇyāḥ kulajāḥ smṛtāḥ ।  
nandopanantadau mitraśca kukṣimitrastathācalaḥ ।। 34.169 ।।  
  
citropa citre kanye ca sthitaḥ puṣṭirathāparaḥ।  
madirāyāḥ sutā hyete sudevo'tha vijajñire ।। 34.170 ।।  
  
upabimbo'tha bimbaśca sattvadantamahaujasau।  
catvāra ete vikhyātā bhadrāputrā mahābalāḥ ।। 34.171 ।।  
  
vaiśākhyāṃ samadācchauriḥ putraṃ kauśikamuttamam।  
devakyāṃ jajñire śauriḥ suṣeṇaḥ kīrtimānapi ।। 34.172 ।।  
  
tadayo bhadrasenaśca yajudāyaśca pañcamaḥ।  
ṣaṣṭo bhadravidekaśca kaṃsaḥ sarvāñjaghāna tān ।। 34.173 ।।  
  
atha tasyāmavasthāyāmāyuṣmān saṃbabhūva ha।  
loka nāthaḥ punarviṣṇuḥ pūrvakṛṣṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। 34.174 ।।  
  
anujātā'bhavat kṛṣṇā subhadrā bhadrabhāṣiṇī।  
kṛṣṇā subhadreti punarvyākhyātā vṛṣṇinandinī ।। 34.175 ।।  
  
subhadrāyāṃ rathī pārthādabhimanyurajāyata।  
vasudevasya bhāryāsu mahābhāgāsu saptasu।  
ye putrā jajñireśūrā nāmatastānnibodhata ।। 34.176 ।।  
  
ato'sya saha devāyāṃ śūro jajñe'bhayāsakhaḥ।  
śārṅgadevājanattambuṃ śaurī jajñe kulodvaham ।। 34.177 ।।  
  
upasaṅgaṃ vasuñcāpi tanayau devarakṣitau।  
evaṃ daśa sutāstasya kaṃsastānapyaghātayat ।। 34.178 ।।  
  
vijayaṃ rojanañcaiva varddhamānaṃ tathaiva ca।  
etān sarvvān mahābhāgānupadevā vyajāyata ।। 34.179 ।।  
  
svagāhavaṃ mahātmānaṃ vṛka devī tvajāyata ।  
āgāhī ca svasā caiva surūpā śiśirāyiṇī ।। 34.180 ।।  
  
saptamaṃ devakīputraṃ sunāsā suṣuve bhuvam।  
gaveṣaṇaṃ mahābhāgaṃ saṅgrāme citra yodhinam ।। 34.181 ।।  
  
śrāddhadevaṃ purā yena vane viracitā dvijāḥ।  
śaibyāyāmadadacchauriḥ putraṃ kauśikamavyayam ।। 34.182 ।।  
  
sugandhī vanarājī ca śaurerāstāṃ parigrahaḥ।  
puṇḍraśca kapilaścaiva vasudevātmajau hi tau।  
tayo rājā'bhavat puṇḍraḥ kapilastu vanaṃ yayo ।। 34.183 ।।  
  
tasyāṃ samabhavadvīro vasudevātmajo balī।  
rājā nāma niṣādo'sau prathamaḥ sa dhanurddharaḥ ।। 34.184 ।।  
  
vikhyāto devarātasya mahābhāgaḥ suto'bhavat।  
paṇḍitānāṃ mataṃ prāhurdevaśravasamudbhavam ।। 34.185 ।।  
  
asmakyāṃ labhate putramanādṛṣṭiṃ yaśasvinam।  
nivarttaḥ śakraśatrughnaṃ śrāddhadevaṃ mahābalam ।। 34.186 ।।  
  
ajāyata śrāddhadevo niṣadhādiryataḥ śrutaḥ।  
ekalavyo mahāvīryo niṣādaiḥ parivarddhitaḥ ।। 34.187 ।।  
  
gaṇḍūṣāyānapatyāya kṛṣṇastuṣṭo'dadat sutau।  
cārudeṣṇañca sāmbañca kṛtāstrau śastalakṣaṇau ।। 34.188 ।।  
  
tantijastantimālaśca svaputrau kanakasya tu।  
vastāvanestvaputrāya vasudevaḥ pratāpavān।  
sautirdadau sutaṃ vīraṃ śauriṃ kauśikameva ca ।। 34.189 ।।  
  
tapāśca kodhanuścaiva virajāḥ śyāmasṛñjimau।  
anapatyo'bhavacchyāmaḥ śyāmakastu vanaṃ yayau।  
jugupsamāno bhojatvaṃ rājarṣitvamavāpnuyāt ।। 34.190 ।।  
  
ya idaṃ janma kṛṣṇasya paṭhate niyatavrataḥ।  
śrāvayedbrāhmaṇañcāpi sumahatsukhamāpnuyāt ।। 34.191 ।।  
  
devadevo mahātejāḥ pūrvvaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।  
vihārārthaṃ manuṣyeṣu jajñe nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 34.192 ।।  
  
devakyāṃ vasudevena tapasā puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ।  
caturbāhuḥ sa vijñeyo divyarūpaḥ śriyānvitaḥ ।। 34.193 ।।  
  
prakāśo bhagavān yogī kṛṣṇo mānuṣamāgataḥ।  
avyakto'vyaktaliṅgasthaḥ sa eva bhagavān prabhuḥ ।। 34.194 ।।  
  
nārāyaṇo yataścakre prabhavaṃ cāvyayo hi saḥ।  
devo nārāyaṇo bhūtvā harirāsītsanātanaḥ ।। 34.195 ।।  
  
yo'sṛjaccādipuruṣaṃ purā cakre prajāpatim।  
aditerapi putratvametya yādavanandanaḥ।  
devo viṣṇuriti khyātaḥ śakrādavarajo'bhavat ।। 34.196 ।।  
  
prasādajaṃ yasya vibhoradityāḥ putrakāraṇam।  
vadhārthaṃ suraśatrūṇāṃ daityadānavarakṣasām ।। 34.197 ।।  
  
yayātivaṃśajasyātha vasudevasya dhīmataḥ।  
kulaṃ puṇyaṃ yataḥ karma bheje nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 34.198 ।।  
  
sāgarāḥ samakampanta celuśca dharaṇīdharāḥ।  
jajvaluścāgnihotrāṇi jāyamāne janārdane ।। 34.199 ।।  
  
śivāśca pravavurvātāḥ praśāntimabhavadrajaḥ।  
jyotīṃṣyabhyadhikaṃ rejurjāyamāne janārdane ।। 34.200 ।।  
  
abhijinnāma nakṣatraṃ jayantī nāma śarvarī।  
muhūrtto vijayo nāma yatra jāto janārdanaḥ ।। 34.201 ।।  
  
avyaktaḥ śāśvataḥ kṛṣṇo harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ।  
jāyate smaiva bhagavān nayanairmohayan prajāḥ ।। 34.202 ।।  
  
ākāśāt puṣpavṛṣṭīśca vavarṣa tridaśeśvaraḥ।  
gīrbhirmaṅgalayuktābhiḥ stuvanto madhusūdanam।  
maharṣayaḥ sagandharvā upatasthuḥ sahasraśaḥ ।। 34.203 ।।  
  
vasudevastu taṃ rātrau jātaṃ putramadhokṣajam।  
śrīvatsalakṣaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā divi divyaiḥ sulakṣaṇaiḥ।  
uvāca vasudevaḥ svaṃ rūpaṃ saṃhara vai prabho ।। 34.204 ।।  
  
bhīto'haṃ kaṃsatastāta etadeva bravīmyaham।  
mama putrā hatāstena jyeṣṭāste'dbhutadarśanāḥ ।। 34.205 ।।  
  
vasudevavacaḥ śrutvā rūpaṃ sa hṛtavān prabhuḥ।  
anujñātaḥ pitā tvenaṃ nandagopagṛhaṃ gataḥ।  
ugrasenamate tiṣṭhan yaśodāyai tadā dadau ।। 34.206 ।।  
  
tulyakālantu garbhiṇyau yaśodā devakī tathā।  
yaśodā nandagopasya patnī sā nandagopateḥ ।। 34.207 ।।  
  
yāmeva rajanīṃ kṛṣṇo jajñe vṛṣṇikulaprabhuḥ।  
tāmeva rajanīṃ kanyāṃ yaśodāpi vyajāyata ।। 34.208 ।।  
  
taṃ jātaṃ rakṣamāṇastu vasudevo mahāyaśāḥ।  
prādāt putraṃ yaśodāyai kanyāntu jagṛhe svayam ।। 34.209 ।।  
  
dattvainaṃ nandagopasya rakṣamāmiti cābravīt।  
sutaste sarvvakalyāṇo yādavānāṃ bhaviṣyati।  
ayaṃ sa garbho devakyā asmatkleśān haniṣyati ।। 34.210 ।।  
  
ugrasenātmajāyāñca kanyāmānakadundubheḥ।  
nivedayāmāsa tadā kanyeti śubhalakṣaṇā ।। 34.211 ।।  
  
svāsāyāṃ tanayaṃ kaṃso jātaṃ naivāvadhārayat।  
atha tāmapi duṣṭātmā hyutsasarja mudānvitaḥ ।। 34.212 ।।  
  
hatā vai yā yadā kanyā japatyeṣa vṛthāmatiḥ।  
kanyā sā vavṛdhe tatra vṛṣṇisadmani pūjitā ।। 34.213 ।।  
  
putravatparipālyanto devā devān yathā tadā ।  
tāmeva vidhinotpannāmāhuḥ kanyāṃ prajāpatim ।। 34.214 ।।  
  
ekādaśā tu jajñe vai rakṣārthaṃ keśavasya ha।  
tāṃ vai sarve sumanasaḥ pūjayiṣyanti yādavāḥ।  
devadevo divyavapuḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃrakṣito'nayā ।। 34.215 ।।  
  
          ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
kimarthaṃ vasudevasya bhojaḥ kaṃso narādhipaḥ।  
jaghāna putrān bālān vai tanno vyākhyātumarhasi ।। 34.216 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
śrṛṇudhvaṃ vai yathā kaṃsaḥ putrānānakadundubheḥ।  
jātāñjātāñciśūn sarvvān niṣpipeṣa vṛthāmatiḥ ।। 34.217 ।।  
  
bhayādyathā mahābāhurjātaḥ kṛṣṇo vivāsitaḥ।  
tathā ca goṣu govindaḥ saṃvṛddha- puruṣottamaḥ ।। 34.218 ।।  
  
uktaṃ hi kila devakyā vasudevasya dhīmataḥ ।  
sārathyaṃ kṛtavān kaṃso yuvarājastadā'bhavat ।। 34.219 ।।  
  
tato'ntarikṣe vāgāsīddivyā bhūtasya kasyacit।  
kaṃso yayā sadā bhītaḥ puṣkalā lokasākṣiṇī ।। 34.220 ।।  
  
yāmetāṃ vahase kaṃsa rathena parakāraṇāt।  
asyā yaḥ saptamo garbhaḥ sa te mṛtyurbhaviṣyati ।। 34.221 ।।  
  
tāṃ śrutvā vyathito vāṇīṃ tadā kaṃso vṛthāmatiḥ।  
niṣkramya khaḍgaṃ tāṃ kanyāṃ hantukāmo'bhavattadā ।। 34.222 ।।  
  
tamuvāca mahābāhurvasudevaḥ pratāpavān।  
ugrasenātmajaṃ kaṃsaṃ sauhṛdātpraṇayena ca ।। 34.223 ।।  
  
nastriyaṃ kṣatriyo jātu hantumarhati kaścana।  
upāyaḥ paridṛṣṭo'tra mayā yādavanandana ।। 34.224 ।।  
  
yo'syāḥ sambhavate garbhaḥ saptamaḥ pṛthivī pate।  
tamahante prayacchāmi tatra kuryyā yathākramam ।। 34.225 ।।  
  
tvaṃ tvidānīṃ yatheṣṭatvaṃ vartethā bhūridakṣiṇa।  
sarvānasyāstu vai garbhān satyaṃ neṣyāmi te vaśam ।। 34.226 ।।  
  
evaṃ mithyā naraśreṣṭha vāgeṣā na bhaviṣyati।  
evamukto'nunītaḥ sa jagrāha tanayāṃstadā ।। 34.227 ।।  
  
vasudevaśca tāṃ bhāryyāmavāpya mudito'bhavat।  
kaṃsaścāsyāvadhīt putrān pāpakarmmā vṛthāmatiḥ ।। 34.228 ।।  
  
        ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
  
ka eṣa vasudevaśca devakī ca yaśasvinī।  
nandagopastu kastveṣa yaśodā ca mahāyaśāḥ।  
yo viṣṇuṃ janayāmāsa yā cainaṃ cābhyavarddhayat ।। 34.229 ।।  
  
           sūta ūvāca।।  
puruṣāḥ kaśyapasyāsannādityāstu striyāstathā।  
atha kāmān mahābāhurdevakyāḥ samavarddhayat ।। 34.230 ।।  
  
acarat sa mahīṃ devaḥ praviṣṭo mānuṣīṃ tanum।  
mohayan sarvabhūtāni yogātmā yogamāyayā ।। 34.231 ।।  
  
naṣṭe dharmme tadā jajñe viṣṇurvṛṣṇikule svayam।  
kartuṃ dharmmavyavasthānamasurāṇāṃ praṇāśanam ।। 34.232 ।।  
  
āhṛtā rukmiṇī kanyā satyā nagnajitastadā।  
sātrājitī satyabhāmā jāmbavatyapi rohiṇī ।। 34.233 ।।  
  
śaibyā sudevī mādrī ca suśīlā nāma cāparā।  
kālindī mitravindā ca lakṣmaṇā jālavāsinī ।। 34.234 ।।  
  
evamādīni devānāṃ sahasrāṇi ca ṣoḍaśa।  
caturddaśa tu ye proktā gaṇāścāpsarasāṃ divi ।  
vicintya devaiḥ śakreṇa viśiṣṭāstviha preṣitāḥ ।। 34.235 ।।  
  
patnyarthaṃ vāsudevasya utpannā rājaveśmasu।  
etāḥ patnyo mahābhāgā viṃṣvaksenasya viśrutāḥ ।। 34.236 ।।  
  
pradyumnaścārudeṣṇaśca sudeṣṇaḥ śarabhastathā।  
cāruśca cārubhadraśca bhadracārustathā'paraḥ ।। 34.237 ।।  
  
cāruvindhyaśca rukmiṇyāṃ kanyā cārumatī tathā।  
sānurbhānustathākṣaśca rohito mantrayastathā ।। 34.238 ।।  
  
jarāndhakastāmravakṣā bhaumariśca jarandhamaḥ।  
catasro jajñire teṣāṃ svasāro garuḍadhvajāt ।। 34.239 ।।  
  
bhānurbhaumarikā caiva tāmraparṇī jarandhamā।  
satyabhāmāsutānetāñjāmbavatyāḥ prajāḥ śrṛṇu ।। 34.240 ।।  
  
bhadraśca bhadraguptaśca bhadravindrastathaiva ca।  
saptabāhuśca vikhyātaḥ kanyā bhadrāvatī tathā।  
sambodhanī ca vikhyātā jñeyā jāmbavatīsutāḥ ।। 34.241 ।।  
  
saṃgrāmajicca śatajit ta na ca sahasrajit।  
ete putrāḥ sudevyāśca viṣvaksenasya kīrttitāḥ ।। 34.242 ।।  
  
vṛko vṛkāśvo vṛkajidvṛjinī ca surāṅganā।  
mitrabāhuḥ sunīthaśca nāgnajityāḥ prajāstviha ।। 34.243 ।।  
  
evamādīni putrāṇāṃ saha srāṇi nibodhata।  
prayutantu samākhyātaṃ vāsudevasya ye sutāḥ ।। 34.244 ।।  
  
ayutāni tathāṣṭau ca śūrā raṇaviśāradāḥ।  
janārdanasya vaṃśo vaḥ kīrttito'yaṃ yathātatham ।। 34.245 ।।  
  
bṛhatī nartakonneyī sunaye saṅgatā tathā ।  
kanyā sā bṛhaducchasya śauneyasya mahātmanaḥ ।। 34.246 ।।  
  
tasyāḥ putrāstu vikhyātā strayaḥ samitiśobhanāḥ ।  
aṅgadaḥ kumudaḥ śvetaḥ kanyā śvetā tathaiva ca ।। 34.247 ।।  
  
avagāhaśca citraśca śūraścitravaraśca yaḥ।  
citrasenaḥ sutaścāsya kanyā citravatī tathā ।। 34.248 ।।  
  
tumbaśca tumbabāṇaśca janastambaśca tāvubhau।  
upāṅgasya smṛtau dvau tu vajrāraḥ kṣipra eva ca ।। 34.249 ।।  
  
bhūrīndraseno bhūriśca gaveṣasya sutāvubhau ।  
yudhiṣṭirasya kanyā tu sutanurnāma viśrutā ।। 34.250 ।।  
  
tasyāmaśvasuto jajñe vajro nāma mahāyaśāḥ।  
vajrasya pratibāhustu sucārustasya cātmajaḥ ।। 34.251 ।।  
  
kāśmā supārśvaṃ tanayaṃ jajñe sāmbā tarasvinam।  
tisraḥ koṭyastu putrāṇāṃ yādavānāṃ mahātmanām ।। 34.252 ।।  
  
ṣaṣṭiṃśatasahasrāṇi vīryyavanto mahābalāḥ।  
devāṃśāḥ sarvva eveha utpannāste mahaujasaḥ ।। 34.253 ।।  
  
daivāsure hatā ye ca asurā vai mahātapāḥ।  
ihotpannā manuṣyeṣu bādhante sarvvamānavān ।  
teṣāmutsādanārthantu utpannā yādave kule ।। 34.254 ।।  
  
kulāni daśa caikañca yādavānāṃ mahātmanām।  
sarvvamakakulaṃ yadvadvarttate vaiṣṇave kule ।। 34.255 ।।  
  
viṣṇusteṣāṃ pramāṇe ca prabhutve ca vyavasthitaḥ ।  
nideśasthāyibhistasya baddhyante sarvamānuṣāḥ ।। 34.256 ।।  
  
iti prasūtirvṛṣṇīnāṃ samāsavyāsayogataḥ।  
kīrttitā kīrttanāccaiva kīrttisiddhimabhīpsitām ।। 34.257 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte viṣṇuvaṃśānukīrttanaṃ nāma catustriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 34 ।। 


---
title: 035

---
manuṣyaprakṛtīn devān kīrtyamānānnibodhata ।  
saṅkarṣaṇo vāsudevaḥ pradyumnaḥ sāmba eva ca ।। 35.1 ।।  
aniruddhaśca pañcaite vaṃśavīrāḥ prakīrttitāḥ।  
saptarṣayaḥ kuberaśca yakṣo maṇivarastathā ।। 35.2 ।।  
śālakī badaraścaiva vidvān dhanvantaristathā।  
nandinaśca mahādevaḥ śālaṅkāyana ucyate।  
ādidevastadā jiṣṇurebhiśca saha daivataiḥ ।। 35.3 ।।  
           ।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
viṣṇuḥ kimarthaṃ sambhūtaḥ smṛtāḥ sambhūtayaḥ kati।  
bhaviṣyāḥ kati vānye tu prādurbhāvā mahātmanaḥ ।। 35.4 ।।  
brahmakṣetre yugānteṣu kimarthamiha jāyate ।  
punaḥ punarmmanuṣyeṣu tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ।। 35.5 ।।  
vistareṇaiva sarvāṇi karmmāṇi ripughātinaḥ।  
śrotumicchāmahe samyag dehaiḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ ।। 35.6 ।।  
karmmaṇāmānupūrvyañca prādurbhāvāśca ye prabho ।  
yā cāsya prakṛtiḥ sūta tāścāsmān vaktumarhasi ।। 35.7 ।।  
kathaṃ sa bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sureṣvariniṣūdanaḥ।  
vasudevakule dhīmān vāsudevatvamāgataḥ ।। 35.8 ।।  
amaraiḥ sūta kiṃ puṇyaṃ puṇyakṛdbhiralaṃkṛtam।  
devalokaṃ samutsṛjya martyalokamihāgataḥ ।। 35.9 ।।  
devamānuṣayornetā bhūrbhuvaḥprasavo hariḥ।  
kimarthaṃ divyamātmānaṃ mānuṣe samaveśayat ।। 35.10 ।।  
yaścakraṃ vartayatyeko manuṣyāṇāṃ manomayam।  
manuṣye sa kathaṃ buddhiṃ cakre cakrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।। 35.11 ।।  
gopāyanaṃ yaḥ kurute jagatāṃ sārvvalaukikam।  
sa kathaṃ gāṃ gato viṣṇurgopamanvakarotprabhuḥ ।। 35.12 ।।  
mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā yo dadāra cakāra ha।  
śrīgarbhaḥ sa kathaṃ garbhe striyā bhūcarayā dhṛtaḥ ।। 35.13 ।।  
yena lokān kramairjittvā tribhistrīṃstridaśepsayā।  
sthāpitā jagato mārgāstrivargapravarāstrayaḥ ।। 35.14 ।।  
yo'ntakāle jagatpītvā kṛtvā toyamayaṃ vapuḥ।  
lokamekārṇavaṃ cakre dṛśyādṛśyena vartmanā ।। 35.15 ।।  
yaḥ purāṇe purāṇātmā vārāhaṃ vapurāsthitaḥ।  
dadau jittvā vasumatīṃ surāṇāṃ surasattamaḥ ।। 35.16 ।।  
yena saiṃhaṃ vapuḥ kṛtvā dvidhākṛtvā ca yatpunaḥ।  
pūrvvadaityo mahāvīryyo hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ ।। 35.17 ।।  
yaḥ purā hyanalo bhūtvā aurvvaḥ saṃvarttako vibhuḥ।  
pātālastho'rṇavagataḥ papau toyamayaṃ haviḥ ।। 35.18 ।।  
sahasracaraṇaṃ devaṃ sahasrāṃśuṃ sahasraśaḥ।  
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ yamāhurvai yuge yuge ।। 35.19 ।।  
nābhyāraṇyāḥ samudbhūtaṃ yasya paitāmahaṃ gṛham।  
ekārṇavagate loke tatpaṅkajamapaṅkajam ।। 35.20 ।।  
yena te nihatā daityāḥ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye।  
sarvvadevamayaṃ kṛtvā sarvāyudhadharaṃ vapuḥ ।। 35.21 ।।  
garuḍasthena cotsiktaḥ kālanemirnipātitaḥ।  
uttarāṃśe samudrasya kṣīrodasyāmṛtodadheḥ।  
yaḥ śete śāśvataṃ yogamāsthāya timiraṃ mahat ।। 35.22 ।।  
purāṇī garbhamadhatta divyaṃ tapaḥprakarṣādaditiḥ purā yam।  
śakrañca yo daityagaṇāvaruddhaṃ garbhāvamānena bhṛśaṃ cakāra ।। 35.23 ।।  
yadānilo lokapadāni hṛtvā cakāra daityān salileśayāṃstān ।  
kṛtvādidevastridivasya devāṃścakre sureśaṃ puruhūtameva ।। 35.24 ।।  
gārhapatyena vidhinā anvāhāryyeṇa karmmaṇā।  
agnimāhavanīyañca vediñcaiva kuśasravam ।। 35.25 ।।  
prokṣaṇīyaṃ sruvañcaiva avabhṛthaṃ tathaiva ca।  
atha trīniha yaścakre havyabhāga pradānmakhe ।। 35.26 ।।  
havyādāṃśca surāṃścakre kavyādāṃśca pitṝnapi।  
bhogārthaṃ yajñavidhinā yo yajño yajñakarmmaṇi ।। 35.27 ।।  
yūpān samitsruvaṃ somaṃ pavitraṃ paridhīnapi।  
yajñiyāni ca dravyāṇi yajñīyāṃśca tathānalān ।। 35.28 ।।  
sadasyān yajamānāṃśca aśvamedhān kratūttamān।  
vibabhrāja purā yaśca pārameṣṭyena karmmaṇā ।। 35.29 ।।  
yugānurūpaṃ yaḥ kṛtvā trīlloँkān hi yathākramam।  
kṣaṇā nimeṣāḥ kāṣṭāśca kalāstraikālameva ca ।। 35.30 ।।  
muhūrttāstithayo māsā dinasaṃvatsarāstathā।  
ṛtavaḥ kālayogāśca pramāṇaṃ trividhantathā ।। 35.31 ।।  
āyuḥ kṣetrāṇyupacayaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ rūpasauṣṭhavam।  
medhā vittaṃ ca śauryyañca śāstrasyaiva ca pāraṇam ।। 35.32 ।।  
trayo varṇāstrayo lokāstraividyaṃ pāvakāstrayaḥ।  
traikālyaṃ trīṇi karmmāṇi tisro māyāstrayo guṇāḥ ।। 35.33 ।।  
sṛṣṭā lokāḥ surāścaiva yenātyantena karmmaṇā।  
sarvvabhūtagaṇāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ sarvvabhūtagaṇātmanā ।। 35.34 ।।  
nṛṇāmindriyapūrvveṇa yogena ramate ca yaḥ ।  
gatāgatānāṃ yo netā sarvvatra vividheśvaraḥ ।। 35.35 ।।  
yo gatirdharmayuktānāmagatiḥ pāpakarmmaṇām।  
cāturvarṇyasya prabhavaścāturvarṇyasya rakṣitā ।। 35.36 ।।  
cāturvidyasya yo vettā caturāśramasaṃśrayaḥ।  
digantaraṃ nabho bhūmirāpo vāyurvibhāvasuḥ ।। 35.37 ।।  
candrasūryyadvayaṃ jyotiryugeśaḥ kṣaṇadācaraḥ।  
yaḥ paraḥ śrūyate devo yaḥ paraṃ śrūyate tapaḥ ।। 35.38 ।।  
yaḥ parantapasaḥ prāhuryaḥ paramparamātmavān।  
ādityādistu yo devo yaśca daityāntako vibhuḥ ।। 35.39 ।।  
yugānteṣvantako yaśca yaśca lokāntakāntakaḥ।  
seturyo lokasetūnāṃ medhyo yo medhyakarmmaṇām ।। 35.40 ।।  
vedyo yo vedaviduṣāṃ prabhuryaḥ prabhavātmanām।  
somabhūtastu bhūtānāmagnibhūto'gnivarcasām ।। 35.41 ।।  
manuṣyāṇāṃ manobhūtastapobhūtastapasvinām ।  
vinayo nayatṛptānāṃ tejastejasvināmapi ।। 35.42 ।।  
vigraho vigrahāṇāṃ yo gatirgatimatāmapi।  
ākāśa prabhavo vāyurvāyuprāṇā hutāśanaḥ ।। 35.43 ।।  
divā hutāśanaprāṇāḥ prāṇo'gnermadhusūdanaḥ।  
raso'bhavacchoṇitaṃ vai śoṇitānmāṃsamucyate ।। 35.44 ।।  
māṃsāttu medaso janma medaso'sthi nirūpyate।  
asthnā majjā samabhavanmajjātaḥ śukrasambhavaḥ ।। 35.45 ।।  
śukrādgharbhaḥ samabhavadrasamūlena karmmaṇā।  
tatrāpi prathamañcāpastāḥ saumyarāśirucyate ।। 35.46 ।।  
garbhoṣmasambhavo jñeyo dvitīyo rāśirucyate।  
śukraṃ somātmakaṃ vidyādārttavaṃ pāvakātmakam ।। 35.47 ।।  
bhāvau rasānugāvetau vīryye ca śaśipāvakau।  
kaphavarge'bhavacchukraṃ pittavarge ca śoṇitam ।। 35.48 ।।  
kaphasya hṛdayaṃ sthānaṃ nābhyāṃ pittaṃ pratiṣṭitam।  
dehasya madhye hṛdayaṃ sthānantu manasaḥ smṛtam ।। 35.49 ।।  
nābikoṣṭāntaraṃ yattu tatra devo hutāśanaḥ।  
manaḥ prajāpatirjñeyaṃ kaphaḥ somo vibhāvyate ।। 35.50 ।।  
pittamagniḥ smṛtāvetāvagnisomātmakaṃ jagat।  
evaṃ pravarttito garbho varttate'mbudasannibhaḥ ।। 35.51 ।।  
vāyuḥ praveśanaṃ cakre saṅgataḥ paramātmanā।  
sa pañcadhā śarīrastho vidyate varddhayet punaḥ ।। 35.52 ।।  
prāṇāpānau samānaśca udāno vyāna eva ca।  
prāṇo'sya paramātmānaṃ varddhayan parivarttate ।। 35.53 ।।  
apānaḥ paścimaṃ kāyamudānorddhvaśarīragaḥ।  
vyāno vyānasyate yena samānaḥ sarvvasandhiṣu ।। 35.54 ।।  
bhūtāvāptistatastasya jāyatendriyagocarā।  
pṛthivī vāyurākāśamāpo jyotiśca pañcamam ।। 35.55 ।।  
sarvvendriyā niviṣṭāstaṃ svaṃ svaṃ yogaṃ pracakrire।  
pārthivaṃ dehamāhustaṃ prāṇātmānaṃ ca mārutam ।। 35.56 ।।  
chidrāṇyākāśayonīni jalāsrāvaṃ pravarttate ।  
tejaścakṣuḥṣvitā jyotsnā teṣāṃ yannāmataḥ smṛtam।  
saṅgrāmā viṣayāścaiva yasya vīryyātpravarttitāḥ ।। 35.57 ।।  
ityetān puruṣaḥ sarvvān sṛjaँllokān sanātanaḥ।  
naidhane'smin kathaṃ loke naratvaṃ viṣṇurāgataḥ ।। 35.58 ।।  
eṣa naḥ saṃśayo dhīmanneṣa vai vismayo mahān ।  
kathaṃ gatirgatimatāmāpanno mānuṣīṃ tanum ।। 35.59 ।।  
śrotumicchāmahe viṣṇoḥ karmmāṇi ca yathākramam।  
āścaryyāṇi paraṃ viṣṇurvedadevaiśca kathyate ।। 35.60 ।।  
viṣṇorutpattimāścaryyaṃ kathayasva mahāmate।  
etadāścaryyamākhyānaṃ kathyatāṃ vai sukhāvaham ।। 35.61 ।।  
prakhyātabalavīryyasya prādurbhāvā mahātmanaḥ।  
karmmaṇāścaryyabhūtasya viṣṇoḥ sattvamihocyatām ।। 35.62 ।।  
           ।।sūta uvāca।।  
ahañca kīrttayiṣyāmi prādurbhāvaṃ mahātmanaḥ।  
yathā sa bhagavāñjāto mānuṣeṣu mahātapāḥ ।। 35.63 ।।  
saptasaptatapaḥ proktā bhṛguśāpena mānuṣe।  
jāyate ca yugānteṣu devakāryyarthasiddhaye ।। 35.64 ।।  
tasya divyatanuṃ viṣṇorgadato me nibodhata।  
yugadharmme parāvṛtte kāle ca śithile prabhuḥ ।। 35.65 ।।  
kartuṃ dharmmavyavasthānaṃ jāyate mānuṣeṣviha।  
bhṛgoḥ śāpanimittena devāsurakṛtena ca ।। 35.66 ।।  
            ।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।।  
kathaṃ devāsurakṛte adhyāhāramavāpnuyāt।  
etadveditumicchāmo vṛttaṃ daivāsuraṃ katham ।। 35.67 ।।  
             ।।sūta uvāca।।  
daivāsuraṃ yathāvṛttaṃ bruvatastannibodhata।  
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityastrailokyaṃ prāk praśāsati ।। 35.68 ।।  
balinādhiṣṭitaṃ rāṣṭraṃ punarlokatraye kramāt।  
sakhyamāsītparaṃ teṣāṃ devānāmasuraiḥ saha ।। 35.69 ।।  
yugaṃ vai daśasaṅkīrṇamāsīdavyāhataṃ jagat।  
nideśasthāyinaścaiva tayordevāsurābhavan ।। 35.70 ।।  
balavān vai vivādo'yaṃ saṃpravṛttaḥ sudāruṇaḥ।  
devāsurāṇāṃ ca tadā ghorakṣayakaro mahān ।। 35.71 ।।  
teṣāṃ dāyanimittaṃ vai saṃgrāṇā bahavo'bhavan।  
vārāhe'smin daśa dvau ca ṣaṇḍāmārkottarāḥ smṛtā ।। 35.72 ।।  
nāmatastu samāsena śrṛṇudhvaṃ tān vivakṣataḥ।  
prathamo nārasiṃhastu dvitīyaścāpi vāmanaḥ ।। 35.73 ।।  
tṛtīyaḥ sa tu vārāhaścaturtho'mṛtamandhanaḥ।  
saṃgrāmaḥ pañcamaścaiva sughorastārakāmayaḥ ।। 35.74 ।।  
ṣaṣṭo hyāḍībakasteṣāṃ saptamastraipuraḥ smṛtaḥ।  
andhakāro'ṣṭamasteṣāṃ dhvajaśca navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 35.75 ।।  
vārttaśca daśamo jñeyastato hālā halaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
smṛto dvādaśamasteṣāṃ ghorakolāhalo'paraḥ ।। 35.76 ।।  
hiraṇyakaśipurdaityo narasiṃhena sūditaḥ।  
vāmanena balirvaddhastrailokyākramaṇe kṛte ।। 35.77 ।।  
hiraṇyākṣo hato dvandve prativāde tu daivataiḥ।  
mahābalo mahāsattvaḥ saṃgrāmeṣvaparājitaḥ ।। 35.78 ।।  
daṃṣṭrāyāntu varāheṇa samudrādbhūryadā kṛtā ।  
prāhlādo nirjito yuddhe indreṇāmṛtamanthane ।। 35.79 ।।  
virocanastu prāhlādirnityamindravadhodyataḥ।  
indreṇaiva sa vikramya nihatastārakāmaye ।। 35.80 ।।  
bhavādavadhyatāṃ prāpya viśeṣāstrādibhistu yaḥ।  
sañjabho nihataḥ ṣaṣṭe śakrāviṣṭena viṣṇunā ।। 35.81 ।।  
aśaknuvanto deveṣu puraṃ goptuṃ tridaivatam ।  
nihatā dānavāḥ sarve tripurastryambakeṇa tu ।। 35.82 ।।  
aṣṭame tvasurāścaivaṃ rākṣasāścāndhakārakāḥ।  
jitadevamanuṣyaistu pitṛbhiścaiva saṅgatān ।। 35.83 ।।  
saṃvṛtān dānavāṃścaiva saṅgatān kṛtsnaśaśca tān ।  
tathā viṣṇusahāyena mahendreṇa nibarhitāḥ ।। 35.84 ।।  
hato dhvajo mahendreṇa māyācchannaśca yodhayan।  
dhvaje lakṣyaṃ samāviśya vipravarttirmahābhujaḥ ।। 35.85 ।।  
daityāṃśca dānavāṃścaiva saṃhatān kṛtsnaśaśca tān।  
rajiḥ kolāhale sarvān devaiḥ parivṛto'jayat।  
yajñāmṛtena vijitau ṣaṇḍāmārkau tu daivataiḥ ।। 35.86 ।।  
ete daivāsurā vṛttāḥ saṃgrāmā dvādaśaiva tu।  
devāsurakṣayakarāḥ prajānāmaśivāya ca ।। 35.87 ।।  
hiraṇyakaśipū rājā varṣāṇāmarbudaṃ babhau।  
tathā śatasahasrāṇi hyadikāni dvisaptatiḥ ।  
aśītiṃ ca sahasrāṇi trailokyasyeśvaro'bhavat ।। 35.88 ।।  
paryāye tasya rājā'nu balirvarṣārbudaṃ punaḥ ।  
ṣaṣṭiṃ caiva sahasrāṇi triṃśataṃ niyutāni ca ।। 35.89 ।।  
bale rājyādhikārastu yāvatkālaṃ babhūva ha।  
prahlādena gṛhīto'bhūttāvatkālaṃ tadāsuraiḥ ।। 35.90 ।।  
indrāstrayaste vikhyātā asurāṇāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।  
daityasaṃsthamidaṃ sarvamāsīddaśayugaṃ kila ।। 35.91 ।।  
asapatnaṃ tataḥ sarvaṃ rāṣṭraṃ daśayugaṃ purā।  
trailokyamavyayamidaṃ mahendreṇa tu pālyate ।। 35.92 ।।  
prahlādasya tataścādastrailokyaṃ kālaparyayāt ।  
paryāyeṇa ca saṃprāpte trailokye pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 35.93 ।।  
tato'surān parityajya yajñe devā upāgaman ।  
yajñe devānatha gate kāvyaṃ te hyasurābruvan ।। 35.94 ।।  
kṛtaṃ no miṣatāṃ rāṣṭraṃ tyaktvā yajñaṃ punargatāḥ।  
sthātuṃ na śaknumo hyadya praviśāmo rasātalam ।। 35.95 ।।  
evamukto'bravīdetān viṣaṇṇaḥ sāntvayan girā।  
mābhaiṣṭa dhārayiṣyāmi tejasā svena cāsurāḥ ।। 35.96 ।।  
vṛṣṭiroṣadhayaścaiva rasā vasu ca yadvayam।  
kṛtsnā mayi ca tiṣṭhanti pādasteṣāṃ sureṣu vai।  
yuṣmadarthaṃ pradāsyāmi tatsarvaṃ dhāryate mayā ।। 35.97 ।।  
tato devāsurān dṛṣṭvā dhṛtān kāvyena dhīmatā।  
amantrayaṃstadā te vai saṃvignā vijigīṣayā ।। 35.98 ।।  
eṣa kāvya idaṃ sarvaṃ vyāvarttayati no balāt ।  
sādhu gacchāmahe tūrṇaṃ kṣīṇānnāpyāyayasva tān ।  
prasahya hatvā śiṣṭān vai pātālaṃ prāpayāmahe ।। 35.99 ।।  
tato devāḥ susaṃrabdhā dānavānabhisṛtya vai।  
jadhnustai rvadhyamānāste kāvyamevābhidudruvuḥ ।। 35.100 ।।  
tataḥ kāvyastu tāndṛṣṭvā tūrṇaṃ devairabhidrutān।  
samare'ktrakṣatārttāṃstān devebhyastān diteḥ sutān ।। 35.101 ।।  
kāvyo dṛṣṭvā sthitān devān tatra devo'bhyacintayat।  
tānuvāca tato dhyātvā pūrvavṛttamanusmaran ।। 35.102 ।।  
trailokyaṃ vijitaṃ sarvaṃ vāmanena tribhiḥ kramaiḥ ।  
balirbaddho hato jambho nihataśca virocanaḥ ।। 35.103 ।।  
mahārheṣu dvādaśasu saṃgrāmeṣu surairhatāḥ।  
taistairupāyairbhūyiṣṭā nihatā ye pradhānataḥ ।। 35.104 ।।  
kiñcicchiṣṭāstu vai yūyaṃ yuddheṣvantyeṣu vai svayam।  
nītiṃ vo hi vidhāsyāmi kālaḥ kaścitpratīkṣyatām ।। 35.105 ।।  
yāsyāmyahaṃ mahādevaṃ mantrārthe vijayāya vaḥ।  
agnimāpyāyayeddhotā mantraireva bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 35.106 ।।  
tato yāsyāmyahaṃ devaṃ mantrārthe nīlalohitam।  
yuṣmānanugrahīṣyāmi punaḥ paścādihāgataḥ ।। 35.107 ।।  
yūyaṃ tapaścaradhvaṃ vai saṃvṛtā valkalairvane।  
na vai devā vadhiṣyanti yāvadāgamanaṃ mama ।। 35.108 ।।  
apratīpāṃstato mantrān devāt prāpya maheśvarāt।  
yotsyāmahe punardevāṃstataḥ prāpsyatha vai jayam ।। 35.109 ।।  
tataste kṛtasaṃvādā devānūcustato'surāḥ।  
nyastavādā vayaṃ sarve lokān yūyaṃ kramantu vai ।। 35.110 ।।  
vayaṃ tapaścariṣyāmaḥ saṃvṛtā valkalairvane।  
prahlādasya vacaḥ śrutvā satyavyāharaṇaṃ tu tat ।। 35.111 ।।  
tato devā nivṛttā vai vijvarā muditāśca ha।  
nyastaśastreṣu daityeṣu svān vai jagmuryathāgatān ।। 35.112 ।।  
tatastānabravītkāvyaḥ kañcitkālamupāsyatām।  
nirutsukaistapoyuktaiḥ kālaṃ kāryārthasādhakaiḥ।  
piturmamāśramasthā vai sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।। 35.113 ।।  
sa sandiśyāsurān kāvyo mahādevaṃ prapadya ca।  
praṇamyenasuvācātha jagatprabhavamīśvaram ।। 35.114 ।।  
mantrānicchāmyahaṃ deva me nasanti bṛhaspatau।  
parābhavāya devānāmasureṣvabhayāvahān ।। 35.115 ।।  
evamukto'bravīddevo mantrānicchasi vai dvija।  
vrataṃ cara mayo ddiṣṭaṃ brahmacārī samāhitaḥ ।। 35.116 ।।  
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai kuṇḍadhūmamavākśirāḥ।  
yadyupāsyasi bhadrante matto mantramavāpsyasi ।। 35.117 ।।  
tathokto deva devena sa śukrastu mahātapāḥ।  
pādau saṃspṛśya devasya bāḍhamityabhyabhāṣata ।। 35.118 ।।  
vrataṃ carāmyahaṃ śeṣaṃ yathoddiṣṭo'smi vai prabho।  
tato niyukto devena kuṇḍadhāro'sya dhūmakṛt ।। 35.119 ।।  
asurāṇāṃ hitārthāya tasmiñchukre gate tadā।  
mantrārthaṃ tatra vasati brahmacarye maheśvaraḥ ।। 35.120 ।।  
tadbuddhvā nātipūrvantu rājyaṃ nyastaṃ tadāsuraiḥ।  
tasmiñchidre tadāmarṣā devāstān samabhidravan।  
niśitāttāyudhāḥ sarve bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ ।। 35.121 ।।  
dṛṣṭvāsuragaṇā devān pragṛhītāyudhān punaḥ।  
utpetuḥ sahasā sarve santrastāste tato'bhavan ।। 35.122 ।।  
nyastaśastre jaye datte ācāryavratamāsthite।  
santyajya. samayaṃ devāste sapatnajighāṃsavaḥ ।। 35.123 ।।
