anācāryāstu bhadraṃ vo viśvastāstapasi sthitāḥ।  
cīravalkājinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ ।। 35.124 ।।  
raṇe vijetuṃ devān vai naśakṣyāmaḥ kathañcana।  
aśuddhena prapadyāmaḥ śaraṇaṃ kāvyamātaram ।। 35.125 ।।  
jñāpayāmastatamidaṃ yāvadāgamanaṃ guroḥ।  
vinivṛtte tataḥ kāvye yotsyāmo yudhi tān surān ।। 35.126 ।।  
evamuktvā surān yogyaṃ śaraṇaṃ kāvyamātaram।  
prāpadyanta tato bhītāstadā caiva tadā'bhayam ।। 35.127 ।।  
dattanteṣāntu bhītānāṃ daityā nāmabhayārthinām।  
na bhetavyaṃ na bhetavya bhayantyajata dānavāḥ ।। 35.128 ।।  
matsannidhau vartatāṃ vo na bhīrbhavitumarhati।  
bhayāccāpyabhipannāṃstān dṛṣṭvā devāsurāṃstadā ।। 35.129 ।।  
abhijagmuḥ prasahyaitānavicārya balābalam।  
tāṃstrastān vadhyamānāṃśca devairdṛṣṭvāsurāṃstadā ।। 35.130 ।।  
devī kruddhābravīdenānanindratvaṃ karomyaham।  
saṃstabhya śīghraṃ saṃrambhādindraṃ sā'bhyacarattataḥ ।। 35.131 ।।  
tataḥ saṃstambhitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śakraṃdevāstu yūpavat।  
vyadravanta tato bhītā dṛṣṭvā śakraṃ vaśīkṛtam ।। 35.132 ।।  
gateṣu surasaṅgheṣu viṣṇurindramabhāṣata।  
māṃtvaṃ praviśa bhadrante neṣyāmi tvāṃ sureśvara ।। 35.133 ।।  
evamuktastato viṣṇuṃ praviveśa purandaraḥ।  
viṣṇunā rakṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā devī kruddhā vaco'vadat ।। 35.134 ।।  
eṣā tvāṃ viṣṇunā sārddhaṃ dahāmi maghavāniva।  
miṣatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ dṛśyatāṃ me tapobalam ।। 35.135 ।।  
tayābhibhūtau tau devāvindraviṣṇū jajalpatuḥ।  
kathaṃ mucyeva sahitau viṣṇurindramabhāṣata ।। 35.136 ।।  
indro'bravījjahi hyenāṃ yāvannau na dahedvibho।  
viśeṣeṇābhibhūto'hamatastvañca hi mā ciram ।। 35.137 ।।  
tataḥ samīkṣya tāṃ viṣṇuḥ strīvadhaṃ karttumāsthitaḥ।  
abhidhyāya tataścakramāpannaḥ satvaraṃ prabhuḥ ।। 35.138 ।।  
tasyāḥ satvaramāṇāyāḥ śīghrakārī surārihā।  
striyā viṣṇustato devyā krūraṃ buddhvā cikīrṣitam।  
kruddhastadastramāviddhya śiraściccheda mādhavaḥ ।। 35.139 ।।  
taṃ dṛṣṭvā strīvadhaṃ ghoraṃ cukopa bhṛgurīśvaraḥ।  
tato'bhiśasto bhṛguṇā viṣṇurbhāryāvadhe tadā ।। 35.140 ।।  
yasmātte jānatā dharmānavadhyā strī niṣūditā।  
tasmāttvaṃ saptakṛtvo vai mānuṣeṣu prapatsyasi ।। 35.141 ।।  
tatastenābhiśāpena naṣṭe dharme punaḥ punaḥ।  
loke sarvahitārthāya jāyate mānuṣeṣviha ।। 35.142 ।।  
anuvyāhṛtya viṣṇuṃ sa tadādāya śiraḥ svayam।  
samānīya tataḥ kāye apo gṛhyedamabravīt ।। 35.143 ।।  
eṣa tvāṃ viṣṇunā satye hatāṃ saṃjīvayāmyaham ।  
yadi kṛtsno mayā dharmaścarito jñāyate'pi vā।  
tena satyena jīvasva yadi satyaṃ bravīmyaham ।। 35.144 ।।  
satyābhivyāhṛtā tasyā devī saṃjīvitā tadā।  
tadā tāṃ prokṣya śītābhiradbhirjīveti so'bravīt ।। 35.145 ।।  
tatastāṃ sarvabhūtāni dṛṣṭvā suptotthitāmiva।  
sādhu sādhvityadṛśyānāṃ vācastāḥ sasvarurdiśaḥ ।। 35.146 ।।  
dṛṣṭvā sañjīvitāmevaṃ devīṃ tāṃ bhṛguṇā tadā।  
miṣatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tadadbhutamivābhavat ।। 35.147 ।।  
asaṃbhrāntena bhṛguṇā patnīṃ sañjīvitāṃ tataḥ।  
dṛṣṭvā śakro na lebhe'tha śarma kāvyabhayāttataḥ ।। 35.148 ।।  
prajāgare tataścendro jayantīmātmanaḥ sutām।  
provāca matimān vākyaṃ svāṃ kanyāṃ pākaśāsanaḥ ।। 35.149 ।।  
eṣa kāvyo hyanindrāya carate dāruṇaṃ tapaḥ।  
tenāhaṃ vyākulaḥ putri kṛto dhṛtimatā dṛḍham ।। 35.150 ।।  
gaccha sambhāvayasvainaṃ śramāpanayanaiḥ śubhaiḥ।  
taistairmanonukūlaiśca hyupacārairatandritā ।। 35.151 ।।  
devī sā hīndratuhitā jayantī śubhacāriṇī।  
yuktadhyānañca śāmyaṃ taṃ durbalaṃ dhṛtimāsthitam ।। 35.152 ।।  
pitrā yathoktaṃ kāvyaṃ sā kāvye kṛtavatī tadā।  
gīrbhiścaivānukūlābhiḥ stuvatī valgubhāṣiṇī ।। 35.153 ।।  
gātrasaṃvāhanaiḥ kāle sevamānā sukhāvahaiḥ ।  
śuśrūṣantyanukūlā ca uvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ ।। 35.154 ।।  
pūrṇe dhūmavrate cāpi ghore varṣasahasrike ।  
vareṇa cchandayāmāsa kāvyaṃ prīto'bhavattadā ।। 35.155 ।।  
evaṃ bruvaṃstvayaikena cīrṇaṃ nānyena kenacit।  
tasmāttvaṃ tapasā buddhyā śrutena ca balena ca ।। 35.156 ।।  
tejasā cāpi vibudhān sarvānabhibhaviṣyasi।  
yacca kiñcinmama brahman vidyate bhṛgunandana ।। 35.157 ।।  
sāṅgañca sarahasyañca yajñopaniṣadāntathā।  
pratibhāsyati te sarvaṃ taccādyantaṃ na kasyacit ।। 35.158 ।।  
sarvābhibhāvī tena tvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭo bhaviṣyasi।  
evaṃ dattvā varāṃstasmai bhārgavāya punaḥ punaḥ ।। 35.159 ।।  
ajeyatvaṃ dhaneśatvamavadhyatvaṃ ca vai dadau।  
etān labdhvā varān kāvyaḥ samprahṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ ।। 35.160 ।।  
harṣāt prādurbabhau tasya devastotraṃ maheśvaram।  
tadā tiryaksthitastvevaṃ tuṣṭuve nīlalohitam ।। 35.161 ।।  
namo'stu śitikaṇṭāya surāpāya suvarcase।  
ririhāṇāya lopāya vatsarāya jagatpate ।। 35.162 ।।  
kapardine hyūrddhvaromṇe hayāya karaṇāya ca।  
saṃskṛtāya sutīrthāya devadevāya raṃhase ।। 35.163 ।।  
uṣṇīṣiṇe suvakrāya sahasrākṣāya mīḍhuṣe।  
vasuretāya rudrāya tapase cīravāsase ।। 35.164 ।।  
hrasvāya muktakeśāya senānye rohitāya ca ।। 35.165 ।।  
kavaye rājavṛddhāya takṣakakrīḍanāya ca।  
giriśāyārkanetrāya yatine jāmbavāya ca।  
suvṛttāya suhastāya dhanvine bhārgavāya ca ।। 35.166 ।।  
sahasrabāhave caiva sahasrāmalacakṣuṣe।  
sahasrakukṣaye caiva sahasracaraṇāya ca ।। 35.167 ।।  
sahasraśirase caiva bahurūpāya vedhase।  
bhavāya viśvarūpāya śvetāya puruṣāya ca ।। 35.168 ।।  
niṣaṅgiṇe kavacine sūkṣmāya kṣapaṇāya ca।  
tāmrāya caiva bhīmāya ugrāya ca śivāya ca ।। 35.169 ।।  
babhrave ca piśaṅgāya piṅgalāyāruṇāya ca।  
mahādevāya śarvvāya viśvarūpaśivāya ca ।। 35.170 ।।  
hiraṇyāya ca śiṣṭāya śreṣṭāya madhyamāya ca ।  
pinākine ceṣumate citrāya rohitāya ca ।। 35.171 ।।  
dundubhyāyaikapādāya arhāya buddhaye tathā।  
mṛgavyādhāya sarpāya sthāṇave bhīṣaṇāya ca ।। 35.172 ।।  
bahurūpāya cogrāya trinetrāyeśvarāya ca।  
kapilāyaikavīrāya mṛtyave tryambakāya ca ।। 35.173 ।।  
vāstoṣpate vinākāya śaṅkarāya śivāya ca।  
āraṇyāya guhasthāya yatine brahmacāriṇe ।। 35.174 ।।  
sāṅkhyāya caiva yogāya dhyānine dīkṣitāya ca।  
antarhitāya śarvvāya mānyāya māline tathā ।। 35.175 ।।  
buddhāya caiva puṇyāya dhārmikāya śubhāya ca।  
rodhase cekitānāya brahmiṣṭāya maharṣaye ।। 35.176 ।।  
catuṣpādāya medhyāya dharmiṇe śīghragāya ca।  
śikhaṇḍine kapālāya daṃṣṭriṇe viśvamedhase ।। 35.177 ।।  
apratīghātāya dīptāya bhāskarāya sumedhase।  
krūrāya vikṛtāyaiva bībhatsāya śivāya ca ।। 35.178 ।।  
saumyāya caiva puṇyāya dhārmikāya śubhāya ca।  
avadhyāya mṛtāṅgāya nityāya śāśvatāya ca ।। 35.179 ।।  
sādyāya śarabhāyaiva śūline ca tricakṣuṣe।  
somapāyājyapāyaiva dhūmapāyoṣmapāya ca ।। 35.180 ।।  
śucaye rerihāṇāya sadyojātāya mṛtyave।  
piśitāśāya kharvāya medhāya vaidyutāya ca ।। 35.181 ।।  
vyāśritāya śraviṣṭāya bhāratāyāntarikṣaye।  
kṣamāya saha mānāya satyāya tapanāya ca ।। 35.182 ।।  
tripuraghnāya dīptāya cakrāya romaśāya ca।  
tigmāyudhāya medhyāya siddhāya ca pulastaye ।। 35.183 ।।  
rocamānāya khaṇḍāya sphītāya ṛṣabhāya ca।  
bhogine puñjamānāya śāntāyaivorddhvaretase ।। 35.184 ।।  
aghaghnāya makhghnāya mṛtyave yajñiyāya ca।  
kṛśānave pracetāya vahnaye kiśalāya ca ।। 35.185 ।।  
sikatyāya prasannāya vareṇyāyaiva cakṣuṣe।  
kṣipregave sudhanvāya pramedhyāya priyāya ca ।। 35.186 ।।  
rakṣoghnāya paśughnāya vighnāya śayanāya ca।  
vibhrāntāya mahantāya antaye durgamāya ca ।। 35.187 ।।  
dakṣāya ca jaghanyāya lokānāmīśvarāya ca।  
anāmayāya corddhvāya saṃhatyādhiṣṭitāya ca ।। 35.188 ।।  
hiraṇyabāhave caiva satyāya śamanāya ca।  
asikalyāya māghāya rīriṇyāyaikacakṣuṣe ।। 35.189 ।।  
śreṣṭāya vāmadevāya īśānāya ca dhīmate।  
mahākalpāya dīptāya rādenāya hasāya ca ।। 35.190 ।।  
vṛtadhanvane kavicine rathine ca varūthine।  
bhṛgunāthāya śukrāya vahniriṣṭāya dhīmate ।। 35.191 ।।  
aghāya aghaśaṃsāya vipriyāya priyāya ca ।  
digvāsaḥkṛttivāsāya bhagaghnāya namo'stu te ।। 35.192 ।।  
paśūnāṃ pataye caiva bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ।  
praṇane ṛgyajuḥsāmne svadhāyai ca sudhāya ca ।। 35.193 ।।  
vaṣaṭkāratamāyaiva tubhyamantātmane namaḥ ।  
sraṣṭre dhātre tathā hotre hartre ca kṣapaṇāya ca ।। 35.194 ।।  
bhūtabhavyabhavāyaiva tubhyaṃ kālātmane namaḥ।  
vasave caiva sādhyāya rudrādityāśvināya ca ।। 35.195 ।।  
viśvāya marute caiva tubhyandevātmane namaḥ।  
agnisomartvigijyāya paśumantrauṣadhāya ca ।। 35.196 ।।  
dakṣiṇāvabhṛthāyaiva tubhyaṃ yajñātmane namaḥ ।  
tapase caiva satyāya tyāgāya ca śamāya ca ।। 35.197 ।।  
ahiṃsāyāpyalobhāya suveśāyātiśāya ca।  
sarvabhūtātmabhūtāya tubhyaṃ yogātmane namaḥ ।। 35.198 ।।  
pṛthivyai cāntarikṣāya divāya ca mahāya ca।  
janastapāya satyāya tubhyaṃ lokātmane namaḥ ।। 35.199 ।।  
avyaktāyātha mahate bhūtāyaivondriyāya ca ।  
tanmātrāya mahāntāya tubhyaṃ tattvātmane namaḥ ।। 35.200 ।।  
nityāya cārthaliṅgāya sūkṣmāya cetanāya ca।  
śuddhāya vibhave caiva tubhyaṃ nityātmane namaḥ ।। 35.201 ।।  
namaste triṣu lokeṣu svarānteṣu bhavādiṣu।  
satyānteṣu mahānteṣu caturṣu ca namo'stu te ।। 35.202 ।।  
namaḥstotre mayā hyasmin sadasadvyāhṛtaṃ vibho।  
madbhakta iti brahmaṇya sarvantat kṣantumarhasi ।। 35.203 ।।  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte viṣṇumāhātmye śambhustavakīrttanaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 35 ।। 


---
title: 036

---
         sūta uvāca।।  
evamārādhya deveśamīśānaṃ nīlalohitam।  
brahmeti praṇatastasmai prāñjalirvākyamabravīt ।। 36.1 ।।  
  
kāvyasya gātraṃ saṃspṛśya hastena prītimān bhavaḥ।  
nikāmaṃ darśanaṃ dattvā tatraivāntaradhīyata ।। 36.2 ।।  
  
tataḥ so'ntarhite tasmin deveśānucare tadā।  
tiṣṭhantīṃ prāñjalirbhūtvā jayantīmidamabravīt ।। 36.3 ।।  
  
kasya tvaṃ subhage kā vā duḥkhite mayi duḥkhitā।  
mahatā tapasā yuktaṃ kimarthaṃ māñjugopasi ।। 36.4 ।।  
  
anayā satataṃ bhaktyā praśrayeṇa damena ca।  
snehena caiva suśroṇi prīto'smi varavarṇini ।। 36.5 ।।  
  
kimicchasi varārehe kaste kāmaḥ samṛdhyatām।  
taṃ te saṃpūrayāmyadya yadyapi syāt sudurlabham ।। 36.6 ।।  
  
evamuktā''bravīdanaṃ tapasā jñātumarhasi।  
cikīrṣitaṃ me brahniṣṭhatvaṃ hi vettha yathātatham ।। 36.7 ।।  
  
evamukte'bravīdenāṃ dṛṣṭvā divyena cakṣuṣā।  
māhendrī tvaṃ varārohe maddhitārthamihāgatā ।। 36.8 ।।  
  
mayā saha tvaṃ suśroṇi daśa varṣāṇi bhāmini।  
adṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtaistu saṃprayogamihecchasi ।। 36.9 ।।  
  
devendrānalavarṇābhe varārohe sulocane।  
imaṃ vṛṇīṣva kāmaṃ te matto vai valgubhāṣiṇi ।। 36.10 ।।  
  
evaṃ bhavatu gacchāmo gṛhān vai mattakāśini ।  
tataḥ svagṛhamāgamya jayantyā sahitaḥ prabhuḥ ।। 36.11 ।।  
  
sa tayā saṃ va saddevyā daśa varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ।  
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ māyayā saṃvṛtastadā ।। 36.12 ।।  
  
kṛtārthamāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā kāvyaṃ sarve diteḥ sutāḥ ।  
abhijagmurgṛhaṃ tasya muditāste didṛkṣavaḥ ।। 36.13 ।।  
  
gatā yadā na paśyanto jayantyā saṃvṛtaṃ gurum।  
dākṣiṇyaṃ tasya tadbudhvā pratijagmuryathāgatam ।। 36.14 ।।  
  
bṛhaspatistu saṃruddhaṃ jñātvā kāvyaṃ cakāra ha।  
pitrarthe daśa varṣāṇi jayantyā hitakāmyayā ।। 36.15 ।।  
  
buddhvā tadantaraṃ so'tha daityānāmiva coditaḥ।  
kāvyasya rūpamāsthāya so'surānsamabhāṣata ।। 36.16 ।।  
  
tataḥ samāgatān dṛṣṭvā bṛhaspatiruvāca tān।  
svāgataṃ mama yājyānāṃ saṃprāpto'smi hitāya ca ।। 36.17 ।।  
  
ahaṃ vo'dhyāpayiṣyāmi prāptā vidyā mayā hi sā।  
tataste hṛṣṭamanaso vidyārthamupapedire ।। 36.18 ।।  
  
pūrṇakāmastadā tasmin samaye daśavārṣike।  
yayau ca samakālaṃ sa sadyotpannamatistadā ।। 36.19 ।।  
  
samayānte devayānī sadyo jātā sutā tadā।  
buddhiṃ cakre tataścāpi yājyānāṃ pratyavekṣaṇe ।। 36.20 ।।  
  
           ।।śukra uvāca।।  
devi gacchāmahe draṣṭuṃ tava yājyān śucismite।  
vibhrāntaprekṣite sādhvi trivarṇāyatalocane ।। 36.21 ।।  
  
evamuktā'bravīddevī bhaja bhaktān mahāvrata।  
eṣa brahman satāṃ dharmo na dharmaṃ lopayāmi te ।। 36.22 ।।  
  
           ।।sūta uvāca।।  
tato gatvāsurān dṛṣṭvā devācāryeṇa dhīmatā।  
vāñcitān kāvyarūpeṇa vedhasā'suramabravīt ।। 36.23 ।।  
  
kāvyaṃ māṃ tāta jānīdhvaṃ eṣa hyāṅgiraso bhuvi।  
vañcitā bata yūyaṃ vai mayi śakte tu dānavāḥ ।। 36.24 ।।  
  
śrutvā tathā bruvāṇantaṃ sambhrāntā ditijāstataḥ।  
prekṣante sma hyubhau tatra sitāsitaśucismitau ।। 36.25 ।।  
  
sampramūḍhāḥ sthitāḥ sarve prāpadyanta na kiñcana।  
tatasteṣu pramūḍheṣu kāvyastān punarabravīt ।। 36.26 ।।  
  
ācāryyo vo hyahaṃ kāvyo devācāryo'yamaṅgirāḥ।  
anugacchata māṃ sarve tyajatainaṃ bṛhaspatim ।। 36.27 ।।  
  
evamuktāsurāḥ sarve tāvṛbhau samavaikṣata।  
tadā'surā viśeṣantu na vyajānaṃstayordvayoḥ ।। 36.28 ।।  
  
bṛhaspatiruvācaitānasambhrānto'yamaṅgirāḥ।  
kāvyo'haṃ yo gururdaityā madrūpo'yaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 36.29 ।।  
  
sa mohayati rūpeṇa māmakenaiṣa vo'surāḥ।  
śrutvā tasya tataste vai saṃmantryārthavaco'bruvan ।। 36.30 ।।  
  
ayanno daśa varṣāṇi satataṃ śāsti vai prabhuḥ।  
eṣa vai gururasmākamantarepsurayaṃ dvijaḥ ।। 36.31 ।।  
  
tataste dānavāḥ sarve praṇipatyābhivādya ca।  
vacanaṃ jagṛhustasya cirābhyāsena mohitāḥ ।। 36.32 ।।  
  
ūcustamasurāḥ sarve kruddhāḥ saṃraktalocanāḥ.  
ayaṅgururhite'smākaṃ gaccha tvaṃ nāsi no guruḥ ।। 36.33 ।।  
  
bhārgavo'ṅgiraso vāyaṃ bhavatvevaiṣa noguruḥ।  
sthitā vayaṃ nideśe'sya gacchatvaṃ sādhu mā ciram ।। 36.34 ।।  
  
evamuktvāsurāḥ sarve prāpadyanta bṛhaspatim।  
yadā na pratipadyante tenoktaṃ tanmahaddhitam ।। 36.35 ।।  
  
cukopa bhārgavasteṣāmavalepena vai tadā।  
bodhitā hi mayā yasmānna māṃ bhajata dānavāḥ ।। 36.36 ।।  
  
tasmāt pranaṣṭa saṃjñāṃ vai parābhavaṅgamiṣyatha।  
idi vyāhṛtya tān kāvyo jagāmātha yathāgatam ।। 36.37 ।।  
  
jñātvā'bhiśastānasurān kāvyena tu bṛhaspatiḥ।  
kṛtārthaḥ sa tadā hṛṣṭaḥ svaṃ rūpaṃ pratyapadyata।  
buddhvā'surāṃstadā bhraṣṭān kṛtārtho'ntaradhīyata ।। 36.38 ।।  
  
tataḥ pranaṣṭe tasmiṃste vibhrāntā dānavāstadā।  
aho dhig vañcitāḥ smeha parasparamathābruvan ।। 36.39 ।।  
  
pṛṣṭhato vimukhāścaiva tāḍitā vedhasā vayam।  
dagdhāścaivopayogācca svesve cārtheṣu māyayā ।। 36.40 ।।  
  
tato'surāḥ paritrastā devebhyastvaritā yayuḥ।  
prahlādamagrataḥ kṛtvā kāvyasyānugamaṃ punaḥ ।। 36.41 ।।  
  
tataḥ kāvyaṃ samāsādya abhitasthu ravāṅmukhāḥ।  
tānāgatān punardṛṣṭvā kāvyo yājyānuvāca ha ।। 36.42 ।।  
  
mayāpi bodhitāḥ kāle yato māṃ nābhinandatha।  
tatastenāvalepena gatā yūthaṃ parābhavam ।। 36.43 ।।  
  
prahlādastamathovāca mānaṃ tvaṃ tyaja bhārgava।  
svān yājyān bhajamānāṃśca bhaktāṃścaiva viśeṣataḥ ।। 36.44 ।।  
  
tvayā pṛṣṭā vayaṃ tena devācāryeṇa mohitāḥ।  
bhaktānarhasi nastrātuṃ jñātvā dīrgheṇa cakṣuṣā ।। 36.45 ।।  
  
yadi nastvaṃ na kuruṣe prasādaṃ bhṛgunandana।  
apadhyātā stvayā hyadya pravekṣyāmo rasātalam ।। 36.46 ।।  
  
           sūta uvāca।।  
jñātvā kāvyo yathātattvaṃ kāruṇyenānukampayā ।  
evamukto'nunītaḥ sa stutaḥ kopaṃ nyayacchata ।। 36.47 ।।  
  
uvācedanna bhetavyaṃ na gantanyaṃ rasātalam।  
avaśyambhāvī hyartho'yaṃ prāpto vo mayi jāgrati ।। 36.48 ।।  
  
na śakyamanyathā kartuṃ dṛṣṭaṃ hi balavattaram ।  
saṃjñā pranaṣṭā yā vo'dya kāmaṃ tāṃ pratilapsyatha ।। 36.49 ।।  
  
prāptaḥ paryyāyakālo va iti brahmā'bhyabhāṣata।  
matprasādācca yuṣmābhirbhuktaṃ trailokyamūrjjitam ।। 36.50 ।।  
  
yugākhyo daśa saṃpūrṇo devānākramya mūrddhani।  
tāvantameva kālaṃ vai brahmā rājyamabhāṣata ।। 36.51 ।।  
  
sāvarṇike punastubhyaṃ rājyaṃ kila bhaviṣyati।  
lokānāmīśvaro bhāvī pautrastava punarbaliḥ ।। 36.52 ।।  
  
evaṃ kilamahaṃ proktaḥ pautraste brahmaṇā svayam।  
tathāhṛteṣu lokeṣu tapo'sya na kilābhavat ।। 36.53 ।।  
  
yasmāt pravṛttayaścāsya na kāmānabhisandhitāḥ।  
tasmādajena prītena dattaṃ sāvarṇike'ntare ।। 36.54 ।।  
  
devarājyaṃ balerbhāvyamiti māmīśvaro'bravīt।  
tasmādadṛśyo bhūtānāṃ kālākāṅkṣī sa tiṣṭhati ।। 36.55 ।।  
  
prītena cāmaratvaṃ vai dattaṃ tubyaṃ svayambhuvā।  
tasmānnirutsu kastvaṃ vai paryyāyaṃ saha mākulaḥ ।। 36.56 ।।  
  
na ca śakyaṃ mayā tubhyaṃ purastādvai visarpitum ।  
brahmaṇā pratiṣiddho'smi bhaviṣyaṃ jānatā prabho ।। 36.57 ।।  
  
imau ca śiṣyau dvau mahyaṃ tulyāvetau bṛhaspateḥ ।  
daivataiḥ saha saṃrabdhān sarvvān vo dhārayiṣyataḥ ।। 36.58 ।।  
  
evamuktastu daiteyāḥ kāvyenākliṣṭakarmmaṇā।  
tatastābhyāṃ yayuḥ sārddhaṃ prahlādapramukhāstadā ।। 36.59 ।।  
  
avaśyambhāvamarthatvaṃ śrutvā śukrācca dānavāḥ।  
sakṛdāśaṃsamānāste jayaṃ kāvyena bhāṣitam ।। 36.60 ।।  
  
daṃśitāḥ sāyudhāḥ sarve tato devān samāhvayan।  
atha devāsurān dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme samupasthitān ।। 36.61 ।।  
  
tataḥ saṃvṛttasannāhā devāstān samayodhayan।  
daivāsure tatastasmin varttamāne śataṃ samāḥ।  
ajayannasurā devān bhagnā devā amantrayan ।। 36.62 ।।  
  
             ।।devā ūcuḥ ।।  
  
ṣaṇḍāmārkaprabhāvaṃ na jānīmastva surairvayam।  
tasmādyajñaṃ samuddiśya kāryyaṃ cātmahitañca yat ।। 36.63 ।।  
  
tajjñānāpahṛtāvetau kṛtvā jeṣyāmahe'surān ।  
athopāmantrayan devāḥ ṣaṇḍāmārkau tu tāvubhau ।। 36.64 ।।  
  
yajñe samāhvayiṣyāmastyajatamasurān dvijau ।  
grahaṃ taṃ vā grahīṣyāmo hyanujitya tu dānavān ।। 36.65 ।।  
  
evaṃ tatyajatustau tu ṣaṇḍāmārkau tadāsurān ।  
tato devā jayaṃ prāptā dānavāśca parābhavam ।। 36.66 ।।  
  
devāsurān parābhāvya ṣaṇḍāmārkāvupāgaman।  
kāvyaśāpābhibhūtāśca hyanādhārāśca te punaḥ ।। 36.67 ।।  
  
vadhyamānāstadā devairviviśuste rasātalam।  
evaṃ nirudyamāste vai kṛtāḥ śakreṇa dānavāḥ।  
tataḥ prabhṛti śāpena bhṛgunaimittikena ca ।। 36.68 ।।  
  
jajñe punaḥ punarviṣṇuryajñe ca śithile prabhuḥ।  
karttuṃ dharmmavyavasthānamadharmmasya ca nāśanam ।। 36.69 ।।  
  
prahlādasya nideśe tu ye'surā na vyavasthitāḥ।  
manuṣyavadhyāṃstān sarvvān brahmā vyāhārayat prabhuḥ ।। 36.70 ।।  
  
dharmmānnārāyaṇastasmān sambhūtaścākṣuṣe'ntare।  
yajñaṃ pravartayāmāsa caitye vaivasvate'ntare ।। 36.71 ।।  
  
prādurbhāve tadānyasya brahmaivāsīt purohitaḥ।  
caturthyāntu yugākhyāyāmāpanneṣvasureṣvatha ।। 36.72 ।।  
  
sambhūtaḥ sa samudrāntarhiraṇyakaśiporvadhe।  
dvitīyo narasiṃṅo'bhūdrudraḥ surapurassaraḥ ।। 36.73 ।।  
  
balisaṃstheṣu lokeṣu tretāyāṃ saptame yuge।  
daityaistrailokya ākrānte tṛtīyo vāmano'bhavat ।। 36.74 ।।  
  
saṃkṣipyātmānamaṅgeṣu bṛhaspatipurassaram।  
yajamānantu daityendramadityāḥ kulanandanaḥ।  
dvijo bhūtvā śubhe kāle baliṃ vairocanampurā ।। 36.75 ।।  
  
trailokyasya bhavān rājā tvayi sarvvaṃ pratiṣṭitam।  
dātumarhasi me rājan vikramāṃstrīniti prabhuḥ ।। 36.76 ।।  
  
dadāmītyeva taṃ rājā balirvairocano'bravīt।  
vāmanantaṃ ca vijñāya tato'numuditaḥ svayam ।। 36.77 ।।  
  
sa vāmano divaṃ khaṃ ca pṛthivīṃ ca dvijottamāḥ।  
tribhiḥ kramairviśvamidaṃ jagadākrāmata prabhuḥ ।। 36.78 ।।  
  
atyaricyata bhūtātmā bhāskaraṃ svena tejasā।  
prakāśayan diśaḥ sarvvāḥ pradiśaśca mahāyaśāḥ ।। 36.79 ।।  
  
śuśubhe sa mahābāhuḥ sarvvalokān prakāśayan।  
āsurīṃ śriyamāhṛtya trīṃllokāṃśca janārdanaḥ।  
saputrapautrānasurān pātālatalamānayat ।। 36.80 ।।  
  
namuciḥ śambaraścaiva prahlādaścaiva viṣṇunā।  
krūrā hatā vinirddhūtā diśaḥ saṃpratipedire ।। 36.81 ।।  
  
mahābhūtāni bhūtātmā saviśeṣāṇi mādhavaḥ।  
kālañca sakalaṃ viprāṃstatrādbhutamadarśayat ।। 36.82 ।।  
  
tasya gātre jagatsarvamātmānamanupaśyati ।  
na kiñcidasti lokeṣu yadavyāptaṃ mahātmanā ।। 36.83 ।।  
  
tadvai rūpamupendrasya devadānavamānavāḥ।  
dṛṣṭvā sammumuhuḥ sarve viṣṇutejovimohitāḥ ।। 36.84 ।।  
  
baliḥ silo mahāpāśaiḥ sabandhuḥ sasuhṛdgaṇaḥ।  
virocana kulaṃ sarvaṃ pātāle sanniveśitam ।। 36.85 ।।  
  
tataḥ sarvāmaraiśvaryaṃ dattvendrāya mahātmane।  
mānuṣeṣu mahābāhuḥ prādurāsījjanārdanaḥ ।। 36.86 ।।  
  
etāstisraḥ smṛtāstasya divyāḥ sambhūtayaḥ śubhāḥ।  
mānuṣyāḥ sapta yāstasya śāpajāṃstānnibodhata ।। 36.87 ।।  
  
tretāyuge tu daśame dattātreyo babhūva ha।  
naṣṭe dharme caturthaśca mārkaṇḍeyapuraḥsaraḥ ।। 36.88 ।।  
  
pañcamaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ tu tretāyāṃ sambabhūva ha।  
māndhātuścakravarttitve tasthau tathyapuraḥsaraḥ ।। 36.89 ।।  
  
eko naviṃśe tretāyāṃ sarvvakṣatrāntako'bhavat।  
jāmadagnyastathā ṣaṣṭo viśvāmitrapuraḥsaraḥ ।। 36.90 ।।  
  
caturviṃśe yuge rāmo vasiṣṭena purodhasā।  
saptamo rāva ṇasyārthe jajñe daśarathātmajaḥ ।। 36.91 ।।  
  
aṣṭamo dvāpare viṣṇuraṣṭāviṃśe parāśarāt ।  
vedavyāsastato jajñe jātūkarṇapuraḥsaraḥ ।। 36.92 ।।  
  
tathaiva navamo viṣṇuradityāḥ kaśyapātmajaḥ।  
devakyāṃ vasudevāttu brahnagārgyapuraḥsaraḥ ।। 36.93 ।।  
  
aprameyo niyojyaśca yatra kāmacaro vaśī।  
krījate bhagavāँ lloke bālaḥ krījanakairiva ।। 36.94 ।।  
  
na pramātuṃ mahābāhuḥ śakyo'sau madhusūdanaḥ।  
paraṃ paramametasmādviśvarūpānna vidyate ।। 36.95 ।।  
  
aṣṭāviṃśa time tadvaddvāparasyāṃśasaṅkṣaye।  
naṣṭe dharme tadā jajñe viṣṇurvṛṣṇikule prabhuḥ ।। 36.96 ।।  
  
karttuṃ dharmavyavasthānamasurāṇāṃ praṇāśanam।  
mohayan sarvabhūtāni yogātmā yogamāyayā ।। 36.97 ।।  
  
praviṣṭo mānuṣīṃ yoniṃ pracchannaścarate mahīm।  
vihārārthaṃ manuṣyeṣu sāndīpanipuraḥsaram ।। 36.98 ।।  
  
yatra kaṃsañca śālvañca dvividañca mahāsuram।  
ariṣṭaṃ vṛṣabhañcaiva pūtanāṃ keśinaṃ hayam ।। 36.99 ।।  
  
nāgaṃ kuvalayāpīḍaṃ mallarājagṛhādhipam।  
daityān mānuṣadehasthān sūdayāmāsa vīryavān ।। 36.100 ।।  
  
chinnaṃ bāhusahasrañca bāṇasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ ।  
narakaśca hataḥ saṅkhaye yavanaśca mahābalaḥ ।। 36.101 ।।  
  
hṛtāni ca mahīpānāṃ sarvaratnāni tejasā।  
durācārā śca nihatāḥ pārthivā ye rasātale ।। 36.102 ।।  
  
ete lokahitārthāya prādurbhāvā mahātmanaḥ।  
asminneva yuge kṣīṇe sandhyā śliṣṭe bhaviṣyati ।। 36.103 ।।  
  
kalkirviṣṇuyaśā nāma pārāśaryaḥ pratāpavān।  
daśamo bhāvyasambhūto yājñavalkyapuraḥsaraḥ ।। 36.104 ।।  
  
anukarṣan sarvasenāṃ hastyaśvarathasaṅkulām।  
pragṛhītāyudhaurviprairvṛtaḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ।। 36.105 ।।  
  
nātyarthaṃ dhārmikā ye ca ye ca dharmadviṣaḥ vkacit।  
īdīcyānmadhyadeśāṃśca tathā vindhyāparāntikān ।। 36.106 ।।  
  
tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃśca dravijān siṃhalaiḥ saha।  
gāndhārān pāradāṃścaiva pahlavān yavanāñchakān ।। 36.107 ।।  
  
tuṣārān barbarāṃścaiva pulindān daradān khasān ।  
lampākānandhakān rudrān kirātāṃścaiva sa prabhuḥ ।। 36.108 ।।  
  
pravṛttacakrobalavān mlecchānāmantakṛdbalī।  
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ pṛthivīṃ vicariṣyati ।। 36.109 ।।  
  
mānavaḥ sa tu saṃjajñe devasyāṃśena dhīmataḥ ।  
pūrvajanmani viṣṇuryaḥ pramitirnāma vīryavān ।। 36.110 ।।  
  
gātreṇa vai candrasamaḥ pūrṇe kaliyuge'bhavat।  
ityetāstasya devasya daśa sambhūtayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 36.111 ।।  
  
taṃ taṃ kālañca kāryañca tattaduddiśya kāraṇam।  
aṃśena triṣu lokeṣu tāstā yonīḥ prapatsyate ।। 36.112 ।।  
  
pañcaviṃśotthite kalpe pañcaviṃśati vai samāḥ।  
vinighnan sarvvabhūtāni mānuṣāneva sarvvaśaḥ ।। 36.113 ।।  
  
kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣāntu mahīṃ krūreṇa karmmaṇā।  
saṃśātayitvā vṛṣalān prāyaśastānadhārmmikān ।। 36.114 ।।  
  
tataḥ sa vai tadā kalkiścaritārthaḥ sasainikaḥ।  
karmaṇā nihatā ye tu siddhāste tu punaḥ svayam ।। 36.115 ।।  
  
akasmāt kupitānyonyaṃ bhaviṣyanti ca mohitāḥ ।  
kṣapayitvā tu tān sarvān bāvinārthena coditān ।। 36.116 ।।  
  
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye niṣṭāṃ prāpsyati sānugaḥ।  
tato vyatīte kalkau tu sāmānyaiḥ saha sainikaiḥ ।। 36.117 ।।  
  
nṛpeṣvatha vinaṣṭeṣu tadā tvapragrahāḥ prajāḥ।  
rakṣaṇe vinivṛtte tu hatvā cānyonyamāhave ।। 36.118 ।।  
  
parasparahṛtāśvāsā nirākrandāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ।  
purāṇi hitvā grāmāṃśca tulyāstā niṣparigrahāḥ ।। 36.119 ।।  
  
pranaṣṭaśrutidharmāśca naṣṭadharmāśramāstathā।  
hrasvā alpāyuṣaścaiva vanaukasa ime smṛtāḥ ।। 36.120 ।।  
  
saritparvatasevinyaḥ patramūlaphalāśanāḥ।  
cīra patrājinadharāḥ saṅkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ ।। 36.121 ।।  
  
alpāyuṣo naṣṭavārttā bahvābādhāḥ suduḥkhitāḥ।  
evaṃ kaṣṭamanuprāptāḥ kalisandhyaṃśake tadā ।। 36.122 ।।  
  
prajāḥ kṣayaṃ prayāsyanti sārddhaṃ kaliyugena tu ।  
kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmin pravṛtte ca kṛte punaḥ ।। 36.123 ।।  
  
prapatsyante yathānyāyaṃ svabhāvādeva nānyatā।  
ityetat kīrtitaṃ sarvaṃ devāsuraviceṣṭitam ।। 36.124 ।।  
  
yaduvaṃśaprasaṅgena mahadvo vaiṣṇavaṃ yaśaḥ ।  
turvasostu pravakṣyāmi pūrordruhyoranostathā ।। 36.125 ।।  
  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte viṣṇumāhātmyakathanaṃ nāma ṣaṭ‌triṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 36 ।।


---
title: 037

---
।।sūta uvāca।।  
turvasostu suto vahnirvahnergobhānurātmajaḥ।  
gobhānostu suto vīrastrisānuraparājitaḥ ।। 37.1 ।।  
karandhamastrisānostu maruttasya na cātmajaḥ।  
anyastvavīkṣito rājā maruttaḥ kathitaḥ purā ।। 37.2 ।।  
anavatyo maruttastu sa rājāsīditi śrutam।  
duṣkṛtaṃ pauravaṃ cāpi sarve putramakalpayan ।। 37.3 ।।  
evaṃ yayādiśāpena jarāyāḥ saṃkrameṇa tu ।  
turvasoḥ pauravaṃ vaṃśaṃ praviveśa purā kila ।। 37.4 ।।  
duṣkṛtasya tu dāyādaḥ śarūtho nāma pārthivaḥ।  
śarūthāttu janāpīḍaścatvārastasya cātmajāḥ ।। 37.5 ।।  
pāṇḍyaśca keralaścaiva colaḥ kulyastathaiva ca।  
teṣāṃ janapadāḥ kulyāḥ pāṇḍyāścolāḥ sakeralāḥ ।। 37.6 ।।  
druhyostu tanayau vīrau babhruḥ setuśca viśrutau।  
aruddhaḥ setuputrastu bābhravo ripurucyate ।। 37.7 ।।  
yauvanāśvena samiti kṛcchreṇa nihato balī।  
yuddhaṃ sumahadāsīttu māsān pari caturdaśa ।। 37.8 ।।  
aruddhasya tu dāyādo gāndhāro nāma pārthivaḥ।  
khyāyate yasya nāmnā tu gāndhāraviṣayo mahān ।। 37.9 ।।  
gāndhāradeśajāścāpi turagā vājināṃ varāḥ।  
gāndhāraputro dharmmastu ghṛtastasya suto'bhavat ।। 37.10 ।।  
ghṛtasya durdamo jajñe pracetāstasya cātmajaḥ ।  
pracetasaḥ putraśataṃ rājānaḥ sarva eva te ।। 37.11 ।।  
mleccharāṣṭrādhipāḥ sarve hyudīcīṃ diśamāśritāḥ।  
anoḥ putrā mahātmānastrayaḥ paramadhārmmikāḥ ।। 37.12 ।।  
sabhānaraśca pakṣaśca parapakṣastathaiva ca।  
sabhānarasya putrastu vidvān kālānalo nṛpaḥ ।। 37.13 ।।  
kālānalasya dharmmātmā sṛñjayo nāma dhārmikaḥ ।  
sṛñjayasyābhavat putro vīro rājā purañjayaḥ ।। 37.14 ।।  
janamejayo mahā satvaḥ purañjayasuto'bhavat।  
janamejayasya rājarṣermahāśālo'bhavabhṛpaḥ ।। 37.15 ।।  
āsīdindrasamo rājā pratiṣṭitayaśā divi।  
mahāmanāḥ sutastasya mahā śālasya dhārmikaḥ ।। 37.16 ।।  
saptadvīpeśvaro rājā cakravarttī mahāyaśāḥ।  
mahāmanāstu putrau dvau janayāmāsa viśrutau ।। 37.17 ।।  
uśīnarañca dharmajñaṃ titikṣuñcaiva dhārmikam।  
uśīnarasya patnyastu pañca rājarṣivaṃśajāḥ ।। 37.18 ।।  
mṛgā kṛmī navā darvā pañcamī ca dṛṣadvatī।  
uśīnarasya putrāstu pañca tāsu kulodvahāḥ।  
tapasā te sumahatā jātavṛddhāśca dhārmikāḥ ।। 37.19।  
mṛgāyāstu mṛgaḥ putro navāyā nava eva tu।  
kṛmyāḥ kṛmistu darvāyāḥ suvrato nāma dhārmikaḥ ।। 37.20 ।।  
dṛṣadvatīsutaścāpi śivirauśīnaro dvijāḥ।  
śiveḥ śivapuraṃ khyātaṃ yaudheyantu mṛgasya tu ।। 37.21 ।।  
navasya navarāṣṭrantu kṛmestu kṛmilā purī।  
suvratasya tathā vṛṣṭā śiviputrānnibodhata ।। 37.22 ।।  
śivestu śivayaḥ putrāścatvāro lokasammatāḥ।  
vṛṣadarbhaḥ suvīrastu kekayo madrakastathā ।। 37.23 ।।  
teṣāñjanapadāḥ sphītāḥ kekayā mādrakāstathā।  
vṛṣadarbhāḥ sūcidarbhāstitikṣoḥ śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ।। 37.24 ।।  
taitikṣurabhavadrājā pūrvasyāndiśi viśrutaḥ।  
uśadratho mahābāhustasya hemaḥ suto'bhavat ।। 37.25 ।।  
hemasya sutapā jajñe sutaḥ sutayaśā balī ।  
jāto manuṣyayonyāṃ vai kṣīṇe vaṃśe prajepsayā ।। 37.26 ।।  
mahāyogī sa tu balirbaddho yaḥ sa mahāmanāḥ।  
putrānutpādayāmāsa cāturvarṇyakarān bhuvi ।। 37.27 ।।  
aṅgaṃ sa janayāmāsa vaṅgaṃ suhlaṃ tathaiva ca।  
puṇḍraṃ kaliṅgañca tathā bāleyaṃ kṣatramucyate ।। 37.28 ।।  
bāleyā brāhmaṇāścaiva tasya vaṃśakarāḥ prabhoḥ।  
balestu brahmaṇā dattā varāḥ prītena dhīmate ।। 37.29 ।।  
mahāyogitvamāyuśca kalpāyuḥparimāṇakam।  
saṃgrāme cāpyajeyatvaṃ dharme caiva prabhāvanā ।। 37.30 ।।  
trailokyadarśanañcaiva prādhānyaṃ prasave tathā।  
bale cāprati matvaṃ vai dharmatattvārthadarśanam ।। 37.31 ।।  
caturo niyatān varṇān tvaṃ vai sthāpayiteti ca।  
ityukto vibhunā rājā baliḥ śāntimparāṃ yayau ।। 37.32 ।।  
kālena mahatā vidvān svaṃ vai sthānamupāgataḥ।  
teṣāṃ janapadāḥ sphītā vaṅgāṅgasuhlakāstathā ।। 37.33 ।।  
puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgāśca tathā teṣāṃ vaṃśaṃ nibedhata।  
tasya te tanayāḥ sarve kṣetrajā munisambhavāḥ।  
sambhūtā dīrghatamasaḥ sudeṇṇāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ ।। 37.34 ।।  
           ṛṣaya ūcuḥ।  
kathaṃ baleḥ sutāḥ pañca janitāḥ kṣetrajāḥ prabho।  
ṛṣiṇā dīrghatamasā etanno brūhi pṛcchatām ।। 37.35 ।।  
           sūta uvāca।।  
aśijo nāma vikhyāta āsīddhīmā nṛṣiḥ purā।  
bhāryā vai samatā nāma babhūvāsya mahātmanaḥ ।। 37.36 ।।  
aśijasya kanīyāṃstu purodhā yo divaukasām।  
bṛhaspatirbṛhattejā mamatāṃ so'bhyapadyata ।। 37.37 ।।  
uvāca mamatā tantu bṛhaspatimanicchatī।  
antarvatnyasmi te bhrāturjyeṣṭhasyāṣṭamitā iti ।। 37.38 ।।  
ayaṃ hi me mahāgarbho rodate'ti bṛhaspate।  
aśijaṃ brahmacābhyasya ṣaḍaṅgaṃ vedamudgiran ।। 37.39 ।।  
amogharetāstvañcāpi na māṃ bhajitamarhasi।  
asminneva gate kāle yathā vā manyase prabho ।। 37.40 ।।  
evamuktastayā samyag bṛhattejā bṛhaspatiḥ।  
kāmātmānaṃ mahātmā ca nātmānaṃ so'bhyadhārayat ।। 37.41 ।।  
sambabhūvaiva dharmātmā tayā sārddhaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ।  
utsṛjantaṃ tadā reto garbhasthaḥ so'bhyabhāṣata ।। 37.42 ।।  
no snātako nyaseddhyasmin dvayornehāsti sambhavaḥ।  
amogharetāstvañcāpi pūrvañcāhamihāgataḥ ।। 37.43 ।।  
śaśāpa taṃ tadā kruddha evamukto bṛhaspatiḥ।  
āśijantaṃ sutaṃ bhrāturgarbhasthaṃ bhagavānṛṣiḥ ।। 37.44 ।।  
yasmāttvamīdṛśe kāle sarvabhūtepsite sati।  
māmevamuktavān mohāttamo dīrghaṃ pravekṣyasi ।। 37.45 ।।  
tato dīrghatamā nāma śāpādṛṣirajāyata।  
athāśijo bṛhatkīrttirbṛhaspatirivaujasā ।। 37.46 ।।  
ūrddhvaretāstataścāpi nyavasadbhrāturāśrame।  
godharmaṃ saurabheyāttu vṛṣabhācchrutavān prabho ।। 37.47 ।।  
tasya bhrātā pitṛvyastu cakāra bhavanaṃ tadā।  
tasmin hi tatra vasati yadṛcchābhyāgato vṛṣaḥ ।। 37.48 ।।  
darśārthamāhṛtān darbhāṃścacāra surabhīvṛtaḥ।  
jagrāha taṃ dīrghatamā visphurantañca śrṛṅgayoḥ ।। 37.49 ।।  
sa tena nigṛhītastu na cacāla padātpadam।  
tato'bravīdvṛṣastaṃ vai muñca māṃ balināṃ vara ।। 37.50 ।।  
na mayāsāditastāta balavaṃstvadvidhaḥ kvacit।  
tryambakaṃ vahatā devaṃ yato jāto'smi bhūtale ।। 37.51 ।।  
muñca māṃ balināṃ śraṣṭha prītaste'haṃ varaṃ vṛṇu।  
evamukto'bravīdenaṃ jīvastvaṃ me kva yāsyasi ।। 37.52 ।।  
tena tvāhaṃ na mokṣyāmi parasvāhaṃ catuṣpadam।  
tatastaṃ dīrghatamasaṃ sa vṛṣaḥ pratyuvāca ha ।। 37.53 ।।  
nāsmākaṃ vidyate tāta pātakaṃ steyameva vā।  
bhakṣyābhakṣyaṃ na jānīmaḥ peyāpeyañca sarvaśaḥ ।। 37.54 ।।  
kāryākāryaṃ na vai vijho gamyāgamyaṃ tathaiva ca।  
na pāpmāno vayaṃ vipra dharmo hyeṣāṃ gavāṃ smṛtaḥ ।। 37.55 ।।  
gavāṃ nāma sa vai śrutvā saṃbhrāntastvanumucya tam।  
bhaktyā cānuśravikayā goṣu taṃ vai prasāda yat ।। 37.56 ।।  
prasādite gate tasmin godharmaṃ bhaktitastu tam।  
manasaiva tadādatte tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ ।। 37.57 ।।  
tato yavīyasaḥ patnīmautathyasyābhyamanyata।  
viceṣṭamānāṃ rudatīṃ daivāt sa mūḍhacetanaḥ ।। 37.58 ।।  
avalepantu taṃ matvā śaradvāṃstasya nākṣamat।  
godharmaṃvai balaṃ kṛtvā snuṣāṃ sa samamanyata ।। 37.59 ।।  
viparyayantu taṃ dṛṣṭvā śaradvān pratyacintayat।  
bhaviṣyamarthaṃ jñātvā ca mahātmā ca na mṛtyutām ।। 37.60 ।।  
provāca dīrghatamasaṃ krodhāt saṃrakta locanaḥ।  
gamyāgamyaṃ na jīnīṣe godharmāt prārthayat snuṣām ।। 37.61 ।।  
durvṛttastvaṃ tyajāmyeva gaccha tvaṃ svena karmaṇā।  
yasmāttvamandho vṛddhaśca bharttavyo duranuṣṭitaḥ।  
tenāsi tvaṃ parityakto durācāro'si me matiḥ ।। 37.62 ।।  
          sūta uvāca।।  
karmaṇyasmistataḥ krūre tasya buddhirajāyata।  
nirbhatsya caiva bahuśo bāhubhyāṃ parigṛhya ca।  
koṣṭe samudre prakṣipya gaṅgāmbhasi samutsṛjat ।। 37.63 ।।  
uhyamānaḥ samudrastu saptāhaṃ srotasā tadā।  
taṃ sastrīko balirnāma rājā dharmārthatattvavit।  
apaśyanmajjamānantu srotasābhyāśamāgatam ।। 37.64 ।।  
taṃ gṛhītvā sa dharmātmā balirvairocanastadā।  
antaḥpure jugopainaṃ bhakṣyairbhojyaiśca tarpayan ।। 37.65 ।।  
prītaḥ sa vai vareṇātha cchandayāmāsa vai balim।  
sa ca tasmādvaraṃ vavre putrārthaṃ dānavarṣabhaḥ ।। 37.66 ।।  
            ।।baliruvāca।।  
santānārthaṃ mahābhāga bhāryayā mama mānada।  
putrān dharmārthasaṃyuktānutpādayitumarhasi ।। 37.67 ।।  
evamuktastu tenarṣistathāstvityuktavān hi tam ।  
sudeṣṇāṃ nāma bāryāṃ vai rājāsmai prāhiṇottadā ।। 37.68 ।।  
andhaṃ vṛddhañca taṃ dṛṣṭvā na sā devī jagāma ha ।  
svāñca dhātreyakīṃ tasmai bhūṣayitvā vyasarjayat ।। 37.69 ।।  
kakṣīvacakṣuṣau tasyāṃ śūdrayonyāmṛṣirvaśī।  
janayāmāsa dharmātmā putrāvetau mahojasau ।। 37.70 ।।  
kakṣivacakṣuṣau tau tu dṛṣṭvā rājā balistadā।  
prādhītau vidhivatsamyagīśvarau brahmavādinau ।। 37.71 ।।  
siddhau pratyakṣadharmāṇau buddhau śreṣṭhatamāvapi।  
mamaitāviti hovāca balirvairocanastvṛṣim ।। 37.72 ।।  
netyuvāca tatastantu mamaitāviti cābravīt।  
utpannau śūdrayonau tu bhavacchadmā surottamau ।। 37.73 ।।  
anadhaṃ bṛddhaṃ ca māṃ matvā sudeṣṇā mahiṣī tava।  
prāhiṇodavamānāya śūdrāṃ dhātreyakīṃ mama ।। 37.74 ।।  
tataḥ prasādayāmāsa punastamṛṣisattamam।  
balirbhāryāṃ sudeṣṇāṃ ca bhartsayāmāsa vai prabhuḥ ।। 37.75 ।।  
punaścaināmalaṃkṛtya ṛṣaye pratyapādayat।  
tāṃ sa dīrghatamā devīmabravīdyadi māṃ śubhe ।। 37.76 ।।  
dadhnā lavaṇamiśreṇa svabya(vya)ktaṃ nagnakaṃ tathā।  
lihiṣyasyajugupsantī hyāpādatalamastakam ।। 37.77 ।।  
tatastvaṃ prāpsyase devi putrāṃśca manasepsitān।  
tasya sā tadvaco devī sarvaṃ kṛtavatī tathā ।। 37.78 ।।  
apānañca samāsādya jugupsantī nyavarjayat।  
tāmuvāca tataḥ sarṣiryatte parihṛtaṃ śubhe।  
vināpānaṃ kumāraṃ tvaṃ janayiṣyasi pūrvajam ।। 37.79 ।।  
tatastaṃ dīrghatamasaṃ sā devī pratyuvāca ha।  
nārhasi tvaṃ mahābhāga putraṃ dātuṃ mamedṛśam ।। 37.80 ।।  
           ।।ṛṣiruvāca।।  
tavāparādho devyeṣa nānyathā bhavitānu vai ।  
devī dānīñca te putramahaṃ dāsyāmi suvrate ।। 37.81 ।।  
tasyāpānaṃ vinā caiva yogyābhāvo bhaviṣyati।  
tāṃ sa dīrghatamāścaiva kukṣau spṛṣṭvedamabravavīt ।। 37.82 ।।  
prāśitaṃ dadhi yatte'dya mamāṅgādvai śucismite ।  
tena te pūrito garbhaḥ paurṇamāsyāmivodadhiḥ ।। 37.83 ।।  
bhaviṣyanti kumārāste pañca devasutopamāḥ।  
tejasvinaḥ parākrāntā yajvāno dhārmikāstathā ।। 37.84 ।।  
tatoṅgastu sudeṣṇāyā jyeṣṭhaputro vyajāyata।  
vaṅgastasmātkaliṅgastu puṇḍro brahmastathaiva ca ।। 37.85 ।।  
vaṃśabhājastu pañcaite baleḥ kṣetre'bhavaṃstadā।  
ityete dīrghatamasā balerdattāḥ sutāḥ purā ।। 37.86 ।।  
prajāstvapahatāstasya brahmaṇā kāraṇaṃ prati।  
apatyā mātyadāreṣu sveṣu mā bhūnmahātmanaḥ ।। 37.87 ।।  
tato manuṣyayonyāṃ vai janayāmāsa sa prajāḥ।  
surabhirdīrghatamasamatha prīto vaco'bravīt ।। 37.88 ।।  
vicārya yasmādgodharmmaṃ tvamevaṃ kṛtavānasi ।  
tena nyāyena mumuce hyahaṃ prītosmi tena te ।। 37.89 ।।  
tasmāttava tamo dīrghaṃ nistudāmyadya paśya vai।  
bārhaspatyañca yatte'nyatpāpaṃ santiṣṭhate tanau ।। 37.90 ।।  
jarāmṛtyubhayañcaiva āghrāya praṇudāmi te।  
hyāghrātamātraḥ so'paśyata sadyastamasi nāśite ।। 37.91 ।।  
āyuṣmāṃśca yuvā caiva cakṣuṣmāṃśca tato'bhavat।  
gavā dīrghatamāḥ so'tha gautamaḥ samapadyata ।। 37.92 ।।  
kakṣīvāṃstu tato gatvā saha pitrā giriprajām।  
yathoddiṣṭaṃ hi pitrarthe cacāra vipulaṃ tapaḥ ।। 37.93 ।।  
tataḥ kālena mahatā tamasā bhāvitaḥ savai।  
vidhūya manujo doṣān brahmaṇyaṃ prāptavān prabhuḥ ।। 37.94।  
tato'bravīt pitā cainaṃ putravānasmyahaṃ prabho।  
satputreṇa tvayā tāta kṛtārtho'smi yaśasvinā ।। 37.95 ।।  
yuktātmā hi tataḥ so'tha prāptavān brahmaṇā kṣayam।  
brahmaṇyaṃ prāpya kakṣīvān sahasramasṛjat sutān ।। 37.96 ।।  
kṛṣṇāṅgā gautamāste vai smṛtāḥ kakṣīvataḥ sutāḥ।  
ityeṣa dīrghatamaso balervairocanasya vai ।। 37.97 ।।  
samāgamaḥ samākhyātaḥ santānañcobhayostayoḥ।  
balistānabiṣicyeha pañca putrānakalmaṣān ।। 37.98 ।।  
kṛtārthaḥ so'pi yogātmā yogamāśritya ca prabhuḥ।  
adṛśyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kālākāṅkṣī caratyuta ।। 37.99 ।।  
tatrāṅgasya tu rājarṣe rājāsīddadhivāhanaḥ।  
sāparādhasudeṣṇāyā anapāno'bhavanṛpaḥ ।। 37.100 ।।  
anapānasya putrastu rājā divirathaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
putro divirathasyāsīdvidvān dharmaratho nṛpaḥ ।। 37.101 ।।  
sa vai dharmarathaḥ śrīmān yena viṣṇupade girau।  
somaḥ śakreṇa saha vai yajñe pīto mahātmanā ।। 37.102 ।।  
śrṛṇu dharmmarathasyāpi rājā citraratho'bhavat।  
lomapāda iti khyāto yasya śāntā sutā'bhavat ।। 37.103 ।।  
jajñe vai caṇḍikastasya vāraṇaḥ śakravāraṇaḥ।  
ānayāmāsa sa mahīṃ mandhorvāhanamuttamam ।। 37.104 ।।*(pāṭhabhedaḥ)  
haryyaṅgasya tu dāyādo rājā bhadrarathaḥ kila।  
atha bhadrarathasyāsīdbṛhatkarmā prajeśvaraḥ ।। 37.105 ।।  
bṛhadrathaḥ sutastasya tasmājjajñe bṛhanmanāḥ।  
bṛhanmanāstu rājendraṃ janayāmāsa vai sutam ।। 37.106 ।।  
nāmnā jayadrathaṃ nāma tasmādṝḍharatho nṛpaḥ।  
āsīdṝḍharathasyāpi viśvajijjanamejayaḥ ।। 37.107 ।।  
dāyādastasya cāṅgebhyo yasmāt karṇo'bhavannṛpaḥ।  
karṇasya śūrasenastu dvija stasyātmajaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 37.108 ।।  
             ।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
sūtātmajaḥ kathaṃ karṇaḥ kathaṃ cāṅgasya vaṃśajaḥ।  
etadicchāmahe śrotumatyarthaṃ kuśalo hyasi ।। 37.109 ।।  
           ।।sūta uvāca।।  
bṛhadbhānoḥ suto jajñe nāmnā rājā bṛhanmanāḥ।  
tasya patnīdvayaṃ cāsīccaidyasyobhe ca te sute ।। 37.110 ।।  
yaśodevī ca satyā ca tābhyāṃ vaṃśastu bhidyate।  
jayadrathastu rājendro yaśodevyāṃ vyajāyata ।। 37.111 ।।  
brahmakṣatrāntaraḥ satyāvijayo nāma viśrutaḥ।  
vijayasya dhṛtiḥ putra stasya putro dhṛtavrataḥ ।। 37.112 ।।  
dhṛtavratasya putrastu satyakarmā mahāyaśāḥ।  
satyakarmasutaścāpi sūtastvadhirathastu vai ।। 37.113 ।।  
sa karṇaṃ parijagrāha tena karṇastu sūtajaḥ।  
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ karṇe yadvai pracoditam ।। 37.114 ।।  
ete'ṅgavaṃśajāḥ sarve rājānaḥ kīrttitā mayā।  
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca pūrostu śrṛṇuta prajāḥ ।। 37.115 ।।  
           sūta uvāca।।  
pūroḥ putro mahābāhū rājāsījjanamejayaḥ।  
aviddhastu sutastasya yaḥ prācīmajayaddiśam ।। 37.116 ।।  
aviddhataḥ pravīrastu manasyurabhavatsutaḥ।  
rājātho jayado nāma manasyorabhavatsutaḥ ।। 37.117 ।।  
dāyādastasya cāpyāsīddhundhurnāma mahīpatiḥ।  
dhundhorbahu gavī putraḥ sañjātistasya cātmajaḥ ।। 37.118 ।।  
sañjāteratha raudrāśvastasya putrānnibodhata।  
raudrāśvasya ghṛtācyāṃ vai daśāpsarasi sūnavaḥ ।। 37.119 ।।  
rajeyuśca kṛte yuśca vakṣeyuḥ sthaṇḍileyu ca।  
ghṛteyuśca jaleyuśca sthaleyuścaiva saptamaḥ ।। 37.120 ।।  
dharmeyuḥ sannateyuśca vaneyurddaśamastu saḥ।  
rudrā śūdrā ca madrā ca śubhā jāmalajā tathā ।। 37.121 ।।  
talā khalā ca saptaitā yā ca gopajalā smṛtā।  
tathā tāmrarasā caiva ratnakūṭī ca tādṛśī ।। 37.122 ।।  
ātreyo vaṃśatastāsāṃ bharttā nāmnā prabhākaraḥ।  
anādṛṣṭastu rājarṣī riveyustasya cātmajaḥ ।। 37.123 ।।  
riveyorjvalanā nāma bhāryā vai takṣakātmajā।  
yasyāṃ devyāṃ sa rājarṣī rantiṃ nāma tvajījanat ।। 37.124 ।।  
rantirnāraḥ sarasvatyāṃ putrānajanayacchubhān।  
trasuṃ tathā pratirathaṃ dhruvañcaivātidhārmikam ।। 37.125 ।।  
gaurī kanyā ca vikhyātā māndhāturjananī śubhā।  
dhuryaḥ pratirathasyāpi kaṇṭhastasyābhavat sutaḥ ।। 37.126 ।।  
medhātithiḥ surastasya yasmāt kāṇṭāyanā dvijāḥ।  
itinānuyamasyāsīt kanyā sājanayatsutān ।। 37.127 ।।  
trasuḥ sudayitaṃputraṃ malinaṃ brahmavādinam।  
upadātaṃ tato lebhe caturastviti sātmajān ।। 37.128 ।।  
suṣmantamatha duṣyantaṃ pravīramanaghantathā।  
cakravarttī tato jajñe dauṣyantirnṛpasattamaḥ ।। 37.129 ।।  
śakuntalāyāṃ bharato yasya nāmnā tu bhāratam।  
duṣyantaṃ prati rājānaṃ vāguvācāśarīriṇī ।। 37.130 ।।  
mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa eva saḥ।  
bharasva putraṃ duṣyantaṃ satyamāha śakuntalā ।। 37.131 ।।  
retodhāḥ putraṃ nayati naradeva yamakṣayāt।  
tvañcāsya dhātā garbhasya māvamaṃsthāḥ śakuntalām ।। 37.132 ।।  
bharatastrisṛṣu strīṣu nava putrānajījanat।  
nābhyanandacca tān rājā nānurūpānmametyuta ।। 37.133 ।।  
tatastā mātaraḥ kruddhāḥ putrānninyuryamakṣayam।  
tatastasya narendrasya vitataṃ putrajanma tat ।। 37.134 ।।  
tato marudbhirānīya putrastu sa bṛhaspateḥ।  
saṅkrāmito bharadvājo marudbhiḥ kratubhirvibhuḥ ।। 37.135 ।।  
tatraivodārahantīdaṃ bharadvājasya dhīmataḥ।  
janmasaṅkramaṇañcaiva marudbhirbharatāya vai ।। 37.136 ।।  
patnyāmāsannagarbhāyāmaśijaḥ saṃsthitaḥ kilaḥ।  
bhrāturbhāryāṃ sa dṛṣṭvātha bṛhaspatiruvāca ha।  
alaṃkṛtya tanuṃ svāntu maithunaṃ dehi me śubhe ।। 37.137 ।।  
evamuktā'bravīdena mantarvatnī hyahaṃ vibho।  
garbhaḥ pariṇataścāyaṃ brahma vyāharate girā ।। 37.138 ।।  
amogharetāstvañcāpi dharmaścaiva vigarhitaḥ।  
evamukto'bravīdenāṃ smayamāno bṛhaspatiḥ ।। 37.139 ।।  
vinayo nopadeṣṭavyastvayā mama kathañcana।  
harṣamāṇaḥ prasahyaināṃ maithunāyopacakrame ।। 37.140 ।।  
tato bṛhaspatiṃ garbho harṣamāṇamuvāca ha।  
sanniviṣṭo hyahaṃ pūrvamiha tāta bṛhaspate ।। 37.141 ।।  
amogharetāśca bhavānnāvakāśo'sti ca dvayoḥ।  
evamuktaḥ sa garbheṇa kupitaḥ pratyuvāca ha ।। 37.142 ।।  
yasmānmāmīdṛśe kāle sarvabhūtepsite sati।  
pratiṣedhasitattasmāt tamo dīrghaṃ pravekṣyasi ।। 37.143 ।।  
pādābhyāntena tacchannaṃ māturdvāraṃ bṛhaspateḥ।  
tadretastu tayormadhye nivāryaḥ śiśuko'bhavat ।। 37.144 ।।  
sadyo jātaṃ kumārantaṃ dṛṣṭvā'tha mamatā'bravīt।  
gamiṣyāmi gṛhaṃ svaṃ vai bharadvājaṃ bṛhaspate ।। 37.145 ।।  
evamuktvā gatāyāṃ sa putrantyajati tatkṣaṇāt।  
bharasva bāḍhamityukto bharadvājastato'bhavat ।। 37.146 ।।  
mātāpitṛbhyāṃ saṃtyaktaṃ dṛṣṭvātha marutaḥ śiśum।  
gṛhītvainaṃ bharadvājaṃ jagmuste kṛpayā tataḥ ।। 37.147 ।।  
tasmin kāle tu bharato marudbhiḥ kratubhiḥ kramāt।  
kāmyanaimittikairyajñairyajate putralipsayā ।। 37.148 ।।  
yadā sa yajamāno vai putrānnāsādayat prabhuḥ ।  
yajñaṃ tato marutsomaṃ putrārthe punarāharat ।। 37.149 ।।  
tena te marutastasya marutsomena toṣitāḥ।  
bharadvājaṃ tataḥ putraṃ bārhaspatyaṃ manīṣiṇam ।। 37.150 ।।  
bharatastu bharadvājaṃ putraṃ prāpya tadābravīt।  
prajāyāṃ saṃhṛtāyāṃ vai kṛtārtho'haṃ tvayā vibho ।। 37.151 ।।  
pūrvantu vitathaṃ tasya kṛtaṃ vai putrajanma hi।  
tataḥ sa vitatho nāma bharadvājastathā'bhavat ।। 37.152 ।।  
tasmāddivyo bharadvājo brāhmaṇyāt kṣatriyo'bhavat।  
dvimukhyāyananāmā sa smṛto dvipitṛkastu vai ।। 37.153 ।।  
tato'tha vitathe jāte bharataḥ sa divaṃ yayau।  
vitathasya tu dāyādo bhuvamanyurbabhūva ha ।। 37.154 ।।  
mahābhūtopamāścāsaṃścatvāro bhuvamanyujāḥ।  
bṛhatkṣatro mahāvīryo naro gāgraśca vīryavān ।। 37.155 ।।  
narasya sāṃkṛtiḥ putrastasya putrau mahaujasau।  
guruvīryastridevaśca sāṃkṛtyāvavarau smṛtau ।। 37.156 ।।  
dāyādāścāpi gāgrasya śinibaddhāt babhūva ha।  
smṛtāścaite tato gāgryāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ ।। 37.157 ।।  
mahāvīryasutaścāpi bhīmastasmādubhakṣayaḥ।  
tasya bhāryā viśālā tu suṣuve vai sutāṃstrayaḥ ।। 37.158 ।।  
trayyāruṇiṃ puṣkariṇaṃ tṛtīyaṃ suṣuve kapim।  
kapeḥ kṣatravarā hyete tayoḥ proktā maharṣayaḥ ।। 37.159 ।।  
gāgrāḥ sāṃkṛtayo vīryāḥ kṣātropetā dvijātayaḥ।  
saṃśritāṅgirasaṃ pakṣaṃ bṛhatkṣatrasya vakṣyati ।। 37.160 ।।  
bṛhatkṣatrasya dāyādaḥ suhotro nāma dhārmikaḥ।  
suhotrasyāpi dāyādo hastī nāma babhūva ha।  
tenedaṃ nirmitaṃ pūrvaṃ nāmnā vai hāstinaṃ puram ।। 37.161 ।।  
hastinaścāpi dāyādāstrayaḥ paramadhārmikāḥ।  
ajamīḍho dvimīḍhaśca purumīḍhastathaiva ca ।। 37.162 ।।  
ajamīḍhasya putrāstu śabhāḥ śubhakulodvahāḥ।  
tapaso'nte sumahato rājño vṛddhasya dhārmikāḥ ।। 37.163 ।।  
bharadvājaprasādena śrṛṇudhvaṃ tasya vistaram।  
aja mīḍhasya keśinyāṃ kaṇṭhaḥ samabhavatkila ।। 37.164 ।।  
medhātithiḥ sutastasya tasmāt kaṇṭāyanā dvijāḥ।  
ajamīḍhasya dhūminyāṃ jajñe bṛhadvasurnṛpaḥ ।। 37.165 ।।  
bṛhadvasorbṛhadviṣṇuḥ putrastasya mahābalaḥ।  
bṛhatkarmā sutastasya putrastasya bṛhadrathaḥ ।। 37.166 ।।  
viśvajittanayastasya senajittasya cātmajaḥ।  
atha senajitaḥ putrāścatvāro lokaviśrutāḥ ।। 37.167 ।।  
rucirāśvaśca kāvyaśca rāmo dṛḍhadhanustathā।  
vatsaścāvantako rājā yasya te parivatsarāḥ ।। 37.168 ।।  
rucirāśvasya dāyādaḥ pṛthuṣeṇo mahāyaśāḥ।  
pṛthuṣeṇasya pārastu pārānnīpo'tha jajñivān ।। 37.169 ।।  
yasya caikaśatañcāsīt putrāṇāmiti naḥ śrutam।  
nīpā iti samākhyātā rājānaḥ sarva eva te ।। 37.170 ।।  
teṣāṃ vaṃśakaraḥ śrīmān rājāsītkīrttivarddhanaḥ।  
kāmpilye samaro nāma sa ceṣṭasamaro'bhavat ।। 37.171 ।।  
samarasya paraḥ pāraḥ satvadaśca iti trayaḥ।  
putrāḥ sarvaguṇopetāḥ pāraputro vṛṣurbabhau ।। 37.172 ।।  
vṛṣostu sukṛtirnāma sukṛteneha karmaṇā।  
jajñe sarvaguṇopeto vibrājastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 37.173 ।।  
vibhrājasya tu dāyādastvaṇuho nāma pārthivaḥ।  
babhūva śukajāmātā ṛcībharttā mahāyaśāḥ ।। 37.174 ।।  
aṇuhasya tu dāyādo brahmadatto mahātapāḥ।  
yogasūnuḥ sutastasya viṣvakseno'bhavanṛpaḥ ।। 37.175 ।।  
vibrājaputrā rājānaḥ kukṛteneha karmmaṇā।  
viṣvaksenasya putrastu udakseno babhūva ha ।। 37.176 ।।  
bhallāṭastasya dāyādo yena rājā purāhataḥ।  
bhallāṭasya tu dāyādo rājāsījjanamejayaḥ।  
ugrāyudhena tasyārthe sarve nīpāḥ praṇāśitāḥ ।। 37.177 ।।  
            ।।ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
ugrāyudhaḥ kasya sutaḥ kasmin vaṃśe ca kīrtyate।  
kimarthañcaiva nīpāste tena sarve praṇāśitāḥ ।। 37.178 ।।  
          ।।sūta uvāca।।  
dvimīḍhasya tu dāyādo vidvān jajñe yavīnaraḥ।  
dhṛtimāṃstasya putrastu tasya satyadhṛtiḥ sutaḥ ।। 37.179 ।।  
atha satyadhṛteḥ putro dṛḍhanemiḥ pratāpavān ।  
dṛḍhanemisutaścāpi suvarmā nāma pārthivaḥ ।। 37.180 ।।  
āsītsuvarmmaṇaḥ putraḥ sārvabhaumaḥ pratāpavān।  
sārvabhauma iti khyātaḥ pṛthivyāmekarāḍbabhau ।। 37.181 ।।  
tasyānvaye ca mahati mahatpauravanandanaḥ।  
mahatpauravaputrastu rājā rukmarathaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 37.182 ।।  
atha rukmarathasyāpi supārśvo nāma pārthivaḥ।  
supārśvatanayaścāpi sumatirnāma dhārmikaḥ ।। 37.183 ।।  
sumaterapi dharmmātmā rājā sannatimān prabhuḥ।  
tasyāsītsanatirnāma kṛtastasya suto'bhavat ।। 37.184 ।।  
śiṣyo hiraṇyanābhestu kauthumasya mahātmanaḥ।  
caturviṃśatidhā tena proktāstāḥ sāmasaṃhitāḥ ।। 37.185 ।।  
smṛtāste prācyanāmānaḥ kārttāḥ sāmnāntu sāmagaḥ ।  
kārtirugrāyudhaḥ so'tha vīraḥ pauravanandanaḥ ।। 37.186 ।।  
babhūva yena vikramya pṛṣatasya pitāmahaḥ।  
nīlo nāma mahābāhuḥ pañcālādhipatirhataḥ ।। 37.187 ।।  
ugrāyudhasya dāyādaḥ kṣemo nāma mahāyaśāḥ।  
kṣemātsu vīraḥ saṃjajñe suvīrasya nṛpañjayaḥ।  
nṛpañjayādvīraratho ityete pauravāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 37.188 ।।  
ajamīḍhasya nīlinyāṃ nīlaḥ samabhavannṛpaḥ।  
nīlasya tapasogreṇa suśāntirabhyajāyata ।। 37.189 ।।  
purujānuḥ suśāntestu rikṣastu purujānujaḥ।  
tatastu rikṣadāyādā bhedāśca tanayāstvime ।। 37.190 ।।  
mudgalaḥ sṛñjayaścaiva rājā bṛhadiṣustathā ।  
yavīyāṃścāpi vikrāntaḥ kampilyaścaiva pañcamaḥ ।। 37.191 ।।  
pañcānāṃ rakṣaṇārthāya pitaitānabhyabhāṣata।  
pañcānāṃ viddhi pañcaitān sphītā janapadā yutāḥ ।। 37.192 ।।  
alaṃ saṃrakṣaṇe teṣāṃ pañcālā iti viśrutāḥ।  
mudgalasyāpi maudgalyāḥ kṣātropetadvijātayaḥ ।। 37.193 ।।  
ete hyaṅgirasaḥ pakṣe saṃśritāḥ kaṇṭhamudghalāḥ ।  
mudghalasya suto jyeṣṭo brahmiṣṭhaḥ sumahāyaśāḥ ।। 37.194 ।।  
indrasenā yato garbhaṃ badhyaśvaṃ pratyapadyata।  
badhyaśvānmithunaṃ jajñe menakā iti naḥ śrutiḥ ।। 37.195 ।।  
divodāsaśca rājarṣirahalyā ca yaśasvinī।  
śāradvatastu dāyādamahalyā samasūyata ।। 37.196 ।।  
śatānandamṛṣiśreṣṭhaṃ tasyāpi sumahāyaśāḥ।  
putraḥ satyadhṛtirnāma dhanurvedasya pāragaḥ ।। 37.197 ।।  
atha satyadhṛteḥ śukraṃ dṛṣṭvāpsarasamagrataḥ।  
pracaskande śarastambe maithunaṃ samapadyata ।। 37.198 ।।  
kṛpayā tacca jagrāha śantanurmṛgayāṃ gataḥ।  
kṛpaḥ smṛtaḥ sa vai tasmādgautamī ca kṛpī tathā ।। 37.199 ।।  
ete śāradvatāḥ proktāḥ ṛtathyo gautamānvayaḥ।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi divodāsasya santatim ।। 37.200 ।।  
divodāsasya dāyādo brahmiṣṭo mitrayurnṛpaḥ।  
maitreyastu tato jajñe smṛtā ete'pi saṃśritāḥ ।। 37.201 ।।  
ete'pi saṃśritāḥ pakṣaṃ kṣātropetāstu bhārgavāḥ।  
rājāpi cyavano vidvāṃstataḥ pratiratho'bhavat ।। 37.202 ।।  
atha vai cyavanāddhīmān sudāsaḥ samapadyata।  
saudāsaḥ sahadevaśca somakastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 37.203 ।।  
ajamīḍhaḥ punarjātaḥ kṣīṇe vaṃśe sa somakaḥ।  
somakasya suto janturhate tasmiñchataṃ vibho ।। 37.204 ।।  
puṣāṇāmajamīḍhasya somakatve mahātmanaḥ।  
teṣāṃ yavīyān pṛṣato drupadasya pitāmahaḥ ।। 37.205 ।।  
dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ sutastasya dhṛṣṭaketuśca tatsutaḥ।  
mahiṣī cājamīḍhasya dhūminī putragardhinī ।। 37.206 ।।  
punarbhave tapastepe śataṃ varṣāṇi duścaram।  
hutāgnyanidrā hyabhavat pavitramitabhojanā ।। 37.207 ।।  
ahorātraṃ kuśeṣveva suṣvāpa sumahāvratā।  
tasyāṃ vai dhūmravarṇāyāmajamīḍhaśca vīryavān ।। 37.208 ।।  
ṛkṣaṃ saṃjanayāmāsa dhūmravarṇa sitāgrajam।  
ṛkṣāt saṃvaraṇo jajñe kuruḥ saṃvaraṇādabhūt ।। 37.209 ।।  
yaḥ prayāgaṃ padākramya kurukṣetrañcakāra ha।  
kṛṣṭvainaṃ sumahātejā varṣāṇi subahūnyatha ।। 37.210 ।।  
kṛṣyamāṇe tadā śakrastatrāsya varado babhau।  
puṇyañca ramaṇīyañca puṇyakṛdbhirniṣevitam ।। 37.211 ।।  
tasyānvavāyajāḥ khyātāḥ kuravo nṛpasattamāḥ।  
kurostu dayitāḥ putrāḥ sudhanvā jahnureva ca ।। 37.212 ।।  
parikṣito mahārājaḥ putrakaścārimardanaḥ।  
sudhanvanastu dāyādaḥ suhotro matimān smṛtaḥ ।। 37.213 ।।  
cyavanastasya putrastu rājā dharmārthakovidaḥ।  
cyavanasya kṛtaḥ putra iṣṭvā yajñairmahātapāḥ ।। 37.214 ।।  
viśrutaṃ janayāmāsa putramindrasakhaṃ nṛpaḥ।  
vidyoparicaraṃ vīraṃ vasuṃ nāmāntarikṣagam ।। 37.215 ।।  
vidyoparicarājjajñe girikā sapta sūnavaḥ।  
mahāratho bhagadharo viśruto yo bṛhadrathaḥ ।। 37.216 ।।  
pratyagrahaḥ kuśaścaiva yamāhurmaṇivāhanam।  
māthailyaśca lalitthaśca matsyakālaśca saptamaḥ ।। 37.217 ।।  
bṛhadrathasya dāyādaḥ kuśāgro nāma viśrutaḥ।  
kuśāgrasyātmajaścaiva ṛṣabho nāma vīryavān ।। 37.218 ।।  
ṛṣabhasyāpi dāyādaḥ puṣpavānnāma dhārmikaḥ।  
vikrāntastasya dāyādo rājā satyahitaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 37.219 ।।  
tasya putraḥ sudhanvā ca tasmādūrjjaḥ pratāpavān।  
ūrjjasya nabhasaḥ putrastasmājjajñe sa vīryavān ।। 37.220 ।।  
śakale dve sa vai jāto jarayā sandhitastu saḥ।  
jarāsandho mahābāhurjarayā sandhitastu saḥ ।। 37.221 ।।  
sarvakṣatrasya jetā'sau jarāsandho mahābalaḥ।  
jarāsandhasya putrastu sahadevaḥ pratāpavān ।। 37.222 ।।  
sahatevātmajaḥ śrīmān somādhiḥ sumahātapāḥ।  
śrutaśruvastu somādhermāgadhaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।। 37.223 ।।  
        ।।sūta uvāca।।  
parikṣitasya dāyādo babhūva janamejayaḥ।  
śrutasenasya dāyādo bhīmaseno'pi nāmataḥ ।। 37.224 ।।  
jahnustvajanayatputraṃ surathaṃ nāma bhūmipam।  
surathasya tu dāyādo vīro rājā vidūrathaḥ ।। 37.225 ।।  
vidūrathasutaścāpi sārvabhauma iti śrutiḥ।  
sārvabhaumā jjayatsena ārādhistasya cātmajaḥ ।। 37.226 ।।  
ārādhito mahāsattva ayutāyustataḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
akrodhano'yutāyo'stu tasmāddevātithiḥ smṛtaḥ ।। 37.227 ।।  
devātithestu dāyāda ṛkṣa eva babhūva ha।  
bhīmasenastathā ṛkṣāddilīpastasya cātmajaḥ ।। 37.228 ।।  
dilīpasūnuḥ pratipastasya putrāstrayaḥ smṛtāḥ।  
devāpiḥ śantanuścaiva bāhlīkaścaiva te trayaḥ ।। 37.229 ।।  
bāhlīkasya tu vijñeyaḥ saptabāhlīśvaro nṛpaḥ।  
bāhlīkasya sutaścaiva somadatto mahāyaśāḥ ।। 37.230 ।।  
jajñire somadattāttu bhūrirbhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ ।  
devāpistu pravavrāja vanaṃ dharmmaparīpsayā ।। 37.231 ।।  
upādhyāyastu devānāṃ devāpirabhavanmuniḥ।  
cyavano'sya hi putrastu iṣṭakaśca mahātmanaḥ ।। 37.232 ।।  
śantanustvabhavadrājā vidvān vai sa mahābhiṣaḥ ।  
imaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ prati mahābhiṣam ।। 37.233 ।।  
yaṃ yaṃ rājā spṛśati vai jīrṇaṃ samayato naram।  
punaryuvā sa bhavati tasmātte śantanuṃ viduḥ ।। 37.234 ।।  
tato'sya śantanutvaṃ vai prajāsviha pariśrutam।  
sa upayeme dharmmātmā śantanu rjāhnavīṃ nṛpaḥ ।। 37.235 ।।  
tasyāṃ devavrataṃ bhīṣmaṃ putraṃ so'janayatprabhuḥ ।  
sa ca bhīṣma iti khyātaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। 37.236 ।।  
kāle vicitravīryantu śantanu rjanayatsutam।  
śantanordayitaṃ putraṃ prajāhitakaramprabhum।  
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaścaiva kṣetre vaicitravīryake ।। 37.237 ।।  
dhṛtarāṣṭrañca pāṇḍuñca vidurañcāpyajījanat।  
dhṛtarāṣṭrāttu gāndhārī putrāṇāṃ suṣuve śatam ।। 37.238 ।।  
teṣāṃ duryodhano jyeṣṭhaḥ sarvvakṣatrasya sa prabhuḥ।  
mādrī rājñī pṛthā caiva pāṇḍorbhārye babhūvatuḥ ।। 37.239 ।।  
devadattāḥ sutāstābhyāṃ pāṇḍorarthe vijajñire।  
dharmmādyudhiṣṭiro jajñe vāyorjajñe vṛkodaraḥ ।। 37.240 ।।  
indrāddhanañjayo jajñe śakratulyaparākramaḥ।  
aśvibhyāṃ saha devaśca nakulaścāpi mādrijau ।। 37.241 ।।  
pañcaiva pāṇḍavebhyaśca draupadyāṃ jajñire sutāḥ।  
draupadyajanayajjyeṣṭhaṃ śrutividdhaṃ yudhiṣṭirāt ।। 37.242 ।।  
hiḍambā bhīmasenāttu jajñe putraṃ ghaṭotkacam।  
kāśyāḥ punarbhīmasenājjajñe sarvvavṛkaṃ sutam ।। 37.243 ।।  
suhotraṃ vijayā mādrī sahadevādajāyata।  
karematyāntu vaidyāyāṃ niramitrastu lāṅgaliḥ ।। 37.244 ।।  
subhadrāyāṃ rathī pārthādabhimanyurajāyata।  
uttarāyāntu vairāṭyāṃ parikṣidabhimanyujaḥ ।। 37.245 ।।  
parikṣitastu dāyādo rājāsījjanamejayaḥ।  
brāhmaṇān sthāpayāmāsa sa vai vājasaneyikān ।। 37.246 ।।  
asapatnaṃ tadāmarṣādvaiśampāyana eva tu।  
na sthāsyatīha durbuddhe tavaitadvacanaṃ bhuvi ।। 37.247 ।।  
yāvatsthā syāmyahaṃ loke tāvannaitatpraśasyate।  
abhitaḥ saṃsthitaścāpi tataḥ sa janamejayaḥ ।। 37.248 ।।  
paurṇamāsyena haviṣā devamiṣṭvā prajāpatim।  
vijñāya saṃsthito'paśyattadvadhīṣṭāṃ vibhormakhe ।। 37.249 ।।  
parikṣittanayaśvāpi pauravo janamejayaḥ ।  
dviraśvamedhamāhṛtya tato vājasaneyakam ।  
pravarttayitvā tadbrahma trikharvvī janamejayaḥ ।। 37.250 ।।  
kharvvamaśvakamukhyānāṃ kharvvamaṅganivāsinām।  
sarvvañca madhyadeśānāṃ trikharvvī janamejayaḥ ।  
viṣādādbrāhmaṇaiḥ sārddhamabhiśastaḥ kṣayaṃ yayau ।। 37.251 ।।  
tasya putraḥ śatanīko balavān satyavikramaḥ ।  
tataḥ sutaṃ śatānīkaṃ viprāstamabhyaṣecayat ।। 37.252 ।।  
putro'śvamedha datto'bhūcchatānīkasya vīryyavān।  
putro'śvamedhadattādvai jātaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ ।। 37.253 ।।  
adhisāmakṛṣṇo dharmātmā sāmprato'yaṃ mahāyaśāḥ।  
yasmin praśāsati mahīṃ yuṣmābhiridamāhṛtam ।। 37.254 ।।  
durāpaṃ dīrghasatraṃ vai trīṇi varṣāṇi duścaram।  
varṣadvayaṃ kurukṣetre dṛṣadvatyāṃ dvijottamāḥ ।। 37.255 ।।  
           ṛṣaya ūcuḥ ।।  
śrotuṃ bhaviṣyamicchāmaḥ prajānāṃ vai mahāmate ।  
sūta sārddhaṃ nṛpairbhāvyaṃ vyatītaṃ kīrttitaṃ tvayā ।। 37.256 ।।  
yattu saṃsthāsyate kṛtyamutpatsyanti ce ye nṛpāḥ।  
varṣāgrato'pi prabrūhi nāmataścaiva tānnṛpān ।। 37.257 ।।  
kālaṃ yugapramāṇañca guṇadoṣān bhaviṣyataḥ।  
sukhaduḥkhe prajānāñca dharmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ ।। 37.258 ।।  
etatsarvaṃ prasaṅkhyāya pṛcchatāṃ brūhi tatvataḥ।  
sa evamukto munibhiḥ sūto buddhimatāṃ varaḥ।  
ācacakṣe yathāvṛttaṃ yathādṛṣṭaṃ yathāśrutam ।। 37.259 ।।  
          ।।sūta uvāca।।  
yathā me kīrttitaṃ sarvaṃ vyāsenādbhutakarmmaṇā।  
bhāvyaṃ kaliyugañcaiva tathā manvantarāṇi tu ।। 37.260 ।।  
anāgatāni sarvāṇi bruvato me nibodhata।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhaviṣyanti vṛpāstu ye ।। 37.261 ।।  
ailāṃścaiva tathekṣvākūn saudyumnāṃścaiva pārthivān।  
yeṣu saṃsthāpyate kṣetraṇaikṣvākavamidaṃ śubham ।। 37.262 ।।  
tān sarvān kīrttayiṣyāmi bhaviṣye paṭitānnṛpān।  
tebhyaḥ pare ca ye cānye utpatsyante mahīkṣitaḥ ।। 37.263 ।।  
kṣatrāḥ pāraśavāḥ śūdrāstathā ye ca dvijātayaḥ।  
andhāḥ śakāḥ pulindāśca tūlikā yavanaiḥ saha ।। 37.264 ।।  
kaivarttābhīraśabarā ye cānye mlecchajātayaḥ।  
varṣāgrataḥ pravakṣyāmi nāmataścaiva tānnṛpān ।। 37.265 ।।  
adhisāmakṛṣṇaḥ so'yaṃ sāmprataṃ pauravānnṛpaḥ।  
tasyānvavāye vakṣyāmi bhaviṣye tāvato nṛpān ।। 37.266 ।।  
adhisāmakṛṣṇaputro nirvakre bhavitā kila।  
gaṅgayāpahṛte tasminnagare nāgasāhvaye।  
tyaktvā ca taṃ suvāsañca kauśāmbyāṃ sa nivatsyati ।। 37.267 ।।  
bhaviṣyaduṣṇastatputra uṣṇāccitrarathaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
śucidrathaścitrarathād‌vṛtimāṃśca śucidrathāt ।। 37.268 ।।  
suṣeṇo vai mahāvīryo bhaviṣyati mahāyaśāḥ।  
tasmātsuṣeṇādbhavitā sutīrtho nāma pārthivaḥ ।। 37.269 ।।  
rucaḥ sutīrthādbhavitā tricakṣo bhavitā tataḥ।  
tricakṣasya tu dāyādo bhavitā vai sukhībalaḥ ।। 37.270 ।।  
sukhībalasutaścāpi bhāvyo rājā pariplutaḥ।  
pariplutasutaścāpi bhavitā sunayo nṛpaḥ ।। 37.271 ।।  
medhāvī sunayasyātha bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ।  
medhāvinaḥ sutaścāpi daṇḍapāṇirbhaviṣyati ।। 37.272 ।।  
daṇḍapāṇernirāmitre nirāmitrācca kṣemakaḥ।  
pañcaviṃśanṛpā hyete bhaviṣyāḥ pūrvavaṃśajāḥ ।। 37.273 ।।  
atrānuvaṃśaśloko'yaṃ gīto vipraiḥ purāvidaiḥ।  
brahmakṣatrasya yo yonirvaṃśo devarṣisatkṛtaḥ ।। 37.274 ।।  
kṣemakaṃ prāpya rājānaṃ saṃsthāṃ prāpsyati vai kalau।  
ityeṣa pauravo vaṃśo yathāvadanukīrttitaḥ ।। 37.275 ।।  
dhīmataḥ pāṇḍuputrasya hyarjunasya mahātmanaḥ।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ikṣvākūṇāṃ mahātmanām ।। 37.276 ।।  
bṛhadrathasya dāyādo vīro rājā bṛhatkṣayaḥ ।  
tataḥ kṣayaḥ sutastasya vatsavyūhastataḥ kṣayāt ।। 37.277 ।।  
vatsavyūhātprativyūhastasya putro divākaraḥ।  
yaśca sāṃpratamadhyāsta ayodhyāṃ nagarīṃ nṛpaḥ ।। 37.278 ।।  
divākarasya bhavitā sahadevo mahāyaśāḥ।  
sahadevasya dāyādo bṛhadaśvo bhaviṣyati ।। 37.279 ।।  
tasya bhānuratho bhāvyaḥ pratītāśvaśca tatsutaḥ।  
pratītāśvasutaścāpi supratīto bhaviṣyati ।। 37.280 ।।  
sahadevaḥ sutastasya sunakṣatraśca tatsutaḥ ।। 37.281 ।।  
kinnarastu sunakṣatrādbhaviṣyati paraṃtapaḥ।  
bhavitā cāntarikṣastu kinnarasya suto mahān ।। 37.282 ।।  
antarikṣātsuparṇastu suparṇāccāpyamitrajit।  
putrastasya bharadvājo dharmī tasya sutaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
putraḥ kṛtañjayo nāma dharmiṇaḥ sa bhaviṣyati।  
kṛtañjayasuto vrāto tasya putro raṇañjayaḥ ।। 37.283 ।।  
bhavitā sañjayaścāpi vīro rājā raṇañjayāt।  
sañjayasya sutaḥ śākyaḥ śākyācchuddhodano'bhavat ।। 37.284 ।।  
śuddhodanasya bhavitā śākyārthe rāhulaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
prasenajittato bhāvyaḥ kṣudrako bhavitā tataḥ ।। 37.285 ।।  
kṣudrakātkṣuliko bhāvyaḥ kṣulikātsurathaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
sumitraḥ surathasyāpi antyaśca bhavitā nṛpaḥ ।। 37.286 ।।  
ete aikṣvākavāḥ proktā bhavitāraḥ kalau yuge।  
bṛhadbalānvaye jātā bhavitāraḥ kalau yuge।  
śūrāśca kṛtavidyāśca satyasandhā jitendriyāḥ ।। 37.287 ।।  
atrānuvaṃśaśloko'yaṃ bhaviṣyajñairudāhṛtaḥ।  
ikṣvākūṇāmayaṃ vaṃśaḥ sumitrānto bhaviṣyati।  
sumitraṃ prāpya rājānaṃ saṃsthāṃ prāpsyati vai kalau।  
ityetanmānavaṃ kṣetramailañca samudāhṛtam ।। 37.288 ।।  
ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi māgadheyānbṛhadrathān।  
jarāsandhasya ye vaṃśe sahadevānvaye nṛpāḥ ।। 37.289 ।।  
atītā varttamānāśca bhaviṣyāśca tathā punaḥ।  
prādhānyataḥ pravakṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata ।। 37.290 ।।  
saṃgrāme bhārate tasmin sahadevo nipātitaḥ।  
somādhistasya tanayo rājarṣiḥ sagirivraje ।। 37.291 ।।  
pañcāśataṃ tathāṣṭau ca samā rājyamakārayat।  
śrutaśravāḥ catuḥṣaṣṭisamāstasya suto'bhavat।  
ayutāyustu ṣaḍviṃśaṃ rājyaṃ varṣāṇyakārayat।  
samāḥ śataṃ nirāmitro mahīṃ bhuktvā divaṅgataḥ ।। 37.292 ।।  
pañcāśataṃ samāḥ ṣaṭ ca sukṛttaḥ prāptavānmahīm।  
trayoviṃśaṃ bṛhatkarmā rājyaṃ varṣāṇyakārayat ।। 37.293 ।।  
senājitsāmprataṃ cāpi etāṃ vai bhujyate samāḥ।  
śrutañjayastu varṣāṇi catvāriṃśadbhaviṣyati ।। 37.294 ।।  
mahābāhurmahābuddhirmahābhīmaparākramaḥ।  
pañcatriṃśattu varṣāṇi mahīṃ pālayitā nṛpaḥ ।। 37.295 ।।  
aṣṭapañcā śataṃ cābdān rājye sthāsyati vai śuciḥ।  
aṣṭāviṃśatsamāḥ pūrṇāḥ kṣemo rājā bhaviṣyati ।। 37.296 ।।  
bhuvatastu catuḥṣaṣṭīrājyaṃ prāpsyati vīryyavān।  
pañcavarṣāṇi pūrṇāni dharmanetro bhaviṣyati ।। 37.297 ।।  
bhokṣyate nṛpatiścaiva hyaṣṭapañcāśataṃ samāḥ।  
aṣṭātriṃśatsamā rājyaṃ suvratasya bhaviṣyati ।। 37.298 ।।  
catvāriṃśaddaśāṣṭau ca dṛḍhaseno bhaviṣyati।  
trayastriṃśattu varṣāṇi sumatiḥ prāpsyate tataḥ ।। 37.299 ।।  
dvāviṃśatisamā rājyaṃ sucalo bhokṣyate tataḥ।  
catvāriṃśatsamā rājā sunetro bhokṣyate tataḥ ।। 37.300 ।।  
satyajitpṛthivīrājyaṃ tryaśītiṃ bhokṣyate samāḥ।  
prāpyemāṃ vīrajiccāpi pañcatriṃśadbhaviṣyati ।। 37.301 ।।  
arīñjayastu varṣāṇi pañcāśatprāpsyate mahīm।  
dvātriṃśacca nṛpā hyete bhavitāro bṛhadrathāḥ ।। 37.302 ।।  
pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ vai teṣāṃ rājyaṃ bhaviṣyati।  
bṛhadratheṣvatīteṣu vītahotreṣu vartiṣu ।। 37.303 ।।  
munikaḥ svāminaṃ hatvā putraṃ samabhiṣekṣyati।  
miṣatāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ hi pradyoto muniko balāt ।। 37.304 ।।  
sa vai praṇatasāmanto bhaviṣye nayavarjjitaḥ ।  
trayoviṃśatsamā rājā bhavitā sa narottamaḥ ।। 37.305 ।।  
caturviṃśatsamā rājā pālako bhavitā tataḥ।  
viśākhayūpo bhavitā nṛpaḥ pañcāśatīṃ samāḥ ।। 37.306 ।।  
ekatriṃśatsamā rājyamajakasya bhaviṣyati।  
bhaviṣyati samā viṃśattatsuto varttivarddhanaḥ ।। 37.307 ।।  
aṣṭātriṃśacchataṃ bhāvyāḥ prādyotāḥ pañca te sutāḥ।  
hatvā teṣāṃ yaśaḥ kṛtsnaṃ śiśunāko bhaviṣyati ।। 37.308 ।।  
vārāṇasyāṃ sutastasya saṃprāpsyati girivrajam।  
śiśunākasya varṣāṇi catvāriṃśadbhaviṣyati ।। 37.309 ।।  
śakavarṇaḥ sutastasya ṣaṭ‌triṃśacca bhaviṣyati।  
tatastu viṃśatiṃ rājā kṣemavarmā bhaviṣyati ।। 37.310 ।।  
ajātaśatrūrbhavitā pañcaviṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ।  
catvāriṃśatsamā rājyaṃ kṣatraujāḥ prāpsyate tataḥ ।। 37.311 ।।  
aṣṭāviṃśatsamā rājā vivisāro bhaviṣyati।  
pañcaviṃśatsamā rājā darśakastu bhaviṣyati ।। 37.312 ।।  
udāyī bhavitā tasmāttrayastriṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ।  
sa vai puravaraṃ rājā pṛthivyāṃ kusumāhvayam।  
gaṅgāyā dakṣiṇe kūle caturthe'bde kariṣyati ।। 37.313 ।।  
dvācatvāriṃśatsamā bhāvyo rājā vai nandivarddhanaḥ।  
catvāriṃśattrayañcaiva mahā nandī bhaviṣyati ।। 37.314 ।।  
ityete bhavitārau vai śaiśunākā nṛpā daśa।  
atāni trīṇi varṣāṇi dviṣaṣṭyabhyadhikāni tu ।। 37.315 ।।  
śaiśunākā bhaviṣyanti tāvatkālaṃ nṛpāḥ pare।  
etaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhaviṣyaṃti rājānaḥ kṣatrabāndhavāḥ ।। 37.316 ।।  
aikṣvākavāścaturviṃśatpāñcālāḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ।  
kālakāstu caturvviṃśaccaturvviṃśattu haihayāḥ ।। 37.317 ।।  
dvātriṃśadvai kaliṅgāstu pañcaviṃśattathā śakāḥ।  
kuravaścāpi ṣaḍviṃśadaṣṭāviṃśati maithilāḥ ।। 37.318 ।।  
śūrase nāstrayoviṃśadvītihotrāśca viṃśatiḥ।  
tulyakālaṃ bhaviṣyanti sarva eva mahīkṣitaḥ ।। 37.319 ।।  
mahānandisutaścāpi śūdrāyāṃ kālasaṃvṛtaḥ।  
utpatsyate mahāpadmaḥ sarvakṣatrāntare nṛpaḥ ।। 37.320 ।।  
tataḥprabhṛti rājāno bhaviṣyāḥ śūdrayonayaḥ।  
ekarāṭ sa mahāpadma ekacchatro bhaviṣyati ।। 37.321 ।।  
aṣṭā viṃśativarṣāṇi pṛthivīṃ pālayiṣyati।  
sarvakṣatrahṛtoddhṛtya bhāvino'rthasya vai balāt ।। 37.322 ।।  
sahasrāstatsutā hyaṣṭau samā dvādaśa te nṛpāḥ।।  
mahāpadmasya paryāye bhaviṣyanti nṛpāḥ kramāt ।। 37.323 ।।  
uddhariṣyati tān sarvān kauṭilyo vai dviraṣṭabhiḥ।  
bhuktvā mahīṃ varṣaśataṃ nandenduḥ sa bhaviṣyati ।। 37.324 ।।  
candraguptaṃ nṛpaṃ rājye kauṭilyaḥ sthāpayiṣyati।  
caturviṃśatsamā rājā candragupto bhaviṣyati ।। 37.325 ।।  
bhavitā bhadra sārastu pañcaviṃśatsamā nṛpaḥ।  
ṣaḍviṃśattu samā rājā hyaśoko bhavitā nṛṣu ।। 37.326 ।।  
tasya putraḥ kunālastu varṣāṇyaṣṭau bhaviṣyati।  
kunāla sūnuraṣṭau ca bhoktā vai bandhupālitaḥ ।। 37.327 ।।  
bandhupālitadāyādo daśamānīndrapālitaḥ।  
bhavitā saptavarṣāṇi devavarmmā narādhipaḥ ।। 37.328 ।।  
rājā śatadharaścāṣṭau tasya putro bhaviṣyati।  
bṛhadaśvaśca varṣāṇi sapta vai bhavitā nṛpaḥ ।। 37.329 ।।  
ityete nava bhūpā ye bhokṣyanti ca vasundharām।  
saptatriṃśacchataṃ pūrṇaṃ tebhyastu gaurbhaviṣyati ।। 37.330 ।।  
puṣpamitrastu senānīruddhṛtya vai bṛhadratham।  
kārayiṣyati vai rājyaṃ samāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ sadaiva tu ।। 37.331 ।।  
puṣpamitrasutāścāṣṭau bhaviṣyanti samā nṛpāḥ।  
bhavitā cāpi tajjyeṣṭhaḥ saptavarṣāṇi vai tataḥ ।। 37.332 ।।  
vasumitraḥ suto bhāvyo daśavarṣāṇi pārthivaḥ।  
tato dhrukaḥ samā dve tu bhaviṣyati sutaśca vai ।। 37.333 ।।  
bhaviṣyanti samāstasmāttisra eva pulindakāḥ।  
rājā ghoṣasutaścāpi varṣāṇi bhavitā trayaḥ ।। 37.334 ।।  
tato vai vikramitrastu samā rājā tataḥ punaḥ।  
dvātriṃśadbhavitā cāpi samā bhāgavato nṛpaḥ ।। 37.335 ।।  
bhaviṣyati sutastasya kṣemabhūmiḥ samā daśa।  
daśaite tuṅgarājāno bhokṣyantīmāṃ vasundharam ।। 37.336 ।।  
śataṃ pūrṇaṃ daśa dve ca tebhyaḥ kiṃ vā gamiṣyati।  
apārthivasudevantu bālyādvyasaninaṃ nṛpam ।। 37.337 ।।  
devabhūmistato'nyaśca śrṛṅgeṣu bhavitā nṛpaḥ।  
bhaviṣyati samā rājā nava kaṇṭāyanastu saḥ ।। 37.338 ।।  
bhūtimitraḥ sutastasya caturvviṃśadbhaviṣyati।  
bhavitā dvādaśa samāstasmānnārāyaṇo nṛpaḥ ।। 37.339 ।।  
suśarmmā tatsutaścāpi bhaviṣyati samā daśa।  
caturastuṅgakṛtyāste nṛpāḥ kaṇṭāyanā dvijāḥ ।। 37.340 ।।  
bhāvyāḥ praṇatasāmantāścatvāriṃśacca pañca ca।  
teṣāṃ paryyāyakāle tu tarandhā tu bhaviṣyati ।। 37.341 ।।  
kaṇṭāyanamathoddhṛtya suśarmmāṇaṃ prasahya tam।  
śrṛṅgāṇāṃ cāpi yacchiṣṭaṃ kṣayayitvā balaṃ tadā।  
sindhuko hyandhrajātīyaḥ prāpsyatīmāṃ vasundharām ।। 37.342 ।।  
trayoviṃśatsamā rājā sindhuko bhavitā tvatha।  
aṣṭau bhātaśca varṣāṇi tasmāddaśa bhaviṣyati ।। 37.343 ।।  
śrīsātakarṇirbhavitā tasya putrastu vai mahān।  
pañcāśataṃ samāḥ ṣaṭ ca sātakarṇirbhaviṣyati ।। 37.344 ।।  
āpādabaddho daśa vai tasya putro bhaviṣyati।  
caturvviṃśattu varṣāṇi ṣaṭ samā vai bhaviṣyati ।। 37.345 ।।  
bhavitā nemikṛṣṇastu varṣāṇāṃ pañcaviṃśatim।  
tataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ hālo rājā bhaviṣyati ।। 37.346 ।।  
pañca saptaka rājāno bhaviṣyanti mahābalāḥ।  
bhāvyaḥ putrikaṣeṇastu samāḥ so'pyekaviṃśatim ।। 37.347 ।।  
sātakarṇirvarṣamekaṃ bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ।  
aṣṭāviṃśattu varṣāṇi śivasvāmī bhaviṣyati ।। 37.348 ।।  
rājā ca gautamīputra ekaviṃśatsamā nṛṣu।  
ekonaviṃśatiṃ rājā yajñaśrīḥ sātakarṇyatha ।। 37.349 ।।  
ṣaḍeva bhavitā tasmādvijayastu samā nṛpaḥ।  
daṇḍaśrīḥ sātakarṇī ca tasya putraḥ samāstrayaḥ ।। 37.350 ।।  
pulovāpi samāḥ sapta anyeṣāñca bhaviṣyati ।  
ityete vai nṛpāstriṃśadandhrā bhokṣyanti ye mahīm ।। 37.351 ।।  
samāḥ śatāni catvāri pañca ṣaḍvai tathaiva ca।  
andhrāṇāṃ saṃsthitāḥ pañca teṣāṃ vaṃśāḥ samāḥ punaḥ ।। 37.352 ।।  
saptaiva tu bhaviṣyanti daśābhīrāstato nṛpāḥ।  
sapta gardabhinaścāpi tato'tha daśa vai śakāḥ ।। 37.353 ।।  
yavanāṣṭau bhaviṣyanti tuṣārāstu caturdaśa।  
trayodaśa maruṇḍāśca maunā hyaṣṭādaśaiva tu ।। 37.354 ।।  
andhrā bhokṣyanti vasudhāṃ śate dve ca śataṃ ca vai।  
śatāni trīṇyaśītiñca bhokṣyanti vasudhāṃ śakāḥ ।। 37.355 ।।  
aśītiñcaiva varṣāṇi bhoktāro yavanā mahīm।  
pañcavarṣaśatānīha tuṣārāṇāṃ mahī smṛtā ।। 37.356 ।।  
śatānyarddhacaturthāni bhavitārastrayodaśa।  
maruṇḍā vṛṣalaiḥ sārddhaṃ bhāvyānyā mlecchajātayaḥ ।। 37.357 ।।  
śatāni trīṇi bhokṣyanti mlecchā ekādaśaiva tu।  
tacchannena ca kālena tataḥ kolikilā vṛṣāḥ ।। 37.358 ।।  
tataḥ kolikilebhyaśca vindhyaśaktirbhaviṣyati।  
samāḥ ṣaṇṇavatiṃ trātvā pṛthivīṃ ca sameṣyati ।। 37.359 ।।  
vṛṣān vai diśakāṃścāpi bhaviṣyāśca nibodhata।  
śeṣasya nāgarājasya putraḥ svarapurañjayaḥ ।। 37.360 ।।  
bhogī bhaviṣyate rājā nṛpo nāgakulodvahaḥ।  
sadācandrastu candrāṃśo dvitīyo nakhavāṃstathā ।। 37.361 ।।  
dhanadharmā tataścāpi caturtho viṃśajaḥ smṛtaḥ।  
bhūtinandastataścāpi vaideśe tu bhaviṣyati ।। 37.362 ।।  
aṅgānāṃ nandanasyānte madhunandirbhaviṣyati।  
tasya bhrātā yavīyāṃstu nāmnā nandiyaśāḥ kila ।। 37.363 ।।  
tasyānvaye bhaviṣyanti rājānaste trayastu vai।  
dohitraḥ śiśuko nāma purikāyāṃ nṛpo'bhavat ।। 37.364 ।।  
vindhyaśaktisutaścāpi pravīro nāma vīryavān ।  
bhokṣyanti ca samāḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ purīṃ kāñcanakāñca vai ।। 37.365 ।।  
yakṣyanti vājapeyaiśca samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ।  
tasya putrāstu catvāro bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ ।। 37.366 ।।  
vindhyakānāṃ kule'tīte nṛpā vai bāhlikā strayaḥ।  
supratīko nabhīrastu samā bhokṣyati triṃśatim ।। 37.367 ।।  
śakyamā nāma vai rājā māhiṣīnāṃ mahīpatiḥ।  
puṣpamitrā bhaviṣyanti paṭṭamitrāstrayodaśa ।। 37.368 ।।  
mekalāyāṃ nṛpāḥ sapta bhaviṣyanti ca sattamāḥ।  
komalāyāntu rājāno bhaviṣyanti mahābalāḥ ।। 37.369 ।।  
meghā iti samākhyātā buddhimanto navaiva tu।  
naiṣadhāḥ pārthivāḥ sarvve bhaviṣyantyāmanukṣayāt ।। 37.370 ।।  
nalavaṃśaprasūtāste vīryavanto mahābalāḥ।  
māgadhānāṃ mahāvīryo viśvasphānirbhaviṣyati ।। 37.371 ।।  
utsādya pārthivān sarvvānso'nyān varṇān kariṣyati।  
kaivarttān pañcakāṃścaiva pulindān brāhmaṇāṃstathā ।। 37.372 ।।  
sthāpayiṣyanti rājāno nānādeśeṣu tejasā।  
viśvasphānirmahāsattvo yuddhe viṣṇusamo balī ।। 37.373 ।।  
viśvasphānirnarapatiḥ klībā kṛtirivocyate।  
utsādayitvā kṣatrantu kṣatramanyat kariṣyati ।। 37.374 ।।  
devān pitṝṃśca viprāṃśca tarpayitvā sakṛtpunaḥ।  
jāhnavītīramāsādya śarīraṃ yasyate balī ।। 37.375 ।।  
saṃnyasya svaśarīrantu śakralokaṃ gamiṣyati।  
navanākāstu bhokṣyanti purīṃ campāvatīṃ nṛpāḥ ।। 37.376 ।।  
mathurāñca purīṃ ramyāṃ nāgā bhokṣyanti sapta vai।  
anugaṅgaṃ prayāgañca sāketaṃ magadhāṃstathā।  
etāñjanapadān sarvvān bhokṣyante guptavaṃśajāḥ ।। 37.377 ।।  
niṣadhān yadukāṃścaiva śaiśī tān kālatopakān।  
etāñjanapadān sarvvān bhokṣyanti maṇidhānyajāḥ ।। 37.378 ।।  
kośalāṃścāndhrapauṇḍrāṃśca tāmraliptān sasāgarān।  
campāṃ caiva purīṃ ramyāṃ bhokṣyanti devarakṣitām ।। 37.379 ।।  
kāliṅgā mahiṣāścaiva mahendranilayāśca ye।  
etāñjanapadān sarvvān pālayiṣyati vai guhaḥ ।। 37.380 ।।  
strīrāṣṭraṃ bhakṣyakāṃścaiva bhokṣyate kanakāhvayaḥ।  
tulyakālaṃ bhaviṣyanti sarve hyete mahīkṣitaḥ ।। 37.381 ।।  
alpaprasādā hyanṛtā mahākrodhāḥ hyadhārmikāḥ।  
bhaviṣyantīha yavanā dharmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ ।। 37.382 ।।  
naiva mūrddhābhiṣiktāste bhaviṣyanti narādhipāḥ।  
yugadoṣadurācārā bhaviṣyanti nṛpāstu te ।। 37.383 ।।  
strīṇāṃ balavadhenaiva hatvā caiva parasparam।  
bhokṣyanti kaliśeṣe tu vasudhāṃ pārthivāstathā ।। 37.384 ।।  
uditoditavaṃśāste uditāstamitāstathā ।  
bhaviṣyantīha paryāye kālena pṛthivīkṣitaḥ ।। 37.385 ।।  
vihīnāstu bhaviṣyanti dharmmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ।  
tairvimiśrā janapadā mlecchācārāśca sarvaśaḥ ।। 37.386 ।।  
viparyyayena varttante nāśayiṣyanti vai prajāḥ।  
lubdhānṛtaratāścaiva bhavitārastadā nṛpāḥ ।। 37.387 ।।  
teṣāṃ vyatīte paryāye bahustrīke yuge tadā।  
lavāllavaṃ bhraśyamānā āyūrūpabalaśrutaiḥ ।। 37.388 ।।  
tathā gatāstu vai kāṣṭāṃ prajāsu jagatīśvarāḥ ।  
rājānaḥ sampraṇaśyanti kālenopahatāstadā ।। 37.389 ।।  
kalkinopahatāḥ sarve mlecchā yāsyanti sarvaśaḥ।  
adhārmikāśca te'tyarthaṃ pāṣaṇḍāścaiva sarvaśaḥ ।। 37.390 ।।  
pranaṣṭe nṛpaśabde ca sandhyāśliṣṭe kalau yuge।  
kiṃñcicchiṣṭāḥ prajāstā vai dharmme naṣṭe'parigrahāḥ ।। 37.391 ।।  
asādhanā hatāśvāsā vyādhiśokena pīḍitāḥ।  
anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva parasparavadhena ca ।। 37.392 ।।  
anāthā hi paritrastā vārttāmutsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ।  
tyaktvā purāṇi grāmāṃśca bhaviṣyanti vanaukasaḥ ।। 37.393 ।।  
evaṃ nṛpeṣu naṣṭeṣu prajāstyaktvā gṛhāṇi tu।  
naṣṭe snehe durāpannā bhraṣṭasnehāḥ suhṛjjanāḥ ।। 37.394 ।।  
varṇāśramaparibhraṣṭāḥ saṅkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ।  
saritparvatasevinyo bhaviṣyanti prajāstadā ।। 37.395 ।।  
saritaḥ sāgarānūpān sevante parvatāni ca।  
aṅgān kaliṅgān vaṅgāṃśca kāśmīrān kāśikośalān ।। 37.396 ।।  
ṛṣikāntagiridroṇīḥ saṃśrayiṣyanti mānavāḥ।  
kṛtsnaṃ himavataḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ kūlaṃ ca lavaṇāmbhasaḥ ।। 37.397 ।।  
araṇyānyabhipatsyanti hyāryyā mlecchajanaiḥ saha।  
mṛgairmīnairvihaṅgaiśca śvāpadaistakṣubhistathā।  
madhuśākaphalairmūlairvarttayiṣyanti mānavāḥ ।। 37.398 ।।  
cīraṃ parṇañca vividhaṃ valkalānyajināni ca।  
svayaṃ kṛtvā vivatsyanti yathā munijanāstathā ।। 37.399 ।।  
bījānnāni tathā nimnesvīhantaḥ kāṣṭhaśaṅkubhiḥ।  
ajaiḍakaṃ kharoṣṭrañca pālayiṣyanti yatnataḥ ।। 37.400 ।।  
nadīrvatsyanti toyārthe kūlamāśritya mānavāḥ।  
pārthivān vyavahāreṇa vibādhantaḥ parasparam ।। 37.401 ।।  
bahumanyāḥ prajāhīnāḥ śaucācāravivarjitāḥ।  
evaṃ bhaviṣyanti narāstadādharmme vyavasthitāḥ ।। 37.402 ।।  
hīnāddhīnāṃstathā dharmmān prajāḥ samanuvarttate।  
āyustadā trayoviṃśaṃ na kaścidativarttate ।। 37.403 ।।  
durbalā viṣayaglānā jarayā saṃpariplutāḥ।  
patramūlaphalāhārāścīrakṛṣṇājināmbarāḥ ।। 37.404 ।।  
vṛttyarthamabhilipsantaścariṣyanti vasundharām।  
etatkālamanuprāptāḥ prajāḥ kaliyugāntake ।। 37.405 ।।  
kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmin divye varṣasahasrake।  
niḥśeṣāstu bhaviṣyanti sārddhaṃ kaliyugena tu।  
sasandhyāṃśe tu niḥśeṣe kṛtaṃ vai pratipatsyate ।। 37.406 ।।  
yadā candraśca sūryyaśca tathā tiṣyabṛhaspatī।  
ekarātre bhariṣyanti tadā kṛtayugaṃ bhavet ।। 37.407 ।।  
eṣa vaṃśakramaḥ kṛtsnaṃ kīrtito vo yathākramam।  
atītā varttamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye ।। 37.408 ।।  
mahādevābhiṣekāttu janma yāvatparikṣitaḥ।  
etadvarṣasahasrantu jñeyaṃ pañcādaśaduttaram ।। 37.409 ।।  
pramāṇaṃ vai tathā coktaṃ mahāpadmāntaraṃ ca yat।  
antaraṃ tacchatānyaṣṭau ṣaṭ‌triṃśacca samāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 37.410 ।।  
etatkālāntaraṃ bhāvyā andhrāntā ye prakīrttitāḥ।  
bhaviṣyaistatra saṅkhyātāḥ purāṇajñaiḥ śrutarṣibhiḥ ।। 37.411 ।।  
saptarṣayastadā prāhuḥ pratīpe rājñi vai śatam।  
saptaviṃśaiḥ śatairbhāvyā andhrāṇāṃ te tvayā punaḥ ।। 37.412 ।।  
saptaviṃśatiparyyante kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale।  
saptarṣayastu tiṣṭhanti paryāyeṇa śataṃ śatam।  
saptarṣīṇāṃ yugaṃ hyetaddivyayā saṅkhyayā smṛtam ।। 37.413 ।।  
sā sā divyā smṛtā ṣaṣṭirdivyāhnāścaiva saptabhiḥ ।  
tebhyaḥ pravarttate kālo divyaḥ saptarṣibhistu taiḥ ।। 37.414 ।।  
saptarṣīṇāntu ye pūrvā dṛśyante uttarādiśi।  
tato madhyena ca kṣetraṃ dṛśyate yatsamaṃ divi ।। 37.415 ।।  
tena saptarṣayo yuktā jñeyā vyomni śataṃ samāḥ।  
nakṣatrāṇāmṛṣīṇāñca yogasyaitannidarśanam ।। 37.416 ।।  
saptarṣayo maghāyuktāḥ kāle pārikṣite śatam।  
andhrāṃśe sa caturvviśe bhaviṣyanti mate mama ।। 37.417 ।।  
imāstadā tu prakṛtirvyāpatsyanti prajā bhṛśam।  
anṛtopahatāḥ sarvā dharmataḥ kāmato'rthataḥ ।। 37.418 ।।  
śrautasmārtte praśithile dharme varṇāśrame tadā।  
śaṅkaraṃ durbalātmānaḥ pratipatsyanti mohitāḥ ।। 37.419 ।।  
saṃsaktāśca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāḥ sārddhaṃ dvijātibhiḥ।  
brāhmaṇāḥ śūdrayaṣṭāraḥ śūdrā vai mantrayonayaḥ ।। 37.420 ।।  
upasthāsyanti tān viprāstadā vai vṛttilipsavaḥ ।  
lavaṃ lavaṃ bhrasyamānāḥ prajāḥ sarvāḥ krameṇa tu ।। 37.421 ।।  
kṣayameva gamiṣyanti kṣīṇaśeṣā yugakṣaye।  
yasmin kṛṣṇo divaṃ yātastasminneva tadā dine ।। 37.422 ।।  
pratipannaḥ kaliyugastasya saṅkhyāṃ nibodhata।  
sahasrāṇāṃ śatānīha trīṇi mānuṣasaṅkhyayā।  
ṣaṣṭiṃ caiva sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāmucyate kaliḥ ।। 37.423 ।।  
divye varṣasahasrantu tatsandhyāṃśaṃ prakīrttitam।  
niḥśeṣe ca tadā tasmin kṛtaṃ vai pratipatsyate ।। 37.424 ।।  
aila ikṣvākuvaṃśaśca saha bhedaiḥ prakīrttitau।  
ikṣvākostu smṛtaḥ kṣatraḥ sumitrāntaṃ vivasvataḥ ।। 37.425 ।।  
ailaṃ kṣatraṃ kṣemakāntaṃ somavaṃśavido viduḥ।  
ete vivasvataḥ putrāḥ kīrttitāḥ kīrttivarddhanāḥ ।। 37.426 ।।  
atītā varttamānāśca tathaivānāgatāśca ye।  
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścaivānvaye smṛtāḥ ।। 37.427 ।।  
yuge yuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥ sahasraśaḥ।  
bahutvānnāmadheyānāṃ parisaṃkhyā kule kule ।। 37.428 ।।  
punaruktā bahutvācca na mayā parikīrttitā।  
vaivasvate'ntare hyasmin nimivaṃśaḥ samāpyate ।। 37.429 ।।  
evāyāntu yugākhyāyāṃ yataḥ kṣatraṃ prapatsyate ।  
tathā hi kathayiṣyāmi gadato me nibodhata ।। 37.430 ।।  
devāpiḥ pauravo rājā ikṣvākoścaiva yo mataḥ।  
mahāyogabalopetaḥ kalāpagrāmamāsthitaḥ ।। 37.431 ।।  
suvarccāḥ somaputrastu ikṣvākostu bhaviṣyati।  
etau kṣatrapraṇetārau caturviṃśe caturyuge ।। 37.432 ।।  
na ca viṃśe yuge somavaṃśasyādirbhaviṣyati।  
devāpirasapatnastu ailādirbhavitā nṛpaḥ ।। 37.433 ।।  
kṣatraprāparttakau hyetau bhaviṣyete caturyuge।  
evaṃ sarvatra vijñeyaṃ santānārthe tu lakṣaṇam ।। 37.434 ।।  
kṣīṇe kaliyuge tasmin bhaviṣye tu kṛte yuge।  
saptarṣibhistu taiḥ sārddhamādye tretāyuge punaḥ ।। 37.435 ।।  
gotrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāñca bhaviṣyete pravarttakau।  
dvāparāṃśe na tiṣṭhanti kṣatriyā ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।। 37.436 ।।  
kāle kṛtayuge caiva kṣīṇe tretāyuge punaḥ।  
bījārthante bhaviṣyanti brahmakṣatrasya vai punaḥ ।। 37.437 ।।  
evameva tu sarveṣu tiṣṭhantīhāntareṣu vai ।  
saptarṣayo nṛpaiḥ sārddhaṃ santānārthaṃ yuge yuge ।। 37.438 ।।  
kṣatrasyaiva samucchedaḥ sambandho vai dvijaiḥ smṛtaḥ।  
manvantarāṇāṃ saptānāṃ santānāśca śrutāśca te ।। 37.439 ।।  
paramparā yugānāñca brahmakṣatrasya codbhavaḥ।  
yathā pravṛttisteṣāṃ vai pravṛttānāṃ tathā kṣayaḥ ।। 37.440 ।।  
saptarṣayo vidusteṣāṃ dīrghāyuṣṭvākṣayantu te।  
etena kramayogena ailekṣvākvanvayā dvijāḥ ।। 37.441 ।।  
utpadyamānāstretāyāṃ kṣīyamāṇe kalau punaḥ।  
anuyānti yugākhyāṃ tu yāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ ।। 37.442 ।।  
jāmadagnyena rāmeṇa kṣatre niravaśeṣite।  
kṛte vaṃśakulāḥ sarvāḥ kṣatriyairvasudhādhipaiḥ।  
dvivaṃśakaraṇāścaiva kīrttayiṣye nibodhata ।। 37.443 ।।  
ailasyekṣvākunandasya prakṛtiḥ parivarttate।  
rājānaḥ śreṇibaddhāstu tathānye kṣatriyā nṛpāḥ ।। 37.444 ।।  
ailavaṃśasya ye khyātāstathaivaikṣvākavā nṛpāḥ ।  
teṣāmekaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ kulānāmabhiṣekinām ।। 37.445 ।।  
tāvadeva tu bhojānāṃ vistāro dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।  
bhajate triṃśakaṃ kṣatraṃ caturdhā tadyathādiśam ।। 37.446 ।।  
teṣvatītāḥ samānā ye bruvatastānnibodhata।  
śataṃ vai prativindhyānāṃ śataṃ nāgāḥ śataṃ hayāḥ ।। 37.447 ।।  
dhṛtarāṣṭrāścaikaśatamaśītirjanamejayāḥ।  
śatañca brahmadattānāṃ śīriṇāṃ vīriṇāṃ śatam ।। 37.448 ।।  
tataḥ śataṃ puromānāṃ śvetakāśakuśādayaḥ ।  
tato'pare sahasraṃ vai ye'tītāḥ śatabindavaḥ ।। 37.449 ।।  
ījire cāśvamedhaiste sarve niyutadakṣiṇaiḥ ।  
evaṃ rājarṣayo'tītāḥ śataśo'tha sahasraśaḥ ।। 37.450 ।।  
manorvaivasvatasyāsmin varttamāne'ntare tu ye ।  
teṣāṃ nibodhatotpannā loke santatayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। 37.451 ।।  
nu śakyaṃ vistaraṃ teṣāṃ santānānāṃ paramparā।  
tatpūrvāparayogena vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi ।। 37.452 ।।  
aṣṭāviṃśadyugākhyāstu gatā vaivasvate'ntare।  
etā rājarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ śiṣṭā yāstā nibodhata ।। 37.453 ।।  
catvāriṃśacca ye caiva bhaviṣyāḥ saha rājabhiḥ।  
yugākhyānāṃ viśiṣṭāstu tato vaivasvatakṣaye ।। 37.454 ।।  
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvvaṃ samāsavyāsayogataḥ।  
punaruktaṃ bahutvācca na śakyantu yugaiḥ saha ।। 37.455 ।।  
ete yayātiputrāṇāṃ pañcaviṃśā viśāṃ hitāḥ।  
kīrttitāścāmitā ye me lokān vai dhārayantyuta ।। 37.456 ।।  
labhate ca vareṇyañca durlabhāniha laukikān।  
āyuḥ kīrttiṃ dhanaṃ putrān svargaṃ cānantyamaśnute ।। 37.457 ।।  
dhāraṇācchravaṇāccaiva te lokān dhārayantyuta।  
ityeṣa vo mayo pādastṛtīyaḥ kathito dvijāḥ।  
vistareṇānupūrvvī ca kimbhūyo varttayāmyaham ।। 37.458 ।।  
iti śrīmahāpurāṇe vāyuprokte anuṣaṅgapādo nāma saptatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ ।। 37 ।। ityanuṣaṅgapādaḥ ।।
